# 9.2 Vision & Architecture Layer Schemas

## Insynergy Cinematic Thought Leadership Platform

### Master Specification v2.0

---

# Purpose

This chapter formalizes the structural contracts established in Part 1 of the Master Specification. It converts the prose and YAML definitions of the Vision & Architecture layer into complete, machine-checkable JSON Schema (draft 2020-12) artifacts. The contracts covered here are the external product contract (1.1.1), the layer contract (1.3.3), the system data-flow contract (1.3.2), the hybrid asset-selection map (1.3.6), and the human-approval record (1.4.1).

These objects are configuration and contract objects, not per-build content artifacts. They describe the fixed boundaries, dependency topology, routing rules, and governance guarantees within which every build shall execute. They shall be validated at platform initialization and at contract-change time, not regenerated per pipeline run.

---

# Design Philosophy

Part 1 defines the platform's fixed boundaries: what enters, what leaves, how the eight logical layers depend on one another, where the single branch and convergence points sit, and where human judgment gates the machine. These schemas make those boundaries machine-checkable. Any instance that validates against the schemas in this chapter shall be a structurally conformant statement of the Part 1 contract; any instance that fails validation shall be rejected before it can influence a build.

---

# Schemas in This Chapter

- **9.2.1 product-contract** (`product_contract`) — the external product contract (Owner: 1.1.1).
- **9.2.2 layer-contract** (`layer_contract`) — the per-layer dependency and capability contract (Owner: 1.3.3).
- **9.2.3 data-flow** (`data_flow`) — the typed adjacency graph of the pipeline (Owner: 1.3.2).
- **9.2.4 asset-selection** (`asset_selection`) — the moment-class to asset-class map (Owner: 1.3.6).
- **9.2.5 approval-record** (`approval_record`) — the two-stage human-approval record (Owner: 1.4.1).

---

# 9.2.1 Product Contract (`product_contract`)

## Insynergy Cinematic Thought Leadership Platform

### Master Specification v2.0

---

# Purpose

The product contract is the external boundary of the platform. It declares exactly what the platform accepts as input, exactly what it emits as output, the guarantees it makes about the transformation, and the responsibilities it explicitly excludes. It is owned by section 1.1.1 and is consumed by every downstream layer as the authoritative statement of scope.

The contract shall bind one and only one insight article to one and only one cinematic trailer, addressed to a CXO audience, with conceptual accuracy preserved and communication (not mere illustration) required. Authoring is upstream of the platform and publishing is downstream; both are out of scope.

---

# Canonical Schema

```json
{
  "$schema": "https://json-schema.org/draft/2020-12/schema",
  "$id": "https://schemas.insynergy.co/cttp/v2.0/vision/product-contract.schema.json",
  "title": "Product Contract",
  "description": "External product contract for the platform. Owner: 1.1.1. Binds exactly one insight article to exactly one cinematic trailer for a CXO audience, with conceptual accuracy preserved and communication required.",
  "type": "object",
  "additionalProperties": false,
  "required": ["input", "output", "guarantees", "excluded"],
  "properties": {
    "schema_version": {
      "$ref": "https://schemas.insynergy.co/cttp/v2.0/common/defs.schema.json#/$defs/SchemaVersion"
    },
    "input": {
      "type": "object",
      "description": "The single accepted input artifact. Owner: 1.1.1.",
      "additionalProperties": false,
      "required": ["type", "cardinality", "format"],
      "properties": {
        "type": {
          "type": "string",
          "const": "insight_article"
        },
        "cardinality": {
          "type": "string",
          "const": "exactly_one"
        },
        "format": {
          "type": "string",
          "const": "structured_markdown"
        }
      }
    },
    "output": {
      "type": "object",
      "description": "The single emitted output artifact. Owner: 1.1.1.",
      "additionalProperties": false,
      "required": ["type", "cardinality", "audience"],
      "properties": {
        "type": {
          "type": "string",
          "const": "cinematic_trailer"
        },
        "cardinality": {
          "type": "string",
          "const": "exactly_one"
        },
        "audience": {
          "type": "string",
          "const": "cxo"
        }
      }
    },
    "guarantees": {
      "type": "object",
      "description": "Transformation guarantees. Owner: 1.1.1.",
      "additionalProperties": false,
      "required": ["conceptual_accuracy", "communication", "illustration_only"],
      "properties": {
        "conceptual_accuracy": {
          "type": "string",
          "const": "preserved"
        },
        "communication": {
          "type": "string",
          "const": "required"
        },
        "illustration_only": {
          "type": "string",
          "const": "rejected"
        }
      }
    },
    "excluded": {
      "type": "object",
      "description": "Responsibilities explicitly out of scope. Owner: 1.1.1.",
      "additionalProperties": false,
      "required": ["authoring", "publishing"],
      "properties": {
        "authoring": {
          "type": "string",
          "const": "upstream"
        },
        "publishing": {
          "type": "string",
          "const": "downstream"
        }
      }
    }
  }
}
```

---

# Field Reference

| Field | Type | Required | Meaning | Constraint |
|---|---|---|---|---|
| `schema_version` | SchemaVersion | No | Contract schema version | Per common defs |
| `input.type` | string | Yes | Accepted input kind | const `insight_article` |
| `input.cardinality` | string | Yes | Number of inputs accepted | const `exactly_one` |
| `input.format` | string | Yes | Input encoding | const `structured_markdown` |
| `output.type` | string | Yes | Emitted output kind | const `cinematic_trailer` |
| `output.cardinality` | string | Yes | Number of outputs emitted | const `exactly_one` |
| `output.audience` | string | Yes | Intended audience | const `cxo` |
| `guarantees.conceptual_accuracy` | string | Yes | Accuracy guarantee | const `preserved` |
| `guarantees.communication` | string | Yes | Communication guarantee | const `required` |
| `guarantees.illustration_only` | string | Yes | Illustration-only disposition | const `rejected` |
| `excluded.authoring` | string | Yes | Authoring boundary | const `upstream` |
| `excluded.publishing` | string | Yes | Publishing boundary | const `downstream` |

---

# Constraints & Invariants

- **INV-9.2.1-1** (INV-1.1.1-1): The platform shall accept exactly one input article; `input.cardinality` shall equal `exactly_one`.
- **INV-9.2.1-2** (INV-1.1.1-2): The platform shall emit exactly one trailer output; `output.cardinality` shall equal `exactly_one`.
- **INV-9.2.1-3** (INV-1.1.1-3): The output shall communicate; `guarantees.communication` shall equal `required` and `guarantees.illustration_only` shall equal `rejected`.
- **INV-9.2.1-4** (INV-1.1.1-4): Conceptual accuracy shall be preserved; `guarantees.conceptual_accuracy` shall equal `preserved`.
- **INV-9.2.1-5** (INV-1.1.1-5): Authoring and publishing shall be out of scope; `excluded.authoring` shall equal `upstream` and `excluded.publishing` shall equal `downstream`.

---

# Example

```json
{
  "schema_version": "2.0.0",
  "input": {
    "type": "insight_article",
    "cardinality": "exactly_one",
    "format": "structured_markdown"
  },
  "output": {
    "type": "cinematic_trailer",
    "cardinality": "exactly_one",
    "audience": "cxo"
  },
  "guarantees": {
    "conceptual_accuracy": "preserved",
    "communication": "required",
    "illustration_only": "rejected"
  },
  "excluded": {
    "authoring": "upstream",
    "publishing": "downstream"
  }
}
```

---

# Acceptance Criteria

- An instance shall validate only if all four contract blocks (`input`, `output`, `guarantees`, `excluded`) are present.
- Any deviation from the fixed `const` values shall cause rejection.
- No additional properties shall be permitted at any level (`additionalProperties: false` throughout).
- The instance shall be treated as a platform-level configuration object, validated at initialization and on contract change.

---

# 9.2.2 Layer Contract (`layer_contract`)

## Insynergy Cinematic Thought Leadership Platform

### Master Specification v2.0

---

# Purpose

The layer contract declares the capability and dependency profile of a single logical layer within the eight-layer architecture. Each of the eight layers states what it consumes, what it produces, the single layer it depends on (the layer whose `id` is one less than its own), and whether it is permitted to be aware of external rendering providers. It is owned by section 1.3.3.

The set of eight layer contracts, taken together, constitutes the platform's dependency topology. A layer shall depend only on its immediate predecessor, and only the Rendering layer (id 5) may set `provider_aware` to `true`.

---

# Canonical Schema

```json
{
  "$schema": "https://json-schema.org/draft/2020-12/schema",
  "$id": "https://schemas.insynergy.co/cttp/v2.0/vision/layer-contract.schema.json",
  "title": "Layer Contract",
  "description": "Per-layer capability and dependency contract for one of the eight logical layers. Owner: 1.3.3. A layer depends only on layer id-1; only the Rendering layer (id 5) may be provider_aware.",
  "type": "object",
  "additionalProperties": false,
  "required": ["id", "name", "consumes", "produces", "depends_on", "provider_aware"],
  "properties": {
    "schema_version": {
      "$ref": "https://schemas.insynergy.co/cttp/v2.0/common/defs.schema.json#/$defs/SchemaVersion"
    },
    "id": {
      "type": "integer",
      "description": "Ordinal layer identifier, 1..8. Owner: 1.3.3.",
      "minimum": 1,
      "maximum": 8
    },
    "name": {
      "type": "string",
      "description": "Human-readable layer name. Owner: 1.3.3.",
      "enum": [
        "Knowledge",
        "Narrative",
        "Screenplay",
        "Direction",
        "Rendering",
        "Composition",
        "Validation",
        "Publishing"
      ]
    },
    "consumes": {
      "type": "string",
      "description": "Artifact this layer consumes from its predecessor. Owner: 1.3.3.",
      "minLength": 1
    },
    "produces": {
      "type": "string",
      "description": "Artifact this layer produces. Owner: 1.3.3.",
      "enum": [
        "Structured Article Model",
        "Story Model",
        "Screenplay",
        "Shot Plan",
        "Visual Assets",
        "Master Video",
        "Approved Build",
        "Distributable Package"
      ]
    },
    "depends_on": {
      "type": ["integer", "null"],
      "description": "Identifier of the sole layer this layer depends on; equals id-1. The Knowledge layer (id 1) has no predecessor and shall set null. Owner: 1.3.3.",
      "minimum": 0,
      "maximum": 7
    },
    "provider_aware": {
      "type": "boolean",
      "description": "Whether the layer may be aware of external rendering providers. Only the Rendering layer (id 5) may set true. Owner: 1.3.3.",
      "default": false
    }
  }
}
```

---

# Field Reference

| Field | Type | Required | Meaning | Constraint |
|---|---|---|---|---|
| `schema_version` | SchemaVersion | No | Contract schema version | Per common defs |
| `id` | integer | Yes | Ordinal layer id | 1..8 |
| `name` | string | Yes | Layer name | enum of 8 names |
| `consumes` | string | Yes | Predecessor artifact consumed | non-empty |
| `produces` | string | Yes | Artifact produced | enum of 8 products |
| `depends_on` | integer or null | Yes | Sole dependency layer id | equals id-1; null for id 1 |
| `provider_aware` | boolean | Yes | Provider awareness flag | true only for id 5 |

---

# Constraints & Invariants

- **INV-9.2.2-1** (INV-1.3.3-1): Each layer shall declare exactly one predecessor dependency; `depends_on` shall equal `id - 1`, and shall be `null` only for the Knowledge layer (id 1).
- **INV-9.2.2-2** (INV-1.3.3-2): The layer set shall span ids 1 through 8 with the fixed name-to-ordinal mapping: 1 Knowledge, 2 Narrative, 3 Screenplay, 4 Direction, 5 Rendering, 6 Composition, 7 Validation, 8 Publishing.
- **INV-9.2.2-3** (INV-1.3.3-3): Each layer shall produce the artifact fixed for its ordinal, per the `produces` enum ordering.
- **INV-9.2.2-4** (INV-1.3.3-4): Only the Rendering layer (id 5) may set `provider_aware` to `true`; every other layer shall set `false`.
- **INV-9.2.2-5** (INV-1.3.3-5): No layer shall reach past its immediate predecessor; transitive or side dependencies shall be rejected.

---

# Example

```json
{
  "schema_version": "2.0.0",
  "id": 5,
  "name": "Rendering",
  "consumes": "Shot Plan",
  "produces": "Visual Assets",
  "depends_on": 4,
  "provider_aware": true
}
```

---

# Acceptance Criteria

- An instance shall validate only if `depends_on` equals `id - 1` (or is `null` when `id` is 1); this cross-field relation shall be enforced by the platform validator in addition to the schema.
- An instance shall validate only if `provider_aware` is `true` exclusively when `id` equals 5.
- The `name` and `produces` values shall correspond to the layer's ordinal per INV-9.2.2-2 and INV-9.2.2-3.
- No additional properties shall be permitted.

---

# 9.2.3 Data Flow (`data_flow`)

## Insynergy Cinematic Thought Leadership Platform

### Master Specification v2.0

---

# Purpose

The data-flow contract is the typed adjacency graph of the pipeline. It enumerates directed edges between named components, each edge carrying a typed payload. It is owned by section 1.3.2 and is consumed by the orchestration layer to verify that every component consumes exactly one upstream payload, that Render Strategy is the sole branch point, and that FFmpeg Composer is the sole convergence point.

The graph shall run in order from Article Loader through Publish Package, with the single branch at Render Strategy diverging to Animated Assets or Runway Provider, and the single convergence at FFmpeg Composer.

---

# Canonical Schema

```json
{
  "$schema": "https://json-schema.org/draft/2020-12/schema",
  "$id": "https://schemas.insynergy.co/cttp/v2.0/vision/data-flow.schema.json",
  "title": "Data Flow",
  "description": "Typed adjacency graph of the pipeline. Owner: 1.3.2. Render Strategy is the sole branch point; FFmpeg Composer is the sole convergence point.",
  "type": "object",
  "additionalProperties": false,
  "required": ["edges"],
  "properties": {
    "schema_version": {
      "$ref": "https://schemas.insynergy.co/cttp/v2.0/common/defs.schema.json#/$defs/SchemaVersion"
    },
    "edges": {
      "type": "array",
      "description": "Directed, typed edges of the pipeline graph. Owner: 1.3.2.",
      "minItems": 1,
      "items": {
        "type": "object",
        "additionalProperties": false,
        "required": ["from", "to", "payload"],
        "properties": {
          "from": {
            "type": "string",
            "description": "Source component. Owner: 1.3.2.",
            "enum": [
              "Article Loader",
              "Argument Extractor",
              "Dramatic Premise Engine",
              "Story Development",
              "Three Act Structure",
              "Screenplay Engine",
              "Shot Planner",
              "Render Strategy",
              "Animated Assets",
              "Runway Provider",
              "FFmpeg Composer",
              "Quality Gates",
              "Human Approval",
              "Publish Package"
            ]
          },
          "to": {
            "type": "string",
            "description": "Destination component. Owner: 1.3.2.",
            "enum": [
              "Article Loader",
              "Argument Extractor",
              "Dramatic Premise Engine",
              "Story Development",
              "Three Act Structure",
              "Screenplay Engine",
              "Shot Planner",
              "Render Strategy",
              "Animated Assets",
              "Runway Provider",
              "FFmpeg Composer",
              "Quality Gates",
              "Human Approval",
              "Publish Package"
            ]
          },
          "payload": {
            "type": "string",
            "description": "Typed payload carried by the edge. Owner: 1.3.2.",
            "enum": [
              "structured_article_model",
              "extracted_argument",
              "dramatic_premise",
              "developed_story",
              "three_act_model",
              "screenplay",
              "shot_plan",
              "render_routing",
              "visual_assets",
              "master_video",
              "validated_build",
              "approved_build"
            ]
          }
        }
      }
    }
  }
}
```

---

# Field Reference

| Field | Type | Required | Meaning | Constraint |
|---|---|---|---|---|
| `schema_version` | SchemaVersion | No | Contract schema version | Per common defs |
| `edges` | array | Yes | Directed typed edges | minItems 1 |
| `edges[].from` | string | Yes | Source component | enum of 14 components |
| `edges[].to` | string | Yes | Destination component | enum of 14 components |
| `edges[].payload` | string | Yes | Typed payload | enum of 12 payload types |

---

# Constraints & Invariants

- **INV-9.2.3-1** (INV-1.3.2-1): Each component shall consume exactly one upstream payload; the graph validator shall reject any component (other than Article Loader) with zero or multiple distinct upstream payload types.
- **INV-9.2.3-2** (INV-1.3.2-2): Render Strategy shall be the sole branch point; only edges originating at `Render Strategy` may fan out to more than one destination.
- **INV-9.2.3-3** (INV-1.3.2-3): FFmpeg Composer shall be the sole convergence point; only `FFmpeg Composer` may receive edges from more than one source.
- **INV-9.2.3-4** (INV-1.3.2-4): Human Approval shall precede Publish Package on every path; no edge shall reach `Publish Package` except downstream of `Human Approval`.
- **INV-9.2.3-5** (INV-1.3.2-5): No path shall bypass Quality Gates; every route to `Human Approval` shall pass through `Quality Gates`.
- **INV-9.2.3-6** (INV-1.3.2-6): No side channels shall exist; every data transfer between components shall be represented as an edge in `edges`.

---

# Example

```json
{
  "schema_version": "2.0.0",
  "edges": [
    { "from": "Article Loader", "to": "Argument Extractor", "payload": "structured_article_model" },
    { "from": "Argument Extractor", "to": "Dramatic Premise Engine", "payload": "extracted_argument" },
    { "from": "Dramatic Premise Engine", "to": "Story Development", "payload": "dramatic_premise" },
    { "from": "Story Development", "to": "Three Act Structure", "payload": "developed_story" },
    { "from": "Three Act Structure", "to": "Screenplay Engine", "payload": "three_act_model" },
    { "from": "Screenplay Engine", "to": "Shot Planner", "payload": "screenplay" },
    { "from": "Shot Planner", "to": "Render Strategy", "payload": "shot_plan" },
    { "from": "Render Strategy", "to": "Animated Assets", "payload": "render_routing" },
    { "from": "Render Strategy", "to": "Runway Provider", "payload": "render_routing" },
    { "from": "Animated Assets", "to": "FFmpeg Composer", "payload": "visual_assets" },
    { "from": "Runway Provider", "to": "FFmpeg Composer", "payload": "visual_assets" },
    { "from": "FFmpeg Composer", "to": "Quality Gates", "payload": "master_video" },
    { "from": "Quality Gates", "to": "Human Approval", "payload": "validated_build" },
    { "from": "Human Approval", "to": "Publish Package", "payload": "approved_build" }
  ]
}
```

---

# Acceptance Criteria

- An instance shall validate only if every edge's `from`, `to`, and `payload` are drawn from the fixed enumerations.
- The platform graph validator shall additionally enforce the single-branch (INV-9.2.3-2) and single-convergence (INV-9.2.3-3) topology, which the schema alone does not express.
- Any edge to `Publish Package` not descended from `Human Approval`, or any path bypassing `Quality Gates`, shall be rejected.
- No additional properties shall be permitted on the object or on any edge.

---

# 9.2.4 Asset Selection (`asset_selection`)

## Insynergy Cinematic Thought Leadership Platform

### Master Specification v2.0

---

# Purpose

The asset-selection map is the hybrid rendering-selection contract. It maps each narrative moment class to the asset class that shall render it, and records the render-ratio targets that bound how much of a build may be routed to premium generative video. It is owned by section 1.3.6 and consumed by the Render Strategy branch point.

High-narrative-value moments shall map to Runway video (with justification required), controlled-motion moments to animated stills, conceptual-emphasis moments to motion graphics, textual framing to typography, and the throughline to narration. The preview render ratio shall not exceed 0.40 and the final render ratio shall not exceed 0.50.

---

# Canonical Schema

```json
{
  "$schema": "https://json-schema.org/draft/2020-12/schema",
  "$id": "https://schemas.insynergy.co/cttp/v2.0/vision/asset-selection.schema.json",
  "title": "Asset Selection",
  "description": "Hybrid moment-class to asset-class selection map with render-ratio targets. Owner: 1.3.6.",
  "type": "object",
  "additionalProperties": false,
  "required": [
    "high_narrative_value",
    "controlled_motion",
    "conceptual_emphasis",
    "textual_framing",
    "throughline",
    "render_ratio_targets"
  ],
  "properties": {
    "schema_version": {
      "$ref": "https://schemas.insynergy.co/cttp/v2.0/common/defs.schema.json#/$defs/SchemaVersion"
    },
    "high_narrative_value": {
      "type": "object",
      "description": "Mapping for high-narrative-value moments. Owner: 1.3.6.",
      "additionalProperties": false,
      "required": ["class", "justification"],
      "properties": {
        "class": {
          "type": "string",
          "const": "runway_video"
        },
        "justification": {
          "type": "string",
          "const": "required"
        }
      }
    },
    "controlled_motion": {
      "type": "object",
      "description": "Mapping for controlled-motion moments. Owner: 1.3.6.",
      "additionalProperties": false,
      "required": ["class"],
      "properties": {
        "class": {
          "type": "string",
          "const": "animated_still"
        }
      }
    },
    "conceptual_emphasis": {
      "type": "object",
      "description": "Mapping for conceptual-emphasis moments. Owner: 1.3.6.",
      "additionalProperties": false,
      "required": ["class"],
      "properties": {
        "class": {
          "type": "string",
          "const": "motion_graphics"
        }
      }
    },
    "textual_framing": {
      "type": "object",
      "description": "Mapping for textual-framing moments. Owner: 1.3.6.",
      "additionalProperties": false,
      "required": ["class"],
      "properties": {
        "class": {
          "type": "string",
          "const": "typography"
        }
      }
    },
    "throughline": {
      "type": "object",
      "description": "Mapping for the throughline. Owner: 1.3.6.",
      "additionalProperties": false,
      "required": ["class"],
      "properties": {
        "class": {
          "type": "string",
          "const": "narration"
        }
      }
    },
    "render_ratio_targets": {
      "type": "object",
      "description": "Upper bounds on the fraction of a build routed to premium generative video. Owner: 1.3.6.",
      "additionalProperties": false,
      "required": ["preview", "final"],
      "properties": {
        "preview": {
          "allOf": [
            { "$ref": "https://schemas.insynergy.co/cttp/v2.0/common/defs.schema.json#/$defs/Ratio" },
            { "maximum": 0.40 }
          ],
          "description": "Preview render ratio; shall not exceed 0.40. Owner: 1.3.6."
        },
        "final": {
          "allOf": [
            { "$ref": "https://schemas.insynergy.co/cttp/v2.0/common/defs.schema.json#/$defs/Ratio" },
            { "maximum": 0.50 }
          ],
          "description": "Final render ratio; shall not exceed 0.50. Owner: 1.3.6."
        }
      }
    }
  }
}
```

---

# Field Reference

| Field | Type | Required | Meaning | Constraint |
|---|---|---|---|---|
| `schema_version` | SchemaVersion | No | Contract schema version | Per common defs |
| `high_narrative_value.class` | string | Yes | Asset class for high-value moments | const `runway_video` |
| `high_narrative_value.justification` | string | Yes | Justification requirement | const `required` |
| `controlled_motion.class` | string | Yes | Asset class for controlled motion | const `animated_still` |
| `conceptual_emphasis.class` | string | Yes | Asset class for conceptual emphasis | const `motion_graphics` |
| `textual_framing.class` | string | Yes | Asset class for textual framing | const `typography` |
| `throughline.class` | string | Yes | Asset class for the throughline | const `narration` |
| `render_ratio_targets.preview` | Ratio | Yes | Preview render ratio bound | ≤ 0.40 |
| `render_ratio_targets.final` | Ratio | Yes | Final render ratio bound | ≤ 0.50 |

---

# Constraints & Invariants

- **INV-9.2.4-1** (INV-1.3.6-1): Each moment class shall map to exactly one asset class drawn from the set `runway_video`, `animated_still`, `motion_graphics`, `typography`, `narration`.
- **INV-9.2.4-2** (INV-1.3.6-2): High-narrative-value moments shall require justification; `high_narrative_value.justification` shall equal `required`.
- **INV-9.2.4-3** (INV-1.3.6-3): The preview render ratio shall not exceed 0.40.
- **INV-9.2.4-4** (INV-1.3.6-4): The final render ratio shall not exceed 0.50.

---

# Example

```json
{
  "schema_version": "2.0.0",
  "high_narrative_value": { "class": "runway_video", "justification": "required" },
  "controlled_motion": { "class": "animated_still" },
  "conceptual_emphasis": { "class": "motion_graphics" },
  "textual_framing": { "class": "typography" },
  "throughline": { "class": "narration" },
  "render_ratio_targets": { "preview": 0.35, "final": 0.48 }
}
```

---

# Acceptance Criteria

- An instance shall validate only if all five moment-class mappings and the render-ratio targets are present with their fixed `const` asset classes.
- A `preview` value above 0.40 or a `final` value above 0.50 shall be rejected.
- The `Ratio` bounds from the common library shall apply in addition to the local `maximum` constraints.
- No additional properties shall be permitted at any level.

---

# 9.2.5 Approval Record (`approval_record`)

## Insynergy Cinematic Thought Leadership Platform

### Master Specification v2.0

---

# Purpose

The approval record captures a single instance of one of the platform's two human-approval gates. Story approval sits before rendering and confirms screenplay, pacing, dialogue, and dramatic arc; final approval sits after rendering and confirms visual quality, timing, branding, and institutional accuracy. Both gates are fail-closed. The record is owned by section 1.4.1 and consumed by the Validation and Publishing layers.

An approval outcome shall be one of `approved`, `rejected`, or `absent`. Absent shall be treated as rejection; silence shall never constitute consent. Each record shall carry an approval reference for traceability.

---

# Canonical Schema

```json
{
  "$schema": "https://json-schema.org/draft/2020-12/schema",
  "$id": "https://schemas.insynergy.co/cttp/v2.0/vision/approval-record.schema.json",
  "title": "Approval Record",
  "description": "Human-approval record for one of the two governance gates. Owner: 1.4.1. Outcome absent is treated as rejection; silence is never consent. Both gates are fail-closed.",
  "type": "object",
  "additionalProperties": false,
  "required": ["gate", "outcome", "position", "confirms", "gates", "fail_closed", "approval_ref"],
  "properties": {
    "schema_version": {
      "$ref": "https://schemas.insynergy.co/cttp/v2.0/common/defs.schema.json#/$defs/SchemaVersion"
    },
    "gate": {
      "type": "string",
      "description": "Which of the two approval gates this record represents. Owner: 1.4.1.",
      "enum": ["story_approval", "final_approval"]
    },
    "outcome": {
      "type": "string",
      "description": "Approval outcome. absent is treated as rejection; silence is never consent. Owner: 1.4.1.",
      "enum": ["approved", "rejected", "absent"]
    },
    "position": {
      "type": "string",
      "description": "Position of the gate relative to rendering. Owner: 1.4.1.",
      "enum": ["before_rendering", "after_rendering"]
    },
    "confirms": {
      "type": "array",
      "description": "Aspects confirmed at this gate. Owner: 1.4.1.",
      "minItems": 1,
      "uniqueItems": true,
      "items": {
        "type": "string",
        "enum": [
          "screenplay",
          "pacing",
          "dialogue",
          "dramatic_arc",
          "visual_quality",
          "timing",
          "branding",
          "institutional_accuracy"
        ]
      }
    },
    "gates": {
      "type": "string",
      "description": "The downstream stage this approval gates. Owner: 1.4.1.",
      "enum": ["rendering", "packaging"]
    },
    "fail_closed": {
      "type": "boolean",
      "description": "Fail-closed guarantee; shall be true. Owner: 1.4.1.",
      "const": true
    },
    "approval_ref": {
      "$ref": "https://schemas.insynergy.co/cttp/v2.0/common/defs.schema.json#/$defs/ApprovalRef"
    }
  }
}
```

---

# Field Reference

| Field | Type | Required | Meaning | Constraint |
|---|---|---|---|---|
| `schema_version` | SchemaVersion | No | Contract schema version | Per common defs |
| `gate` | string | Yes | Identity of the approval gate | enum `story_approval`, `final_approval` |
| `outcome` | string | Yes | Approval outcome | enum `approved`, `rejected`, `absent` |
| `position` | string | Yes | Gate position vs rendering | enum `before_rendering`, `after_rendering` |
| `confirms` | array | Yes | Confirmed aspects | non-empty, unique, from fixed set |
| `gates` | string | Yes | Downstream stage gated | enum `rendering`, `packaging` |
| `fail_closed` | boolean | Yes | Fail-closed guarantee | const `true` |
| `approval_ref` | ApprovalRef | Yes | Traceability reference | Per common defs |

---

# Constraints & Invariants

- **INV-9.2.5-1** (INV-1.4.1-1): Story approval shall precede rendering (`gate` = `story_approval`, `position` = `before_rendering`, `gates` = `rendering`) and confirm screenplay, pacing, dialogue, and dramatic arc; final approval shall follow rendering (`gate` = `final_approval`, `position` = `after_rendering`, `gates` = `packaging`) and confirm visual quality, timing, branding, and institutional accuracy.
- **INV-9.2.5-2** (INV-1.4.1-2): Both gates shall be fail-closed; `fail_closed` shall be `true`.
- **INV-9.2.5-3** (INV-1.4.1-3): An `absent` outcome shall be treated as a rejection; silence shall never constitute consent.
- **INV-9.2.5-4** (INV-1.4.1-4): Every record shall carry a valid `approval_ref` for audit traceability; a record without one shall be rejected.

---

# Example

```json
{
  "schema_version": "2.0.0",
  "gate": "story_approval",
  "outcome": "approved",
  "position": "before_rendering",
  "confirms": ["screenplay", "pacing", "dialogue", "dramatic_arc"],
  "gates": "rendering",
  "fail_closed": true,
  "approval_ref": "APR-2026-07-20-000117"
}
```

---

# Acceptance Criteria

- An instance shall validate only if `gate`, `outcome`, `position`, `confirms`, `gates`, `fail_closed`, and `approval_ref` are all present.
- The platform validator shall additionally enforce the gate-specific coherence of INV-9.2.5-1 across `gate`, `position`, `gates`, and `confirms`.
- Any record with `outcome` equal to `absent` shall be handled as a rejection by consuming layers, never as consent.
- `fail_closed` shall be `true`; any other value shall be rejected. No additional properties shall be permitted.

---
# 9.3 Story Engine Layer Schemas

**Insynergy Cinematic Thought Leadership Platform — Master Specification v2.0**
**Part 9 — JSON Schema / Appendix**
**Chapter 9.3 — Story Engine Layer Schemas (Part 2)**
**Status: Normative**

---

# Purpose

This chapter formalizes the immutable Story artifact set defined in Part 2 (Story Engine). Each schema herein describes a single artifact produced by the Story Engine and consumed downstream by the Screenplay Engine (Part 3). Per Owner 2.1.8, every Story artifact shall be deterministic and immutable: a given input article, engine version, and story profile shall always yield byte-identical artifacts, and no artifact shall be mutated after emission.

These schemas are the contract of record. An artifact that does not validate against its schema shall not be admitted to the story cache, shall not be sealed, and shall not be passed to the Screenplay Engine.

---

# Design Philosophy

The story is the dependency root of the entire pipeline. Every screenplay, shot plan, storyboard, and render is a transformation of, and traceable to, the Story artifact set. Because the story sits at the root, a defect in a story artifact propagates to every downstream stage. These schemas therefore make each artifact **independently validatable**: any single artifact may be checked in isolation, without recourse to the artifacts that produced it, so that failures are localized at the earliest possible stage.

Sealed artifacts compose the common `ArtifactEnvelope` (schema_version, build_id, generated_at, content_hash) and forbid unevaluated properties. Small embedded objects — metrics blocks and the cache-key descriptor — do not carry the full envelope, as they are components of a sealed parent rather than independently sealed artifacts.

---

# Schemas in This Chapter

- **9.3.1** — `argument-map.json` — Argument extraction and dramatic candidate detection (2.1.2)
- **9.3.2** — `theme.json` — Primary theme selection (2.1.2)
- **9.3.3** — `dramatic-question.json` — The central unresolved question (2.1.2)
- **9.3.4** — `dramatic-premise.json` — One-paragraph dramatic premise (2.1.3)
- **9.3.5** — `logline.json` — Declarative logline (2.1.3)
- **9.3.6** — `character-bible.yaml` — Story-side character bible (2.1.4)
- **9.3.7** — `conflict.json` — Three-layer conflict (2.1.5)
- **9.3.8** — `stakes.json` — Measurable, irreversible stakes (2.1.5)
- **9.3.9** — `time-pressure.json` — Countdown deadline (2.1.5)
- **9.3.10** — `story-arc.json` — Six-stage story arc (2.1.6)
- **9.3.11** — `three-act-structure.json` — Act structure and budget (2.1.6)
- **9.3.12** — `emotional-arc.json` — Emotional state progression (2.1.6)
- **9.3.13** — `concept-placement.json` — Concept placement constraints (2.1.6)
- **9.3.14** — `story-quality-report.json` — Mandatory story gate (2.1.7)
- **9.3.15** — `story-metrics` — Embedded story metrics block (2.1.7)
- **9.3.16** — `story-cache-key` — Embedded cache-key descriptor (2.1.8)

---

# 9.3.1 Argument Map (`argument-map.json`)

**Artifact: Sealed Story artifact**
**Owner: 2.1.2**
**Immutable · Deterministic**

---

# Purpose

Per Owner 2.1.2, the Argument Map is the first Story artifact. It decomposes the source article into claims, evidence, and examples, detects exactly one institutional problem and its proposed solution, and surfaces the subset of claims that may seed drama. Only claims classified as `Tension` or `Consequence` shall be admitted as dramatic candidates; `Factual` and `Structural` claims shall not seed drama.

---

# Canonical Schema

```json
{
  "$schema": "https://json-schema.org/draft/2020-12/schema",
  "$id": "https://schemas.insynergy.co/cttp/v2.0/story/argument-map.schema.json",
  "title": "ArgumentMap",
  "description": "Immutable decomposition of the source article into claims, evidence, examples, and dramatic candidates. Owner 2.1.2.",
  "type": "object",
  "allOf": [
    { "$ref": "https://schemas.insynergy.co/cttp/v2.0/common/defs.schema.json" }
  ],
  "properties": {
    "schema_version": { "$ref": "https://schemas.insynergy.co/cttp/v2.0/common/defs.schema.json#/$defs/SchemaVersion" },
    "build_id": { "$ref": "https://schemas.insynergy.co/cttp/v2.0/common/defs.schema.json#/$defs/BuildId" },
    "generated_at": { "$ref": "https://schemas.insynergy.co/cttp/v2.0/common/defs.schema.json#/$defs/Iso8601" },
    "content_hash": { "$ref": "https://schemas.insynergy.co/cttp/v2.0/common/defs.schema.json#/$defs/ContentHash" },
    "claims": {
      "type": "array",
      "minItems": 1,
      "items": {
        "type": "object",
        "additionalProperties": false,
        "properties": {
          "id": { "$ref": "https://schemas.insynergy.co/cttp/v2.0/common/defs.schema.json#/$defs/RefId" },
          "text": { "type": "string", "minLength": 1 },
          "classification": {
            "type": "string",
            "enum": ["Factual", "Structural", "Tension", "Consequence"]
          }
        },
        "required": ["id", "text", "classification"]
      }
    },
    "evidence": {
      "type": "array",
      "items": {
        "type": "object",
        "additionalProperties": false,
        "properties": {
          "id": { "$ref": "https://schemas.insynergy.co/cttp/v2.0/common/defs.schema.json#/$defs/RefId" },
          "text": { "type": "string", "minLength": 1 },
          "supports_claim": { "$ref": "https://schemas.insynergy.co/cttp/v2.0/common/defs.schema.json#/$defs/RefId" }
        },
        "required": ["id", "text", "supports_claim"]
      }
    },
    "examples": {
      "type": "array",
      "items": {
        "type": "object",
        "additionalProperties": false,
        "properties": {
          "id": { "$ref": "https://schemas.insynergy.co/cttp/v2.0/common/defs.schema.json#/$defs/RefId" },
          "text": { "type": "string", "minLength": 1 }
        },
        "required": ["id", "text"]
      }
    },
    "institutional_problem": { "type": "string", "minLength": 1 },
    "proposed_solution": { "type": "string", "minLength": 1 },
    "problem_class": {
      "type": "string",
      "minLength": 1,
      "description": "Classification of the institutional problem, e.g. \"governance\"."
    },
    "dramatic_candidates": {
      "type": "array",
      "minItems": 1,
      "items": { "$ref": "https://schemas.insynergy.co/cttp/v2.0/common/defs.schema.json#/$defs/RefId" },
      "description": "References to claims classified Tension or Consequence."
    }
  },
  "required": [
    "schema_version",
    "build_id",
    "generated_at",
    "content_hash",
    "claims",
    "evidence",
    "examples",
    "institutional_problem",
    "proposed_solution",
    "problem_class",
    "dramatic_candidates"
  ],
  "unevaluatedProperties": false
}
```

---

# Field Reference

| Field | Type | Required | Meaning | Constraint |
|---|---|---|---|---|
| `schema_version` | SchemaVersion | Yes | Envelope: schema version | From common defs |
| `build_id` | BuildId | Yes | Envelope: producing build | From common defs |
| `generated_at` | Iso8601 | Yes | Envelope: emission timestamp | From common defs |
| `content_hash` | ContentHash | Yes | Envelope: artifact content hash | From common defs |
| `claims` | array[Claim] | Yes | Extracted claims | `minItems: 1` |
| `claims[].classification` | enum | Yes | Claim category | `Factual` \| `Structural` \| `Tension` \| `Consequence` |
| `evidence` | array[Evidence] | Yes | Supporting evidence | Each references a claim |
| `examples` | array[Example] | Yes | Illustrative examples | — |
| `institutional_problem` | string | Yes | Detected institutional problem | Exactly one; non-empty |
| `proposed_solution` | string | Yes | Article's proposed solution | Non-empty |
| `problem_class` | string | Yes | Problem classification | e.g. `governance` |
| `dramatic_candidates` | array[RefId] | Yes | Claims eligible to seed drama | `minItems: 1`; Tension/Consequence only |

---

# Constraints & Invariants

- **INV-9.3.1-A** — Exactly one institutional problem shall be present (Owner 2.1.2). `institutional_problem` is a single string, not an array.
- **INV-9.3.1-B** — Every `RefId` in `dramatic_candidates` shall resolve to a claim whose `classification` is `Tension` or `Consequence` (Owner 2.1.2). `Factual` and `Structural` claims shall not appear.
- **INV-9.3.1-C** — Every `evidence[].supports_claim` shall resolve to an existing `claims[].id` (referential integrity).
- **INV-9.3.1-D** — The artifact shall be immutable and deterministic per 2.1.8; `content_hash` shall cover all body fields.

---

# Example

```json
{
  "schema_version": "2.0.0",
  "build_id": "bld_20260720_0001",
  "generated_at": "2026-07-20T09:14:05Z",
  "content_hash": "sha256:5f3c9a1b7e0d24a8c6b1f0e93d7a2c4b8e1f6079a3d5c2b1e0f4a9c8d7b6e5f4",
  "claims": [
    { "id": "clm-001", "text": "Boards approved the merger without independent review.", "classification": "Tension" },
    { "id": "clm-002", "text": "The oversight committee met quarterly.", "classification": "Factual" },
    { "id": "clm-003", "text": "Unchecked approval led to a regulatory penalty.", "classification": "Consequence" }
  ],
  "evidence": [
    { "id": "evd-001", "text": "Minutes show no dissent recorded.", "supports_claim": "clm-001" }
  ],
  "examples": [
    { "id": "exm-001", "text": "A 2024 fine imposed after a similar lapse." }
  ],
  "institutional_problem": "Governance approvals bypass independent review under deadline pressure.",
  "proposed_solution": "Mandatory independent review gate before irreversible approval.",
  "problem_class": "governance",
  "dramatic_candidates": ["clm-001", "clm-003"]
}
```

---

# Acceptance Criteria

- The instance validates against `argument-map.schema.json` under draft 2020-12.
- `additionalProperties`/`unevaluatedProperties` are honored: no undeclared fields.
- Exactly one `institutional_problem`; at least one dramatic candidate.
- All dramatic candidates reference Tension/Consequence claims; all evidence references existing claims.

---

# 9.3.2 Theme (`theme.json`)

**Artifact: Sealed Story artifact**
**Owner: 2.1.2**
**Immutable · Deterministic**

---

# Purpose

Per Owner 2.1.2, the Theme artifact records the single primary theme selected for the story, its score, and the themes considered and rejected. The primary theme drives institutional conflict derivation downstream (see 9.3.7).

---

# Canonical Schema

```json
{
  "$schema": "https://json-schema.org/draft/2020-12/schema",
  "$id": "https://schemas.insynergy.co/cttp/v2.0/story/theme.schema.json",
  "title": "Theme",
  "description": "Primary theme selection with score and rejected alternatives. Owner 2.1.2.",
  "type": "object",
  "allOf": [
    { "$ref": "https://schemas.insynergy.co/cttp/v2.0/common/defs.schema.json" }
  ],
  "properties": {
    "schema_version": { "$ref": "https://schemas.insynergy.co/cttp/v2.0/common/defs.schema.json#/$defs/SchemaVersion" },
    "build_id": { "$ref": "https://schemas.insynergy.co/cttp/v2.0/common/defs.schema.json#/$defs/BuildId" },
    "generated_at": { "$ref": "https://schemas.insynergy.co/cttp/v2.0/common/defs.schema.json#/$defs/Iso8601" },
    "content_hash": { "$ref": "https://schemas.insynergy.co/cttp/v2.0/common/defs.schema.json#/$defs/ContentHash" },
    "primary_theme": { "type": "string", "minLength": 1 },
    "theme_score": { "$ref": "https://schemas.insynergy.co/cttp/v2.0/common/defs.schema.json#/$defs/Score" },
    "rejected_themes": {
      "type": "array",
      "items": { "type": "string", "minLength": 1 }
    }
  },
  "required": [
    "schema_version",
    "build_id",
    "generated_at",
    "content_hash",
    "primary_theme",
    "theme_score",
    "rejected_themes"
  ],
  "unevaluatedProperties": false
}
```

---

# Field Reference

| Field | Type | Required | Meaning | Constraint |
|---|---|---|---|---|
| `schema_version` | SchemaVersion | Yes | Envelope | From common defs |
| `build_id` | BuildId | Yes | Envelope | From common defs |
| `generated_at` | Iso8601 | Yes | Envelope | From common defs |
| `content_hash` | ContentHash | Yes | Envelope | From common defs |
| `primary_theme` | string | Yes | The selected theme | Exactly one; non-empty |
| `theme_score` | Score | Yes | Weighted theme score | `0..1` per Score def |
| `rejected_themes` | array[string] | Yes | Themes considered and rejected | May be empty |

---

# Constraints & Invariants

- **INV-9.3.2-A** — There shall be exactly one `primary_theme` (Owner 2.1.2).
- **INV-9.3.2-B** — `theme_score` shall be computed deterministically from the theme scoring weights: `dramatic_potential 0.4`, `institutional_accuracy 0.3`, `audience_relevance 0.2`, `uniqueness 0.1` (weights sum to 1.0). These weights are descriptive of the derivation and are fixed for the engine version.
- **INV-9.3.2-C** — `primary_theme` shall not appear within `rejected_themes`.

---

# Example

```json
{
  "schema_version": "2.0.0",
  "build_id": "bld_20260720_0001",
  "generated_at": "2026-07-20T09:14:06Z",
  "content_hash": "sha256:9b2e7c4d1a806f35e2c9b0a7d64f1e83c5a2b9d0e7f4c1a6b3e0d9c8f7a6b5e4",
  "primary_theme": "Governance fails when speed overrides independent review.",
  "theme_score": 0.91,
  "rejected_themes": [
    "Regulation is always burdensome.",
    "Individual negligence causes institutional failure."
  ]
}
```

---

# Acceptance Criteria

- Validates against `theme.schema.json` under draft 2020-12.
- Exactly one primary theme; score within `[0,1]`.
- Primary theme is disjoint from rejected themes.

---

# 9.3.3 Dramatic Question (`dramatic-question.json`)

**Artifact: Sealed Story artifact**
**Owner: 2.1.2**
**Immutable · Deterministic**

---

# Purpose

Per Owner 2.1.2, the Dramatic Question artifact records the single central question that drives the narrative. The question shall remain unresolved until Act 3 and shall be answerable only by a human decision — never by exposition or by the concept itself.

---

# Canonical Schema

```json
{
  "$schema": "https://json-schema.org/draft/2020-12/schema",
  "$id": "https://schemas.insynergy.co/cttp/v2.0/story/dramatic-question.schema.json",
  "title": "DramaticQuestion",
  "description": "The single central dramatic question, resolved only in Act 3. Owner 2.1.2.",
  "type": "object",
  "allOf": [
    { "$ref": "https://schemas.insynergy.co/cttp/v2.0/common/defs.schema.json" }
  ],
  "properties": {
    "schema_version": { "$ref": "https://schemas.insynergy.co/cttp/v2.0/common/defs.schema.json#/$defs/SchemaVersion" },
    "build_id": { "$ref": "https://schemas.insynergy.co/cttp/v2.0/common/defs.schema.json#/$defs/BuildId" },
    "generated_at": { "$ref": "https://schemas.insynergy.co/cttp/v2.0/common/defs.schema.json#/$defs/Iso8601" },
    "content_hash": { "$ref": "https://schemas.insynergy.co/cttp/v2.0/common/defs.schema.json#/$defs/ContentHash" },
    "dramatic_question": { "type": "string", "minLength": 1 },
    "resolved_in_act": {
      "allOf": [ { "$ref": "https://schemas.insynergy.co/cttp/v2.0/common/defs.schema.json#/$defs/Act" } ],
      "const": 3
    }
  },
  "required": [
    "schema_version",
    "build_id",
    "generated_at",
    "content_hash",
    "dramatic_question",
    "resolved_in_act"
  ],
  "unevaluatedProperties": false
}
```

---

# Field Reference

| Field | Type | Required | Meaning | Constraint |
|---|---|---|---|---|
| `schema_version` | SchemaVersion | Yes | Envelope | From common defs |
| `build_id` | BuildId | Yes | Envelope | From common defs |
| `generated_at` | Iso8601 | Yes | Envelope | From common defs |
| `content_hash` | ContentHash | Yes | Envelope | From common defs |
| `dramatic_question` | string | Yes | The central question | Exactly one; non-empty |
| `resolved_in_act` | Act | Yes | Act of resolution | `const: 3` |

---

# Constraints & Invariants

- **INV-9.3.3-A** — Exactly one `dramatic_question` shall be present (Owner 2.1.2).
- **INV-9.3.3-B** — `resolved_in_act` shall be `3`; the question shall be unresolved until Act 3.
- **INV-9.3.3-C** — The question shall be phrased such that it can be answered only by a human decision (Owner 2.1.2); it shall not be answerable by exposition or by the concept alone.

---

# Example

```json
{
  "schema_version": "2.0.0",
  "build_id": "bld_20260720_0001",
  "generated_at": "2026-07-20T09:14:07Z",
  "content_hash": "sha256:1c8a3f5b9d2e60471a0c8b7f4e6d3a2c9b1e0f8d5a7c4b3e2d1f0a9c8b7e6d5c",
  "dramatic_question": "Will the chair halt the approval before the deadline, or let it pass unchecked?",
  "resolved_in_act": 3
}
```

---

# Acceptance Criteria

- Validates against `dramatic-question.schema.json` under draft 2020-12.
- `resolved_in_act` equals `3`.
- Question is a single non-empty string requiring a human decision to answer.

---

# 9.3.4 Dramatic Premise (`dramatic-premise.json`)

**Artifact: Sealed Story artifact**
**Owner: 2.1.3**
**Immutable · Deterministic**

---

# Purpose

Per Owner 2.1.3, the Dramatic Premise is a single-paragraph statement establishing the protagonist's situation, a discovery, the institutional tension, an irreversible deadline, and the required decision. The premise is character-first: it shall not lead with the concept.

---

# Canonical Schema

```json
{
  "$schema": "https://json-schema.org/draft/2020-12/schema",
  "$id": "https://schemas.insynergy.co/cttp/v2.0/story/dramatic-premise.schema.json",
  "title": "DramaticPremise",
  "description": "One-paragraph, character-first dramatic premise. Owner 2.1.3.",
  "type": "object",
  "allOf": [
    { "$ref": "https://schemas.insynergy.co/cttp/v2.0/common/defs.schema.json" }
  ],
  "properties": {
    "schema_version": { "$ref": "https://schemas.insynergy.co/cttp/v2.0/common/defs.schema.json#/$defs/SchemaVersion" },
    "build_id": { "$ref": "https://schemas.insynergy.co/cttp/v2.0/common/defs.schema.json#/$defs/BuildId" },
    "generated_at": { "$ref": "https://schemas.insynergy.co/cttp/v2.0/common/defs.schema.json#/$defs/Iso8601" },
    "content_hash": { "$ref": "https://schemas.insynergy.co/cttp/v2.0/common/defs.schema.json#/$defs/ContentHash" },
    "premise": {
      "type": "object",
      "additionalProperties": false,
      "properties": {
        "protagonist_situation": { "type": "string", "minLength": 1 },
        "discovery": { "type": "string", "minLength": 1 },
        "institutional_tension": { "type": "string", "minLength": 1 },
        "irreversible_deadline": { "type": "string", "minLength": 1 },
        "required_decision": { "type": "string", "minLength": 1 }
      },
      "required": [
        "protagonist_situation",
        "discovery",
        "institutional_tension",
        "irreversible_deadline",
        "required_decision"
      ]
    },
    "paragraph_count": { "type": "integer", "const": 1 },
    "protagonist_present": { "type": "boolean", "const": true },
    "institutional_tension_present": { "type": "boolean", "const": true },
    "irreversible_deadline_present": { "type": "boolean", "const": true },
    "decision_required": { "type": "boolean", "const": true },
    "concept_first": { "type": "boolean", "const": false }
  },
  "required": [
    "schema_version",
    "build_id",
    "generated_at",
    "content_hash",
    "premise",
    "paragraph_count",
    "protagonist_present",
    "institutional_tension_present",
    "irreversible_deadline_present",
    "decision_required",
    "concept_first"
  ],
  "unevaluatedProperties": false
}
```

---

# Field Reference

| Field | Type | Required | Meaning | Constraint |
|---|---|---|---|---|
| `schema_version` | SchemaVersion | Yes | Envelope | From common defs |
| `build_id` | BuildId | Yes | Envelope | From common defs |
| `generated_at` | Iso8601 | Yes | Envelope | From common defs |
| `content_hash` | ContentHash | Yes | Envelope | From common defs |
| `premise.protagonist_situation` | string | Yes | Protagonist's starting state | Non-empty |
| `premise.discovery` | string | Yes | The precipitating discovery | Non-empty |
| `premise.institutional_tension` | string | Yes | The institutional conflict | Non-empty |
| `premise.irreversible_deadline` | string | Yes | The irreversible deadline | Non-empty |
| `premise.required_decision` | string | Yes | Decision the protagonist must make | Non-empty |
| `paragraph_count` | integer | Yes | Paragraph count | `const: 1` |
| `protagonist_present` | boolean | Yes | Protagonist established | `const: true` |
| `institutional_tension_present` | boolean | Yes | Tension established | `const: true` |
| `irreversible_deadline_present` | boolean | Yes | Deadline established | `const: true` |
| `decision_required` | boolean | Yes | A decision is required | `const: true` |
| `concept_first` | boolean | Yes | Whether concept leads | `const: false` |

---

# Constraints & Invariants

- **INV-9.3.4-A** — `paragraph_count` shall equal 1 (Owner 2.1.3): the premise is exactly one paragraph.
- **INV-9.3.4-B** — `protagonist_present`, `institutional_tension_present`, `irreversible_deadline_present`, and `decision_required` shall all be `true` (Owner 2.1.3).
- **INV-9.3.4-C** — `concept_first` shall be `false`: the premise shall be character-first, never concept-first (Owner 2.1.3).

---

# Example

```json
{
  "schema_version": "2.0.0",
  "build_id": "bld_20260720_0001",
  "generated_at": "2026-07-20T09:14:08Z",
  "content_hash": "sha256:7e1d4a9c2b806f53c1a9b0e7d4f6c3a2b9e1f0d8c5a7b4e3d2f1a0c9b8e7d6c5",
  "premise": {
    "protagonist_situation": "A newly appointed committee chair inherits a fast-tracked approval.",
    "discovery": "She finds the independent review was skipped.",
    "institutional_tension": "Halting it defies the board that promoted her.",
    "irreversible_deadline": "Approval auto-finalizes at midnight.",
    "required_decision": "She must decide whether to stop the vote."
  },
  "paragraph_count": 1,
  "protagonist_present": true,
  "institutional_tension_present": true,
  "irreversible_deadline_present": true,
  "decision_required": true,
  "concept_first": false
}
```

---

# Acceptance Criteria

- Validates against `dramatic-premise.schema.json` under draft 2020-12.
- All five premise fields non-empty; all boolean flags at their required const values.
- `paragraph_count == 1`; `concept_first == false`.

---

# 9.3.5 Logline (`logline.json`)

**Artifact: Sealed Story artifact**
**Owner: 2.1.3**
**Immutable · Deterministic**

---

# Purpose

Per Owner 2.1.3, the Logline is a single declarative sentence of at most 50 words, derivable from the premise, that names the inciting incident, protagonist, goal, stakes, and potential loss. It shall be declarative, not interrogative.

The 50-word limit is enforced as a documented derivation constraint (INV-9.3.5-A). A `maxLength` character bound is optional and, if present, is advisory only.

---

# Canonical Schema

```json
{
  "$schema": "https://json-schema.org/draft/2020-12/schema",
  "$id": "https://schemas.insynergy.co/cttp/v2.0/story/logline.schema.json",
  "title": "Logline",
  "description": "Declarative logline (<=50 words) derived from the premise. Owner 2.1.3.",
  "type": "object",
  "allOf": [
    { "$ref": "https://schemas.insynergy.co/cttp/v2.0/common/defs.schema.json" }
  ],
  "properties": {
    "schema_version": { "$ref": "https://schemas.insynergy.co/cttp/v2.0/common/defs.schema.json#/$defs/SchemaVersion" },
    "build_id": { "$ref": "https://schemas.insynergy.co/cttp/v2.0/common/defs.schema.json#/$defs/BuildId" },
    "generated_at": { "$ref": "https://schemas.insynergy.co/cttp/v2.0/common/defs.schema.json#/$defs/Iso8601" },
    "content_hash": { "$ref": "https://schemas.insynergy.co/cttp/v2.0/common/defs.schema.json#/$defs/ContentHash" },
    "logline": {
      "type": "string",
      "minLength": 1,
      "description": "Declarative sentence, <=50 words (word limit enforced by INV-9.3.5-A)."
    },
    "incident_present": { "type": "boolean", "const": true },
    "protagonist_present": { "type": "boolean", "const": true },
    "goal_present": { "type": "boolean", "const": true },
    "stakes_present": { "type": "boolean", "const": true },
    "loss_present": { "type": "boolean", "const": true },
    "question_form": { "type": "boolean", "const": false }
  },
  "required": [
    "schema_version",
    "build_id",
    "generated_at",
    "content_hash",
    "logline",
    "incident_present",
    "protagonist_present",
    "goal_present",
    "stakes_present",
    "loss_present",
    "question_form"
  ],
  "unevaluatedProperties": false
}
```

---

# Field Reference

| Field | Type | Required | Meaning | Constraint |
|---|---|---|---|---|
| `schema_version` | SchemaVersion | Yes | Envelope | From common defs |
| `build_id` | BuildId | Yes | Envelope | From common defs |
| `generated_at` | Iso8601 | Yes | Envelope | From common defs |
| `content_hash` | ContentHash | Yes | Envelope | From common defs |
| `logline` | string | Yes | The logline text | Declarative; ≤50 words |
| `incident_present` | boolean | Yes | Inciting incident named | `const: true` |
| `protagonist_present` | boolean | Yes | Protagonist named | `const: true` |
| `goal_present` | boolean | Yes | Goal named | `const: true` |
| `stakes_present` | boolean | Yes | Stakes named | `const: true` |
| `loss_present` | boolean | Yes | Potential loss named | `const: true` |
| `question_form` | boolean | Yes | Whether phrased as a question | `const: false` |

---

# Constraints & Invariants

- **INV-9.3.5-A** — `logline` shall contain at most 50 words (Owner 2.1.3). Word count is the number of whitespace-delimited tokens.
- **INV-9.3.5-B** — `logline` shall be declarative; `question_form` shall be `false`.
- **INV-9.3.5-C** — `incident_present`, `protagonist_present`, `goal_present`, `stakes_present`, and `loss_present` shall all be `true`; the corresponding elements shall be present in the logline text.
- **INV-9.3.5-D** — The logline shall be derivable from the Dramatic Premise (9.3.4).

---

# Example

```json
{
  "schema_version": "2.0.0",
  "build_id": "bld_20260720_0001",
  "generated_at": "2026-07-20T09:14:09Z",
  "content_hash": "sha256:2f0c7b1a9d4e63852c1b0a9e7f6d3c2b8a1e0f9d5c4b7a3e2d1f0c9b8a7e6d5f",
  "logline": "When a new committee chair discovers a skipped review hours before an irreversible approval, she must halt the board's vote or let a flawed merger finalize and destroy her institution's credibility.",
  "incident_present": true,
  "protagonist_present": true,
  "goal_present": true,
  "stakes_present": true,
  "loss_present": true,
  "question_form": false
}
```

---

# Acceptance Criteria

- Validates against `logline.schema.json` under draft 2020-12.
- Logline is ≤50 words and declarative (`question_form == false`).
- All five presence flags are `true`.

---

# 9.3.6 Character Bible (`character-bible.yaml`)

**Artifact: Sealed Story artifact**
**Owner: 2.1.4**
**Immutable · Deterministic**

---

# Purpose

Per Owner 2.1.4, the Character Bible defines exactly one protagonist, zero to three supporting characters, and zero or one antagonistic force (which may be institutional). The protagonist's `arc` is a continuous, ordered emotional progression (for example, Control → Understanding → Institutional Design).

This is the **Story-side** character bible. It is distinct from the Shot/Render-side reference bible with versioned `RefId`s defined in 4.1.7 / 5.1.4; the two are separate artifacts and shall not be conflated. Although the file extension is `.yaml`, the artifact's logical structure is defined by this JSON Schema and validated after YAML-to-JSON normalization.

---

# Canonical Schema

```json
{
  "$schema": "https://json-schema.org/draft/2020-12/schema",
  "$id": "https://schemas.insynergy.co/cttp/v2.0/story/character-bible.schema.json",
  "title": "CharacterBible",
  "description": "Story-side character bible: one protagonist, 0..3 supporting, 0..1 antagonistic. Owner 2.1.4.",
  "type": "object",
  "allOf": [
    { "$ref": "https://schemas.insynergy.co/cttp/v2.0/common/defs.schema.json" }
  ],
  "properties": {
    "schema_version": { "$ref": "https://schemas.insynergy.co/cttp/v2.0/common/defs.schema.json#/$defs/SchemaVersion" },
    "build_id": { "$ref": "https://schemas.insynergy.co/cttp/v2.0/common/defs.schema.json#/$defs/BuildId" },
    "generated_at": { "$ref": "https://schemas.insynergy.co/cttp/v2.0/common/defs.schema.json#/$defs/Iso8601" },
    "content_hash": { "$ref": "https://schemas.insynergy.co/cttp/v2.0/common/defs.schema.json#/$defs/ContentHash" },
    "protagonist": {
      "type": "object",
      "additionalProperties": false,
      "properties": {
        "id": { "$ref": "https://schemas.insynergy.co/cttp/v2.0/common/defs.schema.json#/$defs/RefId" },
        "role": { "type": "string", "minLength": 1 },
        "goal": { "type": "string", "minLength": 1 },
        "fear": { "type": "string", "minLength": 1 },
        "flaw": { "type": "string", "minLength": 1 },
        "competence": { "type": "string", "minLength": 1 },
        "decision_required": { "type": "string", "minLength": 1 },
        "arc": {
          "type": "array",
          "minItems": 2,
          "items": { "type": "string", "minLength": 1 },
          "description": "Ordered, continuous emotional progression, e.g. Control -> Understanding -> Institutional Design."
        }
      },
      "required": ["id", "role", "goal", "fear", "flaw", "competence", "decision_required", "arc"]
    },
    "supporting": {
      "type": "array",
      "maxItems": 3,
      "items": {
        "type": "object",
        "additionalProperties": false,
        "properties": {
          "id": { "$ref": "https://schemas.insynergy.co/cttp/v2.0/common/defs.schema.json#/$defs/RefId" },
          "function": { "type": "string", "minLength": 1 },
          "pressure_applied": { "type": "string", "minLength": 1 },
          "relationship_to_protagonist": { "type": "string", "minLength": 1 }
        },
        "required": ["id", "function", "pressure_applied", "relationship_to_protagonist"]
      }
    },
    "antagonistic": {
      "type": ["object", "null"],
      "additionalProperties": false,
      "properties": {
        "id": { "$ref": "https://schemas.insynergy.co/cttp/v2.0/common/defs.schema.json#/$defs/RefId" },
        "function": { "type": "string", "minLength": 1 },
        "is_institutional": { "type": "boolean" },
        "pressure_applied": { "type": "string", "minLength": 1 },
        "relationship_to_protagonist": { "type": "string", "minLength": 1 }
      },
      "required": ["id", "function", "is_institutional", "pressure_applied", "relationship_to_protagonist"]
    }
  },
  "required": [
    "schema_version",
    "build_id",
    "generated_at",
    "content_hash",
    "protagonist",
    "supporting",
    "antagonistic"
  ],
  "unevaluatedProperties": false
}
```

---

# Field Reference

| Field | Type | Required | Meaning | Constraint |
|---|---|---|---|---|
| `schema_version` | SchemaVersion | Yes | Envelope | From common defs |
| `build_id` | BuildId | Yes | Envelope | From common defs |
| `generated_at` | Iso8601 | Yes | Envelope | From common defs |
| `content_hash` | ContentHash | Yes | Envelope | From common defs |
| `protagonist` | object | Yes | The single protagonist | Exactly one |
| `protagonist.id` | RefId | Yes | Protagonist identifier | From common defs |
| `protagonist.role` | string | Yes | Role/title | Non-empty |
| `protagonist.goal` | string | Yes | Driving goal | Non-empty |
| `protagonist.fear` | string | Yes | Core fear | Non-empty |
| `protagonist.flaw` | string | Yes | Character flaw | Seeds internal conflict (9.3.7) |
| `protagonist.competence` | string | Yes | Competence | Non-empty |
| `protagonist.decision_required` | string | Yes | Required decision | Non-empty |
| `protagonist.arc` | array[string] | Yes | Ordered emotional progression | `minItems: 2`; continuous |
| `supporting` | array[object] | Yes | Supporting characters | `0..3` |
| `supporting[].function` | string | Yes | Narrative function | Non-empty |
| `supporting[].pressure_applied` | string | Yes | Pressure exerted on protagonist | Non-empty |
| `supporting[].relationship_to_protagonist` | string | Yes | Relationship | Non-empty |
| `antagonistic` | object \| null | Yes | Antagonistic force | `0..1`; may be institutional |
| `antagonistic.is_institutional` | boolean | Yes (if object) | Whether force is institutional | — |

---

# Constraints & Invariants

- **INV-9.3.6-A** — Exactly one protagonist shall be present (Owner 2.1.4).
- **INV-9.3.6-B** — `supporting` shall contain between 0 and 3 entries (`maxItems: 3`).
- **INV-9.3.6-C** — `antagonistic` shall be either a single object or `null` (0..1); the antagonistic force may be institutional (`is_institutional: true`).
- **INV-9.3.6-D** — `protagonist.arc` shall be a continuous, ordered emotional progression with no omitted intermediate stage; it aligns with the emotional arc of 9.3.12.
- **INV-9.3.6-E** — This artifact is the Story-side bible and shall not be confused with the Shot/Render-side reference bible (4.1.7 / 5.1.4).

---

# Example

```json
{
  "schema_version": "2.0.0",
  "build_id": "bld_20260720_0001",
  "generated_at": "2026-07-20T09:14:10Z",
  "content_hash": "sha256:4a9e2c7b1d806f35e0c1b9a7f4d6e3c2b8a1f0e9d5c7b4a3e2d1f0c9b8a7e6d5",
  "protagonist": {
    "id": "chr-protagonist",
    "role": "Committee Chair",
    "goal": "Preserve the institution's integrity",
    "fear": "Being blamed for obstructing the board",
    "flaw": "Deference to hierarchy",
    "competence": "Rigorous procedural knowledge",
    "decision_required": "Whether to halt the approval",
    "arc": ["Control", "Understanding", "Institutional Design"]
  },
  "supporting": [
    {
      "id": "chr-cfo",
      "function": "Advocate for speed",
      "pressure_applied": "Urges immediate approval to hit the deadline",
      "relationship_to_protagonist": "Peer and rival"
    }
  ],
  "antagonistic": {
    "id": "chr-board",
    "function": "Enforce the fast-track norm",
    "is_institutional": true,
    "pressure_applied": "Threatens censure for delay",
    "relationship_to_protagonist": "Governing body"
  }
}
```

---

# Acceptance Criteria

- Validates against `character-bible.schema.json` under draft 2020-12 after YAML-to-JSON normalization.
- Exactly one protagonist; supporting count in `[0,3]`; antagonistic is object or null.
- Protagonist arc has at least two ordered stages.

---

# 9.3.7 Conflict (`conflict.json`)

**Artifact: Sealed Story artifact**
**Owner: 2.1.5**
**Immutable · Deterministic**

---

# Purpose

Per Owner 2.1.5, the Conflict artifact records the three required conflict layers: external, internal, and institutional. All three shall be present. The institutional layer derives from the primary theme (9.3.2); the internal layer derives from the protagonist's flaw (9.3.6).

---

# Canonical Schema

```json
{
  "$schema": "https://json-schema.org/draft/2020-12/schema",
  "$id": "https://schemas.insynergy.co/cttp/v2.0/story/conflict.schema.json",
  "title": "Conflict",
  "description": "Three-layer conflict: external, internal, institutional. Owner 2.1.5.",
  "type": "object",
  "allOf": [
    { "$ref": "https://schemas.insynergy.co/cttp/v2.0/common/defs.schema.json" }
  ],
  "properties": {
    "schema_version": { "$ref": "https://schemas.insynergy.co/cttp/v2.0/common/defs.schema.json#/$defs/SchemaVersion" },
    "build_id": { "$ref": "https://schemas.insynergy.co/cttp/v2.0/common/defs.schema.json#/$defs/BuildId" },
    "generated_at": { "$ref": "https://schemas.insynergy.co/cttp/v2.0/common/defs.schema.json#/$defs/Iso8601" },
    "content_hash": { "$ref": "https://schemas.insynergy.co/cttp/v2.0/common/defs.schema.json#/$defs/ContentHash" },
    "external": { "type": "string", "minLength": 1 },
    "internal": { "type": "string", "minLength": 1 },
    "institutional": { "type": "string", "minLength": 1 }
  },
  "required": [
    "schema_version",
    "build_id",
    "generated_at",
    "content_hash",
    "external",
    "internal",
    "institutional"
  ],
  "unevaluatedProperties": false
}
```

---

# Field Reference

| Field | Type | Required | Meaning | Constraint |
|---|---|---|---|---|
| `schema_version` | SchemaVersion | Yes | Envelope | From common defs |
| `build_id` | BuildId | Yes | Envelope | From common defs |
| `generated_at` | Iso8601 | Yes | Envelope | From common defs |
| `content_hash` | ContentHash | Yes | Envelope | From common defs |
| `external` | string | Yes | External conflict layer | Non-empty |
| `internal` | string | Yes | Internal conflict layer | Non-empty; from protagonist flaw |
| `institutional` | string | Yes | Institutional conflict layer | Non-empty; from primary theme |

---

# Constraints & Invariants

- **INV-9.3.7-A** — All three layers (`external`, `internal`, `institutional`) shall be present and non-empty (Owner 2.1.5).
- **INV-9.3.7-B** — `institutional` shall derive from the `primary_theme` of the Theme artifact (9.3.2).
- **INV-9.3.7-C** — `internal` shall derive from the protagonist's `flaw` in the Character Bible (9.3.6).

---

# Example

```json
{
  "schema_version": "2.0.0",
  "build_id": "bld_20260720_0001",
  "generated_at": "2026-07-20T09:14:11Z",
  "content_hash": "sha256:6d1a4c9e2b807f35c0a1b9e7f4d6c3a2b8e1f0d9c5a7b4e3d2f1a0c9b8e7d6c5",
  "external": "The board pushes to finalize the approval before midnight.",
  "internal": "Her deference to hierarchy fights her duty to intervene.",
  "institutional": "The governance norm rewards speed over independent review."
}
```

---

# Acceptance Criteria

- Validates against `conflict.schema.json` under draft 2020-12.
- All three conflict layers are present and non-empty.

---

# 9.3.8 Stakes (`stakes.json`)

**Artifact: Sealed Story artifact**
**Owner: 2.1.5**
**Immutable · Deterministic**

---

# Purpose

Per Owner 2.1.5, the Stakes artifact enumerates the concrete stakes of the story. At least one stake shall be measurable, and at least one shall be irreversible (`reversible: false`). Vague or generic stakes are forbidden; every stake shall carry a typed category and a quantity.

---

# Canonical Schema

```json
{
  "$schema": "https://json-schema.org/draft/2020-12/schema",
  "$id": "https://schemas.insynergy.co/cttp/v2.0/story/stakes.schema.json",
  "title": "Stakes",
  "description": "Concrete, typed stakes with measurability and reversibility. Owner 2.1.5.",
  "type": "object",
  "allOf": [
    { "$ref": "https://schemas.insynergy.co/cttp/v2.0/common/defs.schema.json" }
  ],
  "properties": {
    "schema_version": { "$ref": "https://schemas.insynergy.co/cttp/v2.0/common/defs.schema.json#/$defs/SchemaVersion" },
    "build_id": { "$ref": "https://schemas.insynergy.co/cttp/v2.0/common/defs.schema.json#/$defs/BuildId" },
    "generated_at": { "$ref": "https://schemas.insynergy.co/cttp/v2.0/common/defs.schema.json#/$defs/Iso8601" },
    "content_hash": { "$ref": "https://schemas.insynergy.co/cttp/v2.0/common/defs.schema.json#/$defs/ContentHash" },
    "stakes": {
      "type": "array",
      "minItems": 1,
      "items": {
        "type": "object",
        "additionalProperties": false,
        "properties": {
          "stake_type": {
            "type": "string",
            "enum": [
              "financial_loss",
              "legal_exposure",
              "operational_failure",
              "reputational_damage",
              "institutional_collapse"
            ]
          },
          "measurable": { "type": "boolean" },
          "quantity": { "type": "string", "minLength": 1 },
          "reversible": { "type": "boolean" }
        },
        "required": ["stake_type", "measurable", "quantity", "reversible"]
      }
    }
  },
  "required": [
    "schema_version",
    "build_id",
    "generated_at",
    "content_hash",
    "stakes"
  ],
  "unevaluatedProperties": false
}
```

---

# Field Reference

| Field | Type | Required | Meaning | Constraint |
|---|---|---|---|---|
| `schema_version` | SchemaVersion | Yes | Envelope | From common defs |
| `build_id` | BuildId | Yes | Envelope | From common defs |
| `generated_at` | Iso8601 | Yes | Envelope | From common defs |
| `content_hash` | ContentHash | Yes | Envelope | From common defs |
| `stakes` | array[Stake] | Yes | Enumerated stakes | `minItems: 1` |
| `stakes[].stake_type` | enum | Yes | Category of stake | See enum |
| `stakes[].measurable` | boolean | Yes | Whether measurable | ≥1 must be `true` |
| `stakes[].quantity` | string | Yes | Concrete quantity | Non-empty; no vague terms |
| `stakes[].reversible` | boolean | Yes | Whether reversible | ≥1 must be `false` |

---

# Constraints & Invariants

- **INV-9.3.8-A** — At least one stake shall have `measurable: true` (Owner 2.1.5).
- **INV-9.3.8-B** — At least one stake shall have `reversible: false` (irreversible) (Owner 2.1.5).
- **INV-9.3.8-C** — `stake_type` shall be one of `financial_loss`, `legal_exposure`, `operational_failure`, `reputational_damage`, `institutional_collapse` (verbatim enum).
- **INV-9.3.8-D** — Vague or generic stakes are forbidden; `quantity` shall be concrete and non-empty.

---

# Example

```json
{
  "schema_version": "2.0.0",
  "build_id": "bld_20260720_0001",
  "generated_at": "2026-07-20T09:14:12Z",
  "content_hash": "sha256:8c1e4a9d2b706f35c0a9b1e7f4d6c3a2b8e1f0d9c5a7b4e3d2f1a0c9b8e7d6c4",
  "stakes": [
    { "stake_type": "financial_loss", "measurable": true, "quantity": "$40M merger write-down", "reversible": true },
    { "stake_type": "institutional_collapse", "measurable": false, "quantity": "Loss of the committee's chartered authority", "reversible": false }
  ]
}
```

---

# Acceptance Criteria

- Validates against `stakes.schema.json` under draft 2020-12.
- At least one measurable stake and at least one irreversible stake.
- All `stake_type` values are within the enum; no empty quantities.

---

# 9.3.9 Time Pressure (`time-pressure.json`)

**Artifact: Sealed Story artifact**
**Owner: 2.1.5**
**Immutable · Deterministic**

---

# Purpose

Per Owner 2.1.5, the Time Pressure artifact defines the countdown deadline that drives the narrative to its climax. The deadline shall be irreversible at expiry and perceivable by the audience.

---

# Canonical Schema

```json
{
  "$schema": "https://json-schema.org/draft/2020-12/schema",
  "$id": "https://schemas.insynergy.co/cttp/v2.0/story/time-pressure.schema.json",
  "title": "TimePressure",
  "description": "Countdown deadline, irreversible at expiry and audience-visible. Owner 2.1.5.",
  "type": "object",
  "allOf": [
    { "$ref": "https://schemas.insynergy.co/cttp/v2.0/common/defs.schema.json" }
  ],
  "properties": {
    "schema_version": { "$ref": "https://schemas.insynergy.co/cttp/v2.0/common/defs.schema.json#/$defs/SchemaVersion" },
    "build_id": { "$ref": "https://schemas.insynergy.co/cttp/v2.0/common/defs.schema.json#/$defs/BuildId" },
    "generated_at": { "$ref": "https://schemas.insynergy.co/cttp/v2.0/common/defs.schema.json#/$defs/Iso8601" },
    "content_hash": { "$ref": "https://schemas.insynergy.co/cttp/v2.0/common/defs.schema.json#/$defs/ContentHash" },
    "type": { "type": "string", "const": "countdown" },
    "duration_seconds": { "$ref": "https://schemas.insynergy.co/cttp/v2.0/common/defs.schema.json#/$defs/DurationSeconds" },
    "irreversible_at_expiry": { "type": "boolean", "const": true },
    "visible_to_audience": { "type": "boolean", "const": true }
  },
  "required": [
    "schema_version",
    "build_id",
    "generated_at",
    "content_hash",
    "type",
    "duration_seconds",
    "irreversible_at_expiry",
    "visible_to_audience"
  ],
  "unevaluatedProperties": false
}
```

---

# Field Reference

| Field | Type | Required | Meaning | Constraint |
|---|---|---|---|---|
| `schema_version` | SchemaVersion | Yes | Envelope | From common defs |
| `build_id` | BuildId | Yes | Envelope | From common defs |
| `generated_at` | Iso8601 | Yes | Envelope | From common defs |
| `content_hash` | ContentHash | Yes | Envelope | From common defs |
| `type` | string | Yes | Pressure mechanism | `const: "countdown"` |
| `duration_seconds` | DurationSeconds | Yes | Countdown duration | e.g. `31` |
| `irreversible_at_expiry` | boolean | Yes | Irreversible at expiry | `const: true` |
| `visible_to_audience` | boolean | Yes | Audience-perceivable | `const: true` |

---

# Constraints & Invariants

- **INV-9.3.9-A** — `type` shall be `countdown` (Owner 2.1.5).
- **INV-9.3.9-B** — `irreversible_at_expiry` shall be `true`: the deadline shall be irreversible at expiry.
- **INV-9.3.9-C** — `visible_to_audience` shall be `true`: the countdown shall be perceivable by the audience.
- **INV-9.3.9-D** — The deadline shall escalate toward the climax; `duration_seconds` shall be a positive value per the DurationSeconds definition.

---

# Example

```json
{
  "schema_version": "2.0.0",
  "build_id": "bld_20260720_0001",
  "generated_at": "2026-07-20T09:14:13Z",
  "content_hash": "sha256:3b1d4a9c2e806f75c0a1b9e7f4d6c3a2b8e1f0d9c5a7b4e3d2f1a0c9b8e7d6c3",
  "type": "countdown",
  "duration_seconds": 31,
  "irreversible_at_expiry": true,
  "visible_to_audience": true
}
```

---

# Acceptance Criteria

- Validates against `time-pressure.schema.json` under draft 2020-12.
- `type == "countdown"`; both booleans `true`; positive duration.

# 9.3.10 Story Arc (`story-arc.json`)

**Artifact: Sealed Story artifact**
**Owner: 2.1.6**
**Immutable · Deterministic**

---

# Purpose

Per Owner 2.1.6, the Story Arc artifact records the six ordered narrative stages: Normal World, Incident, Escalation, Crisis, Decision, Resolution. None of the six stages shall be omitted, and each stage maps to one or more dramatic elements.

---

# Canonical Schema

```json
{
  "$schema": "https://json-schema.org/draft/2020-12/schema",
  "$id": "https://schemas.insynergy.co/cttp/v2.0/story/story-arc.schema.json",
  "title": "StoryArc",
  "description": "Six-stage ordered story arc, no stage omitted. Owner 2.1.6.",
  "type": "object",
  "allOf": [
    { "$ref": "https://schemas.insynergy.co/cttp/v2.0/common/defs.schema.json" }
  ],
  "properties": {
    "schema_version": { "$ref": "https://schemas.insynergy.co/cttp/v2.0/common/defs.schema.json#/$defs/SchemaVersion" },
    "build_id": { "$ref": "https://schemas.insynergy.co/cttp/v2.0/common/defs.schema.json#/$defs/BuildId" },
    "generated_at": { "$ref": "https://schemas.insynergy.co/cttp/v2.0/common/defs.schema.json#/$defs/Iso8601" },
    "content_hash": { "$ref": "https://schemas.insynergy.co/cttp/v2.0/common/defs.schema.json#/$defs/ContentHash" },
    "stages": {
      "type": "array",
      "minItems": 6,
      "maxItems": 6,
      "items": {
        "type": "object",
        "additionalProperties": false,
        "properties": {
          "name": {
            "type": "string",
            "enum": ["Normal World", "Incident", "Escalation", "Crisis", "Decision", "Resolution"]
          },
          "maps_to": {
            "type": "array",
            "minItems": 1,
            "items": { "$ref": "https://schemas.insynergy.co/cttp/v2.0/common/defs.schema.json#/$defs/RefId" }
          }
        },
        "required": ["name", "maps_to"]
      }
    }
  },
  "required": [
    "schema_version",
    "build_id",
    "generated_at",
    "content_hash",
    "stages"
  ],
  "unevaluatedProperties": false
}
```

---

# Field Reference

| Field | Type | Required | Meaning | Constraint |
|---|---|---|---|---|
| `schema_version` | SchemaVersion | Yes | Envelope | From common defs |
| `build_id` | BuildId | Yes | Envelope | From common defs |
| `generated_at` | Iso8601 | Yes | Envelope | From common defs |
| `content_hash` | ContentHash | Yes | Envelope | From common defs |
