| `stages` | array[Stage] | Yes | The six ordered stages | Exactly 6 |
| `stages[].name` | enum | Yes | Stage name | Six verbatim values, in order |
| `stages[].maps_to` | array[RefId] | Yes | Dramatic element references | `minItems: 1` |

---

# Constraints & Invariants

- **INV-9.3.10-A** — `stages` shall contain exactly six entries; none of the six stages shall be omitted (Owner 2.1.6).
- **INV-9.3.10-B** — The stages shall appear in the fixed order: `Normal World`, `Incident`, `Escalation`, `Crisis`, `Decision`, `Resolution`.
- **INV-9.3.10-C** — Each stage shall map to at least one dramatic element via `maps_to`.

---

# Example

```json
{
  "schema_version": "2.0.0",
  "build_id": "bld_20260720_0001",
  "generated_at": "2026-07-20T09:14:14Z",
  "content_hash": "sha256:0e1d4a9c2b806f35c7a1b9e0f4d6c3a2b8e1f0d9c5a7b4e3d2f1a0c9b8e7d6c2",
  "stages": [
    { "name": "Normal World", "maps_to": ["clm-002"] },
    { "name": "Incident", "maps_to": ["clm-001"] },
    { "name": "Escalation", "maps_to": ["clm-003"] },
    { "name": "Crisis", "maps_to": ["clm-001"] },
    { "name": "Decision", "maps_to": ["clm-003"] },
    { "name": "Resolution", "maps_to": ["clm-003"] }
  ]
}
```

---

# Acceptance Criteria

- Validates against `story-arc.schema.json` under draft 2020-12.
- Exactly six stages in the mandated order; each maps to at least one element.

---

# 9.3.11 Three-Act Structure (`three-act-structure.json`)

**Artifact: Sealed Story artifact**
**Owner: 2.1.6**
**Immutable · Deterministic**

---

# Purpose

Per Owner 2.1.6, the Three-Act Structure artifact defines the three acts — each with an objective, emotional state, turning point, and duration — and the act budget. The act ratios (0.25 / 0.50 / 0.25) shall sum to 1.

---

# Canonical Schema

```json
{
  "$schema": "https://json-schema.org/draft/2020-12/schema",
  "$id": "https://schemas.insynergy.co/cttp/v2.0/story/three-act-structure.schema.json",
  "title": "ThreeActStructure",
  "description": "Three acts with objectives, emotional states, turning points, and act budget. Owner 2.1.6.",
  "type": "object",
  "allOf": [
    { "$ref": "https://schemas.insynergy.co/cttp/v2.0/common/defs.schema.json" }
  ],
  "$defs": {
    "ActBlock": {
      "type": "object",
      "additionalProperties": false,
      "properties": {
        "objective": { "type": "string", "minLength": 1 },
        "emotional_state": { "type": "string", "minLength": 1 },
        "turning_point": { "type": "string", "minLength": 1 },
        "duration_seconds": { "$ref": "https://schemas.insynergy.co/cttp/v2.0/common/defs.schema.json#/$defs/DurationSeconds" }
      },
      "required": ["objective", "emotional_state", "turning_point", "duration_seconds"]
    }
  },
  "properties": {
    "schema_version": { "$ref": "https://schemas.insynergy.co/cttp/v2.0/common/defs.schema.json#/$defs/SchemaVersion" },
    "build_id": { "$ref": "https://schemas.insynergy.co/cttp/v2.0/common/defs.schema.json#/$defs/BuildId" },
    "generated_at": { "$ref": "https://schemas.insynergy.co/cttp/v2.0/common/defs.schema.json#/$defs/Iso8601" },
    "content_hash": { "$ref": "https://schemas.insynergy.co/cttp/v2.0/common/defs.schema.json#/$defs/ContentHash" },
    "act_1": { "$ref": "#/$defs/ActBlock" },
    "act_2": { "$ref": "#/$defs/ActBlock" },
    "act_3": { "$ref": "#/$defs/ActBlock" },
    "act_budget": {
      "type": "object",
      "additionalProperties": false,
      "properties": {
        "total_duration_seconds": { "$ref": "https://schemas.insynergy.co/cttp/v2.0/common/defs.schema.json#/$defs/DurationSeconds" },
        "act_1_ratio": { "allOf": [ { "$ref": "https://schemas.insynergy.co/cttp/v2.0/common/defs.schema.json#/$defs/Ratio" } ], "const": 0.25 },
        "act_2_ratio": { "allOf": [ { "$ref": "https://schemas.insynergy.co/cttp/v2.0/common/defs.schema.json#/$defs/Ratio" } ], "const": 0.50 },
        "act_3_ratio": { "allOf": [ { "$ref": "https://schemas.insynergy.co/cttp/v2.0/common/defs.schema.json#/$defs/Ratio" } ], "const": 0.25 }
      },
      "required": ["total_duration_seconds", "act_1_ratio", "act_2_ratio", "act_3_ratio"]
    }
  },
  "required": [
    "schema_version",
    "build_id",
    "generated_at",
    "content_hash",
    "act_1",
    "act_2",
    "act_3",
    "act_budget"
  ],
  "unevaluatedProperties": false
}
```

---

# Field Reference

| Field | Type | Required | Meaning | Constraint |
|---|---|---|---|---|
| `schema_version` | SchemaVersion | Yes | Envelope | From common defs |
| `build_id` | BuildId | Yes | Envelope | From common defs |
| `generated_at` | Iso8601 | Yes | Envelope | From common defs |
| `content_hash` | ContentHash | Yes | Envelope | From common defs |
| `act_1` / `act_2` / `act_3` | ActBlock | Yes | Per-act definition | See ActBlock |
| `act_*.objective` | string | Yes | Act objective | Non-empty |
| `act_*.emotional_state` | string | Yes | Dominant emotional state | Non-empty |
| `act_*.turning_point` | string | Yes | Act turning point | Non-empty |
| `act_*.duration_seconds` | DurationSeconds | Yes | Act duration | From common defs |
| `act_budget.total_duration_seconds` | DurationSeconds | Yes | Total runtime | From common defs |
| `act_budget.act_1_ratio` | Ratio | Yes | Act 1 share | `const: 0.25` |
| `act_budget.act_2_ratio` | Ratio | Yes | Act 2 share | `const: 0.50` |
| `act_budget.act_3_ratio` | Ratio | Yes | Act 3 share | `const: 0.25` |

---

# Constraints & Invariants

- **INV-9.3.11-A** — `act_1_ratio + act_2_ratio + act_3_ratio` shall equal `1.0` (0.25 + 0.50 + 0.25) (Owner 2.1.6).
- **INV-9.3.11-B** — Each act shall define all four fields: `objective`, `emotional_state`, `turning_point`, `duration_seconds`.
- **INV-9.3.11-C** — The sum of per-act `duration_seconds` shall equal `act_budget.total_duration_seconds`, apportioned by the fixed ratios.

---

# Example

```json
{
  "schema_version": "2.0.0",
  "build_id": "bld_20260720_0001",
  "generated_at": "2026-07-20T09:14:15Z",
  "content_hash": "sha256:5c1d4a9e2b806f35c0a1b9e7f4d6c3a2b8e1f0d9c5a7b4e3d2f1a0c9b8e7d6c1",
  "act_1": {
    "objective": "Establish the chair and the fast-track norm.",
    "emotional_state": "Control",
    "turning_point": "She finds the skipped review.",
    "duration_seconds": 30
  },
  "act_2": {
    "objective": "Escalate the pressure to approve.",
    "emotional_state": "Understanding",
    "turning_point": "The board threatens censure.",
    "duration_seconds": 60
  },
  "act_3": {
    "objective": "Resolve the decision.",
    "emotional_state": "Institutional Design",
    "turning_point": "She halts the vote.",
    "duration_seconds": 30
  },
  "act_budget": {
    "total_duration_seconds": 120,
    "act_1_ratio": 0.25,
    "act_2_ratio": 0.50,
    "act_3_ratio": 0.25
  }
}
```

---

# Acceptance Criteria

- Validates against `three-act-structure.schema.json` under draft 2020-12.
- Ratios equal 0.25 / 0.50 / 0.25 and sum to 1.0.
- Per-act durations sum to the total budget.

---

# 9.3.12 Emotional Arc (`emotional-arc.json`)

**Artifact: Sealed Story artifact**
**Owner: 2.1.6**
**Immutable · Deterministic**

---

# Purpose

Per Owner 2.1.6, the Emotional Arc artifact records the ordered emotional-state transitions and the continuity rules that govern them: each transition shall advance by at most one stage, the progression shall be monotonic toward the decision, and every transition shall be motivated by an event.

---

# Canonical Schema

```json
{
  "$schema": "https://json-schema.org/draft/2020-12/schema",
  "$id": "https://schemas.insynergy.co/cttp/v2.0/story/emotional-arc.schema.json",
  "title": "EmotionalArc",
  "description": "Ordered emotional transitions with continuity rules. Owner 2.1.6.",
  "type": "object",
  "allOf": [
    { "$ref": "https://schemas.insynergy.co/cttp/v2.0/common/defs.schema.json" }
  ],
  "properties": {
    "schema_version": { "$ref": "https://schemas.insynergy.co/cttp/v2.0/common/defs.schema.json#/$defs/SchemaVersion" },
    "build_id": { "$ref": "https://schemas.insynergy.co/cttp/v2.0/common/defs.schema.json#/$defs/BuildId" },
    "generated_at": { "$ref": "https://schemas.insynergy.co/cttp/v2.0/common/defs.schema.json#/$defs/Iso8601" },
    "content_hash": { "$ref": "https://schemas.insynergy.co/cttp/v2.0/common/defs.schema.json#/$defs/ContentHash" },
    "transitions": {
      "type": "array",
      "minItems": 1,
      "items": {
        "type": "object",
        "additionalProperties": false,
        "properties": {
          "from": { "type": "string", "minLength": 1 },
          "to": { "type": "string", "minLength": 1 },
          "motivated_by": { "type": "string", "minLength": 1 }
        },
        "required": ["from", "to", "motivated_by"]
      }
    },
    "max_stage_jump": { "type": "integer", "const": 1 },
    "monotonic_toward_decision": { "type": "boolean", "const": true },
    "motivated_by_event": { "type": "boolean", "const": true }
  },
  "required": [
    "schema_version",
    "build_id",
    "generated_at",
    "content_hash",
    "transitions",
    "max_stage_jump",
    "monotonic_toward_decision",
    "motivated_by_event"
  ],
  "unevaluatedProperties": false
}
```

---

# Field Reference

| Field | Type | Required | Meaning | Constraint |
|---|---|---|---|---|
| `schema_version` | SchemaVersion | Yes | Envelope | From common defs |
| `build_id` | BuildId | Yes | Envelope | From common defs |
| `generated_at` | Iso8601 | Yes | Envelope | From common defs |
| `content_hash` | ContentHash | Yes | Envelope | From common defs |
| `transitions` | array[Transition] | Yes | Ordered emotional transitions | `minItems: 1` |
| `transitions[].from` | string | Yes | Source emotional state | Non-empty |
| `transitions[].to` | string | Yes | Target emotional state | Non-empty |
| `transitions[].motivated_by` | string | Yes | Motivating event | Non-empty |
| `max_stage_jump` | integer | Yes | Max stage advance per transition | `const: 1` |
| `monotonic_toward_decision` | boolean | Yes | Monotonic toward decision | `const: true` |
| `motivated_by_event` | boolean | Yes | Every transition event-motivated | `const: true` |

---

# Constraints & Invariants

- **INV-9.3.12-A** — `max_stage_jump` shall equal `1`: no transition shall skip an intermediate emotional stage (Owner 2.1.6).
- **INV-9.3.12-B** — `monotonic_toward_decision` shall be `true`: the progression shall not regress away from the decision.
- **INV-9.3.12-C** — `motivated_by_event` shall be `true`, and every transition shall carry a non-empty `motivated_by`.
- **INV-9.3.12-D** — The transitions shall be consistent with the protagonist `arc` in the Character Bible (9.3.6).

---

# Example

```json
{
  "schema_version": "2.0.0",
  "build_id": "bld_20260720_0001",
  "generated_at": "2026-07-20T09:14:16Z",
  "content_hash": "sha256:7c1d4a9e2b806f35c0a1b9e7f4d6c3a2b8e1f0d9c5a7b4e3d2f1a0c9b8e7d6c0",
  "transitions": [
    { "from": "Control", "to": "Understanding", "motivated_by": "Discovery of the skipped review" },
    { "from": "Understanding", "to": "Institutional Design", "motivated_by": "Halting the vote" }
  ],
  "max_stage_jump": 1,
  "monotonic_toward_decision": true,
  "motivated_by_event": true
}
```

---

# Acceptance Criteria

- Validates against `emotional-arc.schema.json` under draft 2020-12.
- `max_stage_jump == 1`; both continuity booleans `true`.
- Every transition has a non-empty motivating event.

---

# 9.3.13 Concept Placement (`concept-placement.json`)

**Artifact: Sealed Story artifact**
**Owner: 2.1.6**
**Immutable · Deterministic**

---

# Purpose

Per Owner 2.1.6, the Concept Placement artifact constrains where and how the concept may appear. The concept shall be the answer to the dramatic question, never the opening. It shall not appear before Act 2, shall require prior tension, and shall occupy at most 20% of the runtime.

---

# Canonical Schema

```json
{
  "$schema": "https://json-schema.org/draft/2020-12/schema",
  "$id": "https://schemas.insynergy.co/cttp/v2.0/story/concept-placement.schema.json",
  "title": "ConceptPlacement",
  "description": "Constraints on concept placement: concept as answer, not opening. Owner 2.1.6.",
  "type": "object",
  "allOf": [
    { "$ref": "https://schemas.insynergy.co/cttp/v2.0/common/defs.schema.json" }
  ],
  "properties": {
    "schema_version": { "$ref": "https://schemas.insynergy.co/cttp/v2.0/common/defs.schema.json#/$defs/SchemaVersion" },
    "build_id": { "$ref": "https://schemas.insynergy.co/cttp/v2.0/common/defs.schema.json#/$defs/BuildId" },
    "generated_at": { "$ref": "https://schemas.insynergy.co/cttp/v2.0/common/defs.schema.json#/$defs/Iso8601" },
    "content_hash": { "$ref": "https://schemas.insynergy.co/cttp/v2.0/common/defs.schema.json#/$defs/ContentHash" },
    "earliest_allowed_act": {
      "allOf": [ { "$ref": "https://schemas.insynergy.co/cttp/v2.0/common/defs.schema.json#/$defs/Act" } ],
      "minimum": 2
    },
    "requires_prior_tension": { "type": "boolean", "const": true },
    "max_concept_ratio": {
      "allOf": [ { "$ref": "https://schemas.insynergy.co/cttp/v2.0/common/defs.schema.json#/$defs/Ratio" } ],
      "const": 0.20
    },
    "concept_as_answer": { "type": "boolean", "const": true }
  },
  "required": [
    "schema_version",
    "build_id",
    "generated_at",
    "content_hash",
    "earliest_allowed_act",
    "requires_prior_tension",
    "max_concept_ratio",
    "concept_as_answer"
  ],
  "unevaluatedProperties": false
}
```

---

# Field Reference

| Field | Type | Required | Meaning | Constraint |
|---|---|---|---|---|
| `schema_version` | SchemaVersion | Yes | Envelope | From common defs |
| `build_id` | BuildId | Yes | Envelope | From common defs |
| `generated_at` | Iso8601 | Yes | Envelope | From common defs |
| `content_hash` | ContentHash | Yes | Envelope | From common defs |
| `earliest_allowed_act` | Act | Yes | Earliest act the concept may appear | `minimum: 2` |
| `requires_prior_tension` | boolean | Yes | Concept requires prior tension | `const: true` |
| `max_concept_ratio` | Ratio | Yes | Max share of runtime | `const: 0.20` |
| `concept_as_answer` | boolean | Yes | Concept is the answer | `const: true` |

---

# Constraints & Invariants

- **INV-9.3.13-A** — `earliest_allowed_act` shall be no earlier than Act 2 (`minimum: 2`); the concept shall never open the story (Owner 2.1.6).
- **INV-9.3.13-B** — `requires_prior_tension` shall be `true`: dramatic tension shall precede any concept exposition.
- **INV-9.3.13-C** — `max_concept_ratio` shall equal `0.20`: the concept shall occupy at most 20% of the runtime.
- **INV-9.3.13-D** — `concept_as_answer` shall be `true`: the concept shall be the answer to the dramatic question (9.3.3).

---

# Example

```json
{
  "schema_version": "2.0.0",
  "build_id": "bld_20260720_0001",
  "generated_at": "2026-07-20T09:14:17Z",
  "content_hash": "sha256:9c1d4a2e2b806f35c0a1b9e7f4d6c3a2b8e1f0d9c5a7b4e3d2f1a0c9b8e7d6cf",
  "earliest_allowed_act": 2,
  "requires_prior_tension": true,
  "max_concept_ratio": 0.20,
  "concept_as_answer": true
}
```

---

# Acceptance Criteria

- Validates against `concept-placement.schema.json` under draft 2020-12.
- `earliest_allowed_act >= 2`; `max_concept_ratio == 0.20`.
- `requires_prior_tension` and `concept_as_answer` are both `true`.

---

# 9.3.14 Story Quality Report (`story-quality-report.json`)

**Artifact: Sealed Story artifact**
**Owner: 2.1.7**
**Immutable · Deterministic**

---

# Purpose

Per Owner 2.1.7, the Story Quality Report is the mandatory, all-or-nothing story gate. Every gate boolean shall be `true` for the story to pass; any `false` blocks rendering. The report also records failed gate items, any forbidden category detected, and a recommended action. The report is immutable.

---

# Canonical Schema

```json
{
  "$schema": "https://json-schema.org/draft/2020-12/schema",
  "$id": "https://schemas.insynergy.co/cttp/v2.0/story/story-quality-report.schema.json",
  "title": "StoryQualityReport",
  "description": "Mandatory all-or-nothing story gate report. Owner 2.1.7.",
  "type": "object",
  "allOf": [
    { "$ref": "https://schemas.insynergy.co/cttp/v2.0/common/defs.schema.json" }
  ],
  "properties": {
    "schema_version": { "$ref": "https://schemas.insynergy.co/cttp/v2.0/common/defs.schema.json#/$defs/SchemaVersion" },
    "build_id": { "$ref": "https://schemas.insynergy.co/cttp/v2.0/common/defs.schema.json#/$defs/BuildId" },
    "generated_at": { "$ref": "https://schemas.insynergy.co/cttp/v2.0/common/defs.schema.json#/$defs/Iso8601" },
    "content_hash": { "$ref": "https://schemas.insynergy.co/cttp/v2.0/common/defs.schema.json#/$defs/ContentHash" },
    "passed": { "type": "boolean" },
    "failed_gate_items": {
      "type": "array",
      "items": { "type": "string", "minLength": 1 }
    },
    "forbidden_category": {
      "type": ["string", "null"],
      "enum": [
        "article_summary",
        "educational_lecture",
        "concept_list",
        "talking_heads",
        "slideshow_narrative",
        "narrator_only",
        "decision_less",
        null
      ]
    },
    "recommended_action": { "type": "string", "minLength": 1 },
    "gate": {
      "type": "object",
      "additionalProperties": false,
      "properties": {
        "protagonist_exists": { "type": "boolean" },
        "goal_exists": { "type": "boolean" },
        "conflict_exists": { "type": "boolean" },
        "stakes_exist": { "type": "boolean" },
        "time_pressure_exists": { "type": "boolean" },
        "decision_exists": { "type": "boolean" },
        "resolution_exists": { "type": "boolean" }
      },
      "required": [
        "protagonist_exists",
        "goal_exists",
        "conflict_exists",
        "stakes_exist",
        "time_pressure_exists",
        "decision_exists",
        "resolution_exists"
      ]
    }
  },
  "required": [
    "schema_version",
    "build_id",
    "generated_at",
    "content_hash",
    "passed",
    "failed_gate_items",
    "forbidden_category",
    "recommended_action",
    "gate"
  ],
  "unevaluatedProperties": false
}
```

---

# Field Reference

| Field | Type | Required | Meaning | Constraint |
|---|---|---|---|---|
| `schema_version` | SchemaVersion | Yes | Envelope | From common defs |
| `build_id` | BuildId | Yes | Envelope | From common defs |
| `generated_at` | Iso8601 | Yes | Envelope | From common defs |
| `content_hash` | ContentHash | Yes | Envelope | From common defs |
| `passed` | boolean | Yes | Overall gate result | `true` only if all gate booleans `true` |
| `failed_gate_items` | array[string] | Yes | Names of failed items | Empty if `passed` |
| `forbidden_category` | string \| null | Yes | Detected forbidden category | Enum or `null` |
| `recommended_action` | string | Yes | Remediation guidance | Non-empty |
| `gate.protagonist_exists` | boolean | Yes | Protagonist present | Must be `true` to pass |
| `gate.goal_exists` | boolean | Yes | Goal present | Must be `true` to pass |
| `gate.conflict_exists` | boolean | Yes | Conflict present | Must be `true` to pass |
| `gate.stakes_exist` | boolean | Yes | Stakes present | Must be `true` to pass |
| `gate.time_pressure_exists` | boolean | Yes | Time pressure present | Must be `true` to pass |
| `gate.decision_exists` | boolean | Yes | Decision present | Must be `true` to pass |
| `gate.resolution_exists` | boolean | Yes | Resolution present | Must be `true` to pass |

---

# Constraints & Invariants

- **INV-9.3.14-A** — The gate is all-or-nothing: `passed` shall be `true` if and only if all seven `gate` booleans are `true` (Owner 2.1.7). Any `false` blocks rendering.
- **INV-9.3.14-B** — When `passed` is `false`, `failed_gate_items` shall enumerate the failing item names; when `passed` is `true`, `failed_gate_items` shall be empty.
- **INV-9.3.14-C** — `forbidden_category`, when non-null, shall be one of `article_summary`, `educational_lecture`, `concept_list`, `talking_heads`, `slideshow_narrative`, `narrator_only`, `decision_less` (verbatim enum). A non-null forbidden category shall force `passed: false`.
- **INV-9.3.14-D** — The report shall be immutable (Owner 2.1.7).

---

# Example

```json
{
  "schema_version": "2.0.0",
  "build_id": "bld_20260720_0001",
  "generated_at": "2026-07-20T09:14:18Z",
  "content_hash": "sha256:1a2d4a9e2b806f35c0a1b9e7f4d6c3a2b8e1f0d9c5a7b4e3d2f1a0c9b8e7d6ce",
  "passed": true,
  "failed_gate_items": [],
  "forbidden_category": null,
  "recommended_action": "Proceed to Screenplay Engine.",
  "gate": {
    "protagonist_exists": true,
    "goal_exists": true,
    "conflict_exists": true,
    "stakes_exist": true,
    "time_pressure_exists": true,
    "decision_exists": true,
    "resolution_exists": true
  }
}
```

---

# Acceptance Criteria

- Validates against `story-quality-report.schema.json` under draft 2020-12.
- `passed` is consistent with the seven gate booleans (all-or-nothing).
- `forbidden_category` is null or a verbatim enum value; `failed_gate_items` consistent with `passed`.

---

# 9.3.15 Story Metrics (`story-metrics`)

**Artifact: Embedded object (component of a sealed parent)**
**Owner: 2.1.7**
**Immutable · Deterministic**

---

# Purpose

Per Owner 2.1.7, the Story Metrics block records the deterministic scores used to evaluate story quality. It is an embedded object — a component of a sealed parent artifact — and therefore does not carry the full `ArtifactEnvelope`. Each score is derived deterministically from the story artifacts.

---

# Canonical Schema

```json
{
  "$schema": "https://json-schema.org/draft/2020-12/schema",
  "$id": "https://schemas.insynergy.co/cttp/v2.0/story/story-metrics.schema.json",
  "title": "StoryMetrics",
  "description": "Embedded deterministic story-quality metrics block. Owner 2.1.7.",
  "type": "object",
  "additionalProperties": false,
  "properties": {
    "dramatic_score": { "$ref": "https://schemas.insynergy.co/cttp/v2.0/common/defs.schema.json#/$defs/Score" },
    "conflict_score": { "$ref": "https://schemas.insynergy.co/cttp/v2.0/common/defs.schema.json#/$defs/Score" },
    "stakes_score": { "$ref": "https://schemas.insynergy.co/cttp/v2.0/common/defs.schema.json#/$defs/Score" },
    "emotional_progression": { "$ref": "https://schemas.insynergy.co/cttp/v2.0/common/defs.schema.json#/$defs/Score" },
    "concept_ratio": { "$ref": "https://schemas.insynergy.co/cttp/v2.0/common/defs.schema.json#/$defs/Ratio" }
  },
  "required": [
    "dramatic_score",
    "conflict_score",
    "stakes_score",
    "emotional_progression",
    "concept_ratio"
  ]
}
```

---

# Field Reference

| Field | Type | Required | Meaning | Constraint |
|---|---|---|---|---|
| `dramatic_score` | Score | Yes | Dramatic quality score | Threshold ≥ 0.85 |
| `conflict_score` | Score | Yes | Conflict quality score | Threshold ≥ 0.80 |
| `stakes_score` | Score | Yes | Stakes quality score | Threshold ≥ 0.85 |
| `emotional_progression` | Score | Yes | Emotional progression score | Threshold ≥ 0.85 |
| `concept_ratio` | Ratio | Yes | Concept share of runtime | Threshold ≤ 0.20 |

---

# Constraints & Invariants

- **INV-9.3.15-A** — Passing thresholds (Owner 2.1.7): `dramatic_score >= 0.85`, `conflict_score >= 0.80`, `stakes_score >= 0.85`, `emotional_progression >= 0.85`, `concept_ratio <= 0.20`.
- **INV-9.3.15-B** — The overall `minimum_story_score` shall be `0.85`; a story failing any threshold shall not pass the gate (9.3.14).
- **INV-9.3.15-C** — All scores shall be derived deterministically from the story artifacts (Owner 2.1.7).
- **INV-9.3.15-D** — As an embedded component, this object does not carry the `ArtifactEnvelope`; its integrity is covered by the `content_hash` of its sealed parent.

---

# Example

```json
{
  "dramatic_score": 0.91,
  "conflict_score": 0.87,
  "stakes_score": 0.89,
  "emotional_progression": 0.90,
  "concept_ratio": 0.18
}
```

---

# Acceptance Criteria

- Validates against `story-metrics.schema.json` under draft 2020-12.
- All five metrics present; each within its Score/Ratio range.
- Values satisfy the passing thresholds for a story that is to pass the gate.

---

# 9.3.16 Story Cache Key (`story-cache-key`)

**Artifact: Embedded object (component of a sealed parent)**
**Owner: 2.1.8**
**Immutable · Deterministic**

---

# Purpose

Per Owner 2.1.8, the Story Cache Key descriptor records the deterministic cache key for the story and the components from which it is derived. The key is `sha256(article_hash + story_engine_version + story_profile)`. It is an embedded object and does not carry the full `ArtifactEnvelope`.

The cache shall be invalidated on any change to the article, the engine version, the profile, or the author style.

---

# Canonical Schema

```json
{
  "$schema": "https://json-schema.org/draft/2020-12/schema",
  "$id": "https://schemas.insynergy.co/cttp/v2.0/story/story-cache-key.schema.json",
  "title": "StoryCacheKey",
  "description": "Embedded deterministic story cache-key descriptor. Owner 2.1.8.",
  "type": "object",
  "additionalProperties": false,
  "properties": {
    "cache_key": { "$ref": "https://schemas.insynergy.co/cttp/v2.0/common/defs.schema.json#/$defs/CacheKey" },
    "components": {
      "type": "object",
      "additionalProperties": false,
      "properties": {
        "article_hash": { "$ref": "https://schemas.insynergy.co/cttp/v2.0/common/defs.schema.json#/$defs/ContentHash" },
        "story_engine_version": { "type": "string", "minLength": 1 },
        "story_profile": { "type": "string", "minLength": 1 }
      },
      "required": ["article_hash", "story_engine_version", "story_profile"]
    }
  },
  "required": ["cache_key", "components"]
}
```

---

# Field Reference

| Field | Type | Required | Meaning | Constraint |
|---|---|---|---|---|
| `cache_key` | CacheKey | Yes | Derived cache key | `sha256(article_hash + story_engine_version + story_profile)` |
| `components.article_hash` | ContentHash | Yes | Hash of the source article | From common defs |
| `components.story_engine_version` | string | Yes | Story Engine version | Non-empty |
| `components.story_profile` | string | Yes | Active story profile | Non-empty |

---

# Constraints & Invariants

- **INV-9.3.16-A** — `cache_key` shall equal `sha256(article_hash + story_engine_version + story_profile)` (Owner 2.1.8). The key is deterministic in these three components.
- **INV-9.3.16-B** — The cache shall be invalidated on any of: article change, engine version change, profile change, or author_style change (Owner 2.1.8).
- **INV-9.3.16-C** — As an embedded component, this object does not carry the `ArtifactEnvelope`.

---

# Example

```json
{
  "cache_key": "sha256:b3f1c9a7e2d05846c1b0a9e7f4d6c3a2b8e1f0d9c5a7b4e3d2f1a0c9b8e7d6c22",
  "components": {
    "article_hash": "sha256:4d2c9a1b7e0f35a8c6b1f0e93d7a2c4b8e1f6079a3d5c2b1e0f4a9c8d7b6e5f31",
    "story_engine_version": "2.0.0",
    "story_profile": "institutional_default"
  }
}
```

---

# Acceptance Criteria

- Validates against `story-cache-key.schema.json` under draft 2020-12.
- `cache_key` is a CacheKey derived from the three declared components.
- All three components present and non-empty.

---
# 9.4 Screenplay Engine Layer Schemas

**Insynergy Cinematic Thought Leadership Platform — Master Specification v2.0**
**Part 9 — JSON Schema / Appendix · Chapter 9.4 (Screenplay Engine Layer, Part 3)**

---

# Purpose

This chapter formalizes the immutable screenplay artifact set produced by the Screenplay Engine (Part 3). The screenplay is derived **only** from validated Story Artifacts (Part 2) and is exported in two faithful representations: **Fountain** (human-authored industry format) and **JSON** (machine-consumable). The JSON representation is consumed downstream by the Shot Planner (Part 4). The schemas below govern the JSON representation exclusively.

Every artifact in this layer is deterministic with respect to its Story Artifact inputs and the recorded configuration snapshot. Sealed artifacts compose the common `ArtifactEnvelope` and carry provenance, content hashing, and approval references.

---

# Design Philosophy

**One screenplay, two faithful representations, no custom syntax.** The Fountain export and the JSON export are lossless projections of a single canonical screenplay model. No proprietary markup, transition vocabulary, or structural extension is permitted in either representation. These schemas define the JSON projection. Fountain conformance is governed separately in Part 3; the two projections must agree.

---

# Schemas in This Chapter

- **9.4.1 `screenplay.json`** — the sealed full screenplay (envelope + acts + scenes).
- **9.4.2 `scene`** — the canonical scene object (embedded in the screenplay).
- **9.4.3 `scene-index.json`** — ordered, stable index over scenes.
- **9.4.4 `dialogue.json`** — the dialogue line set.
- **9.4.5 `continuity.json`** — continuity validation report.
- **9.4.6 `screenplay-metrics`** — embedded quantitative metrics.
- **9.4.7 `screenplay-config`** — layered, runtime-immutable configuration snapshot.
- **9.4.8 `screenplay-state`** — screenplay and per-scene lifecycle state.

---

# 9.4.1 Screenplay (`screenplay.json`)

**Sealed artifact · Owner: 3.1.7, 3.1.3**

---

# Purpose

The `screenplay.json` artifact is the sealed, immutable full screenplay. It composes the common `ArtifactEnvelope` and carries a screenplay body of exactly three acts and an ordered array of 8–12 scenes, each belonging to exactly one act. Scene entries conform to the Scene schema (9.4.2). The artifact is deterministic and its scene identifiers are stable across regeneration.

---

# Canonical Schema

```json
{
  "$schema": "https://json-schema.org/draft/2020-12/schema",
  "$id": "https://schemas.insynergy.co/cttp/v2.0/screenplay/screenplay.schema.json",
  "title": "Screenplay",
  "description": "Sealed full screenplay artifact. Owner: 3.1.7, 3.1.3.",
  "allOf": [
    { "$ref": "https://schemas.insynergy.co/cttp/v2.0/common/defs.schema.json#/$defs/ArtifactEnvelope" },
    {
      "type": "object",
      "properties": {
        "body": {
          "type": "object",
          "properties": {
            "title": { "type": "string" },
            "acts": {
              "type": "integer",
              "const": 3
            },
            "scenes": {
              "type": "array",
              "minItems": 8,
              "maxItems": 12,
              "items": {
                "$ref": "https://schemas.insynergy.co/cttp/v2.0/screenplay/scene.schema.json"
              }
            }
          },
          "required": ["acts", "scenes"],
          "additionalProperties": false
        }
      },
      "required": ["body"]
    }
  ],
  "unevaluatedProperties": false
}
```

---

# Field Reference

| Field | Type | Owner | Description |
|---|---|---|---|
| `body.title` | string | 3.1.7 | Optional screenplay title. |
| `body.acts` | integer (const 3) | 3.1.3 | Number of acts; always three. |
| `body.scenes` | array<Scene> | 3.1.3, 3.1.7 | Ordered scenes (8–12), each conforming to 9.4.2. |
| *(envelope)* | ArtifactEnvelope | common | SchemaVersion, BuildId, ContentHash, ApprovalRef, provenance. |

---

# Constraints & Invariants

- **INV-9.4.1-1** — `scene_count` (length of `body.scenes`) SHALL be in the inclusive range 8..12.
- **INV-9.4.1-2** — `body.acts` SHALL equal 3.
- **INV-9.4.1-3** — Scenes SHALL be ordered; array position defines narrative order and SHALL be stable across regeneration.
- **INV-9.4.1-4** — Each scene's `scene_id` SHALL be stable and unique within the screenplay.
- **INV-9.4.1-5** — Each scene SHALL belong to exactly one act, and act assignment across the ordered scenes SHALL be non-decreasing.
- **INV-9.4.1-6** — Generation SHALL be deterministic given identical Story Artifacts and configuration snapshot; the `ContentHash` SHALL reproduce.
- **INV-9.4.1-7** — The artifact is sealed: post-approval mutation is prohibited (`unevaluatedProperties: false`).

---

# Example

```json
{
  "schema_version": "2.0.0",
  "build_id": "bld_9f2c7a10",
  "content_hash": "sha256:4b1e...c9",
  "approval_ref": "apr_screenplay_0007",
  "created_at": "2026-07-18T09:14:02Z",
  "body": {
    "title": "The Countdown Ledger",
    "acts": 3,
    "scenes": [
      { "scene_id": "scn_0001", "act": "I", "heading": { "location": "Server Room", "time": "NIGHT", "interior": true }, "purpose": "Introduce protagonist", "characters": ["MAYA"], "objective": { "MAYA": "Prove the anomaly is real" }, "conflict": "Human vs Machine", "actions": ["Maya freezes as the dashboard flatlines."], "dialogue": [], "visual_subtext": "Isolation under fluorescent light", "duration_seconds": 7, "transition": "Hard Cut" }
    ]
  }
}
```

---

# Acceptance Criteria

- A conforming validator accepts screenplays with 8–12 ordered scenes and exactly three acts, and rejects any with fewer than 8 or more than 12 scenes.
- Regenerating from identical inputs yields an identical `content_hash`.
- Any scene entry failing 9.4.2 causes the screenplay to fail validation.
- Unknown top-level or body properties are rejected.

---

# 9.4.2 Scene (`scene.schema.json`)

**Embedded object · Owner: 3.1.3, 3.1.4, 3.1.7**

---

# Purpose

The canonical scene object. A scene carries exactly one dramatic purpose and exactly one dominant conflict, a heading, participating characters with per-character objectives, staged actions, dialogue lines, visual subtext, a bounded duration, and an outgoing transition. Scenes are embedded within `screenplay.json` (9.4.1) and referenced by the scene index (9.4.3).

---

# Canonical Schema

```json
{
  "$schema": "https://json-schema.org/draft/2020-12/schema",
  "$id": "https://schemas.insynergy.co/cttp/v2.0/screenplay/scene.schema.json",
  "title": "Scene",
  "description": "Canonical scene object. Owner: 3.1.3, 3.1.4, 3.1.7.",
  "type": "object",
  "properties": {
    "scene_id": { "$ref": "https://schemas.insynergy.co/cttp/v2.0/common/defs.schema.json#/$defs/SceneId" },
    "act": { "$ref": "https://schemas.insynergy.co/cttp/v2.0/common/defs.schema.json#/$defs/Act" },
    "heading": {
      "type": "object",
      "properties": {
        "location": { "type": "string", "minLength": 1 },
        "time": { "type": "string", "minLength": 1 },
        "interior": { "type": "boolean" }
      },
      "required": ["location", "time", "interior"],
      "additionalProperties": false
    },
    "purpose": {
      "type": "string",
      "enum": [
        "Introduce protagonist",
        "Reveal hidden risk",
        "Increase urgency",
        "Create reversal",
        "Force decision",
        "Resolve conflict"
      ]
    },
    "characters": {
      "type": "array",
      "items": { "type": "string", "minLength": 1 }
    },
    "objective": {
      "type": "object",
      "propertyNames": { "type": "string", "minLength": 1 },
      "additionalProperties": { "type": "string", "minLength": 1 }
    },
    "conflict": {
      "type": "string",
      "enum": [
        "Human vs Machine",
        "Human vs Institution",
        "Human vs Time",
        "Human vs Self",
        "Institution vs Reality"
      ]
    },
    "actions": {
      "type": "array",
      "items": { "type": "string", "minLength": 1 }
    },
    "dialogue": {
      "type": "array",
      "items": {
        "$ref": "https://schemas.insynergy.co/cttp/v2.0/screenplay/dialogue.schema.json#/$defs/DialogueLine"
      }
    },
    "visual_subtext": { "type": "string" },
    "duration_seconds": {
      "type": "integer",
      "minimum": 4,
      "maximum": 10
    },
    "transition": {
      "type": "string",
      "enum": ["Hard Cut", "Fade", "Match Cut", "L Cut", "J Cut"]
    }
  },
  "required": [
    "scene_id",
    "act",
    "heading",
    "purpose",
    "characters",
    "objective",
    "conflict",
    "actions",
    "dialogue",
    "visual_subtext",
    "duration_seconds",
    "transition"
  ],
  "additionalProperties": false
}
```

---

# Field Reference

| Field | Type | Owner | Description |
|---|---|---|---|
| `scene_id` | SceneId | 3.1.3 | Stable unique scene identifier. |
| `act` | Act | 3.1.3 | Act to which the scene belongs. |
| `heading.location` | string | 3.1.4 | Scene location. |
| `heading.time` | string | 3.1.4 | Time of day (e.g. NIGHT, DAY). |
| `heading.interior` | boolean | 3.1.4 | True → INT/INT.; false → EXT/EXT. |
| `purpose` | enum | 3.1.3 | Exactly one dramatic purpose. |
| `characters` | array<string> | 3.1.4 | Present characters. |
| `objective` | object map | 3.1.4 | Per-character objective string. |
| `conflict` | enum | 3.1.3 | Exactly one dominant conflict. |
| `actions` | array<string> | 3.1.4 | Staged action beats. |
| `dialogue` | array<DialogueLine> | 3.1.5 | Dialogue lines (see 9.4.4). |
| `visual_subtext` | string | 3.1.4 | Non-verbal meaning conveyed. |
| `duration_seconds` | integer 4..10 | 3.1.7 | Bounded scene duration. |
| `transition` | enum | 3.1.7 | Outgoing transition. |

---

# Constraints & Invariants

- **INV-9.4.2-1** — `purpose` SHALL take exactly one value from the allowed enumeration. The purposes **"Explain concept"**, **"Show architecture"**, and **"Describe framework"** are forbidden and SHALL NOT appear.
- **INV-9.4.2-2** — `conflict` SHALL identify exactly one dominant conflict from the allowed enumeration.
- **INV-9.4.2-3** — Heading interiority SHALL resolve to one of `INT`, `EXT`, `INT.`, `EXT.` in the Fountain projection; the JSON `interior` boolean is authoritative (`true` → interior).
- **INV-9.4.2-4** — `transition` SHALL be one of the allowed values. The transitions **Page Turn**, **Spin**, **Flash**, **Explosion Transition**, and **Swipe** are forbidden and SHALL NOT appear.
- **INV-9.4.2-5** — `duration_seconds` SHALL satisfy 4 ≤ d ≤ 10 with a target of 7. A value exceeding the maximum requires recorded justification and is otherwise rejected.
- **INV-9.4.2-6** — Every character listed in `characters` SHALL have a corresponding entry in the `objective` map.
- **INV-9.4.2-7** — Keys of `objective` SHOULD correspond to `characters` entries; an objective for an absent character is a continuity fault (see 9.4.5).

---

# Example

```json
{
  "scene_id": "scn_0004",
  "act": "II",
  "heading": { "location": "Boardroom", "time": "DAY", "interior": true },
  "purpose": "Force decision",
  "characters": ["MAYA", "DIRECTOR OKAFOR"],
  "objective": {
    "MAYA": "Compel a shutdown before the deadline",
    "DIRECTOR OKAFOR": "Protect the institution from liability"
  },
  "conflict": "Human vs Institution",
  "actions": ["Maya slides the ledger across the table.", "Okafor does not touch it."],
  "dialogue": [
    { "scene_id": "scn_0004", "character": "MAYA", "text": "Sign it or the clock decides.", "category": "Demand", "silence": false }
  ],
  "visual_subtext": "Authority weighed against evidence",
  "duration_seconds": 8,
  "transition": "Match Cut"
}
```

---

# Acceptance Criteria

- Scenes with a forbidden purpose or forbidden transition are rejected.
- A scene missing an objective for any listed character is rejected.
- `duration_seconds` outside 4..10 is rejected.
- Exactly one purpose and one conflict are present; unknown properties are rejected.

---

# 9.4.3 Scene Index (`scene-index.json`)

**Sealed artifact · Owner: 3.1.7**

---

# Purpose

An ordered, stable index over the screenplay's scenes. The index enables the Shot Planner and downstream consumers to iterate scenes in narrative order without parsing the full screenplay body. Each entry records the scene identifier, its act, a contiguous order position, and its purpose.

---

# Canonical Schema

```json
{
  "$schema": "https://json-schema.org/draft/2020-12/schema",
  "$id": "https://schemas.insynergy.co/cttp/v2.0/screenplay/scene-index.schema.json",
  "title": "SceneIndex",
  "description": "Ordered stable index over scenes. Owner: 3.1.7.",
  "allOf": [
    { "$ref": "https://schemas.insynergy.co/cttp/v2.0/common/defs.schema.json#/$defs/ArtifactEnvelope" },
    {
      "type": "object",
      "properties": {
        "scenes": {
          "type": "array",
          "minItems": 8,
          "maxItems": 12,
          "items": {
            "type": "object",
            "properties": {
              "scene_id": { "$ref": "https://schemas.insynergy.co/cttp/v2.0/common/defs.schema.json#/$defs/SceneId" },
              "act": { "$ref": "https://schemas.insynergy.co/cttp/v2.0/common/defs.schema.json#/$defs/Act" },
              "order": { "type": "integer", "minimum": 0 },
              "purpose": {
                "type": "string",
                "enum": [
                  "Introduce protagonist",
                  "Reveal hidden risk",
                  "Increase urgency",
                  "Create reversal",
                  "Force decision",
                  "Resolve conflict"
                ]
              }
            },
            "required": ["scene_id", "act", "order", "purpose"],
            "additionalProperties": false
          }
        }
      },
      "required": ["scenes"]
    }
  ],
  "unevaluatedProperties": false
}
```

---

# Field Reference

| Field | Type | Owner | Description |
|---|---|---|---|
| `scenes[].scene_id` | SceneId | 3.1.7 | Reference to the indexed scene. |
| `scenes[].act` | Act | 3.1.7 | Act of the indexed scene. |
| `scenes[].order` | integer ≥ 0 | 3.1.7 | Contiguous zero-based order position. |
| `scenes[].purpose` | enum | 3.1.7 | Dramatic purpose (mirrors 9.4.2). |

---

# Constraints & Invariants

- **INV-9.4.3-1** — `order` values SHALL be contiguous and zero-based across the array (0, 1, …, n−1) with no gaps or duplicates.
- **INV-9.4.3-2** — Array position SHALL equal `order`; the index is stable across regeneration.
- **INV-9.4.3-3** — Every `scene_id` in the index SHALL resolve to a scene in `screenplay.json`, and vice versa (bijective).
- **INV-9.4.3-4** — `act` and `purpose` for each entry SHALL agree with the corresponding scene (9.4.2).
- **INV-9.4.3-5** — Entry count SHALL match the screenplay `scene_count` (8..12).

---

# Example

```json
{
  "schema_version": "2.0.0",
  "build_id": "bld_9f2c7a10",
  "content_hash": "sha256:7d0a...11",
  "scenes": [
    { "scene_id": "scn_0001", "act": "I", "order": 0, "purpose": "Introduce protagonist" },
    { "scene_id": "scn_0002", "act": "I", "order": 1, "purpose": "Reveal hidden risk" },
    { "scene_id": "scn_0003", "act": "II", "order": 2, "purpose": "Increase urgency" }
  ]
}
```

---

# Acceptance Criteria

- Non-contiguous or duplicated `order` values are rejected.
- An index whose scene set differs from `screenplay.json` is rejected.
- Act or purpose disagreement with the source scene fails validation.

---

# 9.4.4 Dialogue (`dialogue.json`)

**Sealed artifact · Owner: 3.1.5**

---

# Purpose

The dialogue line set for the screenplay. Each line binds to a scene, names its speaking character, carries constrained text, a dramatic category, and an explicit silence flag. Dialogue is terse and non-expository; silence is represented explicitly rather than omitted. The `DialogueLine` definition is referenced by the Scene schema (9.4.2).

---

# Canonical Schema

```json
{
  "$schema": "https://json-schema.org/draft/2020-12/schema",
  "$id": "https://schemas.insynergy.co/cttp/v2.0/screenplay/dialogue.schema.json",
  "title": "Dialogue",
  "description": "Dialogue line set. Owner: 3.1.5.",
  "$defs": {
    "DialogueLine": {
      "type": "object",
      "properties": {
        "scene_id": { "$ref": "https://schemas.insynergy.co/cttp/v2.0/common/defs.schema.json#/$defs/SceneId" },
        "character": { "type": "string", "minLength": 1 },
        "text": { "type": "string" },
        "category": {
          "type": "string",
          "enum": ["Question", "Demand", "Refusal", "Warning", "Decision", "Revelation"]
        },
        "silence": { "type": "boolean" }
      },
      "required": ["scene_id", "character", "text", "category", "silence"],
      "additionalProperties": false
    }
  },
  "allOf": [
    { "$ref": "https://schemas.insynergy.co/cttp/v2.0/common/defs.schema.json#/$defs/ArtifactEnvelope" },
    {
      "type": "object",
      "properties": {
        "lines": {
          "type": "array",
          "items": { "$ref": "#/$defs/DialogueLine" }
        }
      },
      "required": ["lines"]
    }
  ],
  "unevaluatedProperties": false
}
```

---

# Field Reference

| Field | Type | Owner | Description |
|---|---|---|---|
| `lines[].scene_id` | SceneId | 3.1.5 | Scene the line belongs to. |
| `lines[].character` | string | 3.1.5 | Speaking character. |
| `lines[].text` | string | 3.1.5 | Line text (≤ 15 words). |
| `lines[].category` | enum | 3.1.5 | Dramatic function of the line. |
| `lines[].silence` | boolean | 3.1.5 | True → the line is an explicit silence beat. |

---

# Constraints & Invariants

- **INV-9.4.4-1** — `words_per_line` SHALL NOT exceed 15 for any line's `text`.
- **INV-9.4.4-2** — `lines_per_turn` SHALL NOT exceed 2 consecutive lines by the same character within a scene.
- **INV-9.4.4-3** — Exposition is prohibited; dialogue SHALL advance conflict, not explain concepts, architecture, or frameworks.
- **INV-9.4.4-4** — Silence is permitted and SHALL be represented explicitly via `silence: true`; a silence beat carries empty or stage-direction text and a category.
- **INV-9.4.4-5** — Every `scene_id` SHALL resolve to a scene in `screenplay.json`; `category` SHALL be one of the allowed values.

---

# Example

```json
{
  "schema_version": "2.0.0",
  "build_id": "bld_9f2c7a10",
  "content_hash": "sha256:c31f...aa",
  "lines": [
    { "scene_id": "scn_0002", "character": "MAYA", "text": "Who authorized the override?", "category": "Question", "silence": false },
    { "scene_id": "scn_0002", "character": "OKAFOR", "text": "", "category": "Refusal", "silence": true }
  ]
}
```

---

# Acceptance Criteria

- A line exceeding 15 words is rejected.
- More than two consecutive same-character lines in a scene fails validation.
- Silence beats are accepted only when `silence` is present and true.
- Unknown categories or unknown properties are rejected.

---

# 9.4.5 Continuity (`continuity.json`)

**Sealed artifact · Owner: 3.1.8**

---

# Purpose

The continuity validation report. It records the pass/fail status of each continuity dimension, the monotonicity of any countdown, the continuity of emotional state, and an enumerated list of violations. Any recorded violation fails validation of the screenplay.

---

# Canonical Schema

```json
{
  "$schema": "https://json-schema.org/draft/2020-12/schema",
  "$id": "https://schemas.insynergy.co/cttp/v2.0/screenplay/continuity.schema.json",
  "title": "Continuity",
  "description": "Continuity validation report. Owner: 3.1.8.",
  "allOf": [
    { "$ref": "https://schemas.insynergy.co/cttp/v2.0/common/defs.schema.json#/$defs/ArtifactEnvelope" },
    {
      "type": "object",
      "properties": {
        "checks": {
          "type": "object",
          "properties": {
            "character": { "type": "boolean" },
            "wardrobe": { "type": "boolean" },
            "location": { "type": "boolean" },
            "time": { "type": "boolean" },
            "emotion": { "type": "boolean" },
            "countdown": { "type": "boolean" },
            "props": { "type": "boolean" }
          },
          "required": ["character", "wardrobe", "location", "time", "emotion", "countdown", "props"],
          "additionalProperties": false
        },
        "countdown_monotonic": { "type": "boolean" },
        "emotion_continuous": { "type": "boolean" },
        "violations": {
          "type": "array",
          "items": {
            "type": "object",
            "properties": {
              "scene_id": { "$ref": "https://schemas.insynergy.co/cttp/v2.0/common/defs.schema.json#/$defs/SceneId" },
              "dimension": {
                "type": "string",
                "enum": ["character", "wardrobe", "location", "time", "emotion", "countdown", "props"]
              },
              "detail": { "type": "string" }
            },
            "required": ["scene_id", "dimension", "detail"],
            "additionalProperties": false
          }
        }
      },
      "required": ["checks", "countdown_monotonic", "emotion_continuous", "violations"]
    }
  ],
  "unevaluatedProperties": false
}
```

---

# Field Reference

| Field | Type | Owner | Description |
|---|---|---|---|
| `checks.character` | boolean | 3.1.8 | Character continuity passed. |
| `checks.wardrobe` | boolean | 3.1.8 | Wardrobe continuity passed. |
| `checks.location` | boolean | 3.1.8 | Location continuity passed. |
| `checks.time` | boolean | 3.1.8 | Temporal continuity passed. |
| `checks.emotion` | boolean | 3.1.8 | Emotional continuity passed. |
| `checks.countdown` | boolean | 3.1.8 | Countdown continuity passed. |
| `checks.props` | boolean | 3.1.8 | Prop continuity passed. |
| `countdown_monotonic` | boolean | 3.1.8 | Countdown decreases monotonically. |
| `emotion_continuous` | boolean | 3.1.8 | Emotional state transitions are continuous. |
| `violations[]` | array<object> | 3.1.8 | Enumerated continuity violations. |

---

# Constraints & Invariants

- **INV-9.4.5-1** — All seven continuity dimensions SHALL be evaluated and reported.
- **INV-9.4.5-2** — Any non-empty `violations` array SHALL cause the screenplay to fail continuity validation.
- **INV-9.4.5-3** — A passing report SHALL have every `checks.*` field true, `countdown_monotonic` true, `emotion_continuous` true, and `violations` empty.
- **INV-9.4.5-4** — Each violation's `dimension` SHALL correspond to a `checks.*` field reported false.
- **INV-9.4.5-5** — Every `violation.scene_id` SHALL resolve to a scene in `screenplay.json`.

---

# Example

```json
{
  "schema_version": "2.0.0",
  "build_id": "bld_9f2c7a10",
  "content_hash": "sha256:e880...42",
  "checks": {
    "character": true,
    "wardrobe": true,
    "location": true,
    "time": true,
    "emotion": true,
    "countdown": true,
    "props": true
  },
  "countdown_monotonic": true,
  "emotion_continuous": true,
  "violations": []
}
```

---

# Acceptance Criteria

- A report with any violation fails validation regardless of `checks` values.
- A passing report requires all checks true and an empty violations array.
- A violation whose dimension shows `checks.*` true is inconsistent and rejected.

---

# 9.4.6 Screenplay Metrics (`screenplay-metrics`)

**Embedded object · Owner: 3.1.8**

---

# Purpose

Quantitative metrics computed over the screenplay, embedded in the validation record. Metrics report scene count, the ratio of dialogue to action, average scene duration, and a continuity score. Action is expected to dominate dialogue in a cinematic screenplay.

---

# Canonical Schema

```json
{
  "$schema": "https://json-schema.org/draft/2020-12/schema",
  "$id": "https://schemas.insynergy.co/cttp/v2.0/screenplay/screenplay-metrics.schema.json",
  "title": "ScreenplayMetrics",
  "description": "Embedded quantitative metrics. Owner: 3.1.8.",
  "type": "object",
  "properties": {
    "scene_count": { "type": "integer", "minimum": 8, "maximum": 12 },
    "dialogue_ratio": { "$ref": "https://schemas.insynergy.co/cttp/v2.0/common/defs.schema.json#/$defs/Ratio" },
    "action_ratio": { "$ref": "https://schemas.insynergy.co/cttp/v2.0/common/defs.schema.json#/$defs/Ratio" },
    "average_scene_duration": { "type": "number", "minimum": 4, "maximum": 10 },
    "continuity_score": { "$ref": "https://schemas.insynergy.co/cttp/v2.0/common/defs.schema.json#/$defs/Score" }
  },
  "required": [
    "scene_count",
    "dialogue_ratio",
    "action_ratio",
    "average_scene_duration",
    "continuity_score"
  ],
  "additionalProperties": false
}
```

---

# Field Reference

| Field | Type | Owner | Description |
|---|---|---|---|
| `scene_count` | integer 8..12 | 3.1.8 | Number of scenes. |
| `dialogue_ratio` | Ratio | 3.1.8 | Fraction of content that is dialogue. |
| `action_ratio` | Ratio | 3.1.8 | Fraction of content that is action. |
| `average_scene_duration` | number 4..10 | 3.1.8 | Mean scene duration in seconds. |
| `continuity_score` | Score | 3.1.8 | Aggregate continuity score. |

---

# Constraints & Invariants

- **INV-9.4.6-1** — `scene_count` SHALL match the screenplay scene count (8..12).
- **INV-9.4.6-2** — `dialogue_ratio` and `action_ratio` SHALL each be valid `Ratio` values, and their sum SHOULD approximate 1.0 within tolerance.
- **INV-9.4.6-3** — `action_ratio` is expected to dominate: `action_ratio` SHOULD exceed `dialogue_ratio`.
- **INV-9.4.6-4** — `average_scene_duration` SHALL lie within the 4..10 scene-duration envelope.
- **INV-9.4.6-5** — `continuity_score` SHALL be a valid `Score`; a failing continuity report (9.4.5) SHALL be reflected by a reduced score.

---

# Example

```json
{
  "scene_count": 10,
  "dialogue_ratio": 0.28,
  "action_ratio": 0.72,
  "average_scene_duration": 7.4,
  "continuity_score": 0.98
}
```

---

# Acceptance Criteria

- Metrics with `scene_count` outside 8..12 are rejected.
- A screenplay whose `dialogue_ratio` exceeds `action_ratio` is flagged as action-deficient.
- Ratios and score outside their common-type bounds are rejected.

---

# 9.4.7 Screenplay Config (`screenplay-config`)

**Sealed artifact · Owner: 3.1.9**

---

# Purpose

The layered, runtime-immutable configuration governing screenplay generation, dialogue, continuity, export, and caching. The effective configuration is a snapshot recorded with each build; it cannot mutate during a run. It fixes scene-count and duration bounds, one-purpose/one-conflict rules, dialogue limits, continuity enforcement, and export format toggles — including the prohibition of custom syntax.

---

# Canonical Schema

```json
{
  "$schema": "https://json-schema.org/draft/2020-12/schema",
  "$id": "https://schemas.insynergy.co/cttp/v2.0/screenplay/screenplay-config.schema.json",
  "title": "ScreenplayConfig",
  "description": "Layered runtime-immutable configuration snapshot. Owner: 3.1.9.",
  "allOf": [
    { "$ref": "https://schemas.insynergy.co/cttp/v2.0/common/defs.schema.json#/$defs/ArtifactEnvelope" },
    {
      "type": "object",
      "properties": {
        "generation": {
          "type": "object",
          "properties": {
            "scene_count_min": { "type": "integer", "const": 8 },
            "scene_count_max": { "type": "integer", "const": 12 },
            "scene_duration_target": { "type": "integer", "const": 7 },
            "scene_duration_max": { "type": "integer", "const": 10 },
            "one_purpose_per_scene": { "type": "boolean", "const": true },
            "one_conflict_per_scene": { "type": "boolean", "const": true }
          },
          "required": [
            "scene_count_min",
            "scene_count_max",
            "scene_duration_target",
            "scene_duration_max",
            "one_purpose_per_scene",
            "one_conflict_per_scene"
          ],
          "additionalProperties": false
        },
        "dialogue": {
          "type": "object",
          "properties": {
            "words_per_line": { "type": "integer", "const": 15 },
            "lines_per_turn": { "type": "integer", "const": 2 },
            "exposition_allowed": { "type": "boolean", "const": false },
            "silence_allowed": { "type": "boolean", "const": true }
          },
          "required": ["words_per_line", "lines_per_turn", "exposition_allowed", "silence_allowed"],
          "additionalProperties": false
        },
        "continuity": {
          "type": "object",
          "properties": {
            "all_dimensions_checked": { "type": "boolean", "const": true },
            "violation_fails_validation": { "type": "boolean", "const": true }
          },
          "required": ["all_dimensions_checked", "violation_fails_validation"],
          "additionalProperties": false
        },
        "export": {
          "type": "object",
          "properties": {
            "fountain": { "type": "boolean", "const": true },
            "json": { "type": "boolean", "const": true },
            "custom_syntax": { "type": "boolean", "const": false }
          },
          "required": ["fountain", "json", "custom_syntax"],
          "additionalProperties": false
        },
        "cache": {
          "type": "object",
          "properties": {
            "cache_key": { "$ref": "https://schemas.insynergy.co/cttp/v2.0/common/defs.schema.json#/$defs/CacheKey" }
          },
          "additionalProperties": false
        },
        "profile": {
          "type": "string",
          "enum": ["preview", "production"]
        }
      },
      "required": ["generation", "dialogue", "continuity", "export", "cache", "profile"]
    }
  ],
  "unevaluatedProperties": false
}
```

---

# Field Reference

| Field | Type | Owner | Description |
|---|---|---|---|
| `generation.scene_count_min` | const 8 | 3.1.9 | Minimum scenes. |
| `generation.scene_count_max` | const 12 | 3.1.9 | Maximum scenes. |
| `generation.scene_duration_target` | const 7 | 3.1.9 | Target scene seconds. |
| `generation.scene_duration_max` | const 10 | 3.1.9 | Maximum scene seconds. |
| `generation.one_purpose_per_scene` | const true | 3.1.9 | Enforce single purpose. |
| `generation.one_conflict_per_scene` | const true | 3.1.9 | Enforce single conflict. |
| `dialogue.words_per_line` | const 15 | 3.1.9 | Word cap per line. |
| `dialogue.lines_per_turn` | const 2 | 3.1.9 | Line cap per turn. |
| `dialogue.exposition_allowed` | const false | 3.1.9 | Exposition prohibited. |
| `dialogue.silence_allowed` | const true | 3.1.9 | Silence permitted. |
| `continuity.all_dimensions_checked` | const true | 3.1.9 | All dimensions evaluated. |
| `continuity.violation_fails_validation` | const true | 3.1.9 | Violation fails validation. |
| `export.fountain` | const true | 3.1.9 | Fountain export enabled. |
| `export.json` | const true | 3.1.9 | JSON export enabled. |
| `export.custom_syntax` | const false | 3.1.9 | Custom syntax prohibited. |
| `cache.cache_key` | CacheKey | 3.1.9 | Configuration cache key. |
| `profile` | enum | 3.1.9 | `preview` or `production`. |

---

# Constraints & Invariants

- **INV-9.4.7-1** — The configuration is immutable at runtime; the recorded snapshot SHALL NOT change during a build.
- **INV-9.4.7-2** — `generation` bounds SHALL be fixed at the stated constants (8/12/7/10) and align with 9.4.1 and 9.4.2.
- **INV-9.4.7-3** — `dialogue` limits SHALL be fixed at 15 words / 2 lines, with exposition disabled and silence enabled, consistent with 9.4.4.
- **INV-9.4.7-4** — `continuity.violation_fails_validation` SHALL be true, consistent with INV-9.4.5-2.
- **INV-9.4.7-5** — `export.custom_syntax` SHALL be false; both `fountain` and `json` SHALL be true (two faithful representations).
- **INV-9.4.7-6** — `profile` SHALL be exactly one of `preview` or `production`; the effective snapshot is recorded with its `CacheKey`.

---

# Example

```json
{
  "schema_version": "2.0.0",
  "build_id": "bld_9f2c7a10",
  "content_hash": "sha256:1a55...09",
  "generation": {
    "scene_count_min": 8,
    "scene_count_max": 12,
    "scene_duration_target": 7,
    "scene_duration_max": 10,
    "one_purpose_per_scene": true,
    "one_conflict_per_scene": true
  },
  "dialogue": {
    "words_per_line": 15,
    "lines_per_turn": 2,
    "exposition_allowed": false,
    "silence_allowed": true
  },
  "continuity": {
    "all_dimensions_checked": true,
    "violation_fails_validation": true
  },
  "export": { "fountain": true, "json": true, "custom_syntax": false },
  "cache": { "cache_key": "ck_screenplay_prod_7f" },
  "profile": "production"
}
```

---

# Acceptance Criteria

- Any deviation from the fixed constants is rejected.
- `custom_syntax: true` is rejected.
- A `profile` outside the enumeration is rejected.
- The snapshot is recorded per build and does not change mid-run.

---

# 9.4.8 Screenplay State (`screenplay-state`)

**Sealed artifact · Owner: 3.1.11**

---

# Purpose

The lifecycle state of the screenplay and its scenes. It records one active screenplay state and a per-scene state array. State advances forward-only until failure, never skips validation, requires approval before export, and treats the approved state as immutable. Transitions are logged and the process is resumable.

---

# Canonical Schema

```json
{
  "$schema": "https://json-schema.org/draft/2020-12/schema",
  "$id": "https://schemas.insynergy.co/cttp/v2.0/screenplay/screenplay-state.schema.json",
  "title": "ScreenplayState",
  "description": "Screenplay and per-scene lifecycle state. Owner: 3.1.11.",
  "allOf": [
    { "$ref": "https://schemas.insynergy.co/cttp/v2.0/common/defs.schema.json#/$defs/ArtifactEnvelope" },
    {
      "type": "object",
      "properties": {
        "state": {
          "type": "string",
          "enum": [
            "Pending",
            "Generating",
            "Generated",
            "Validating",
            "Validated",
            "AwaitingApproval",
            "Approved",
            "Exported",
            "Failed"
          ]
        },
        "scene_states": {
          "type": "array",
          "items": {
            "type": "object",
            "properties": {
              "scene_id": { "$ref": "https://schemas.insynergy.co/cttp/v2.0/common/defs.schema.json#/$defs/SceneId" },
              "state": {
                "type": "string",
                "enum": ["Drafted", "Populated", "Validated", "Locked"]
              }
            },
            "required": ["scene_id", "state"],
            "additionalProperties": false
          }
        }
      },
      "required": ["state", "scene_states"]
    }
  ],
  "unevaluatedProperties": false
}
```

---

# Field Reference

| Field | Type | Owner | Description |
|---|---|---|---|
| `state` | enum | 3.1.11 | Single active screenplay state. |
| `scene_states[].scene_id` | SceneId | 3.1.11 | Scene reference. |
| `scene_states[].state` | enum | 3.1.11 | Per-scene lifecycle state. |

---

# Constraints & Invariants

- **INV-9.4.8-1** — Exactly one `state` SHALL be active per screenplay.
- **INV-9.4.8-2** — **forward_only_until_failure** — `state` SHALL advance only forward through the enumeration; the sole permitted regression is to `Failed`.
- **INV-9.4.8-3** — **no_skipping_validation** — `Validating`/`Validated` SHALL NOT be bypassed; `Generated` SHALL NOT transition directly to `AwaitingApproval` or `Approved`.
- **INV-9.4.8-4** — **approval_required_before_export** — `Exported` SHALL be reachable only from `Approved`.
- **INV-9.4.8-5** — **approved_is_immutable** — once `Approved`, the screenplay body is immutable; only export may follow.
- **INV-9.4.8-6** — Every `scene_id` in `scene_states` SHALL resolve to a scene in `screenplay.json`; per-scene states advance Drafted → Populated → Validated → Locked.
- **INV-9.4.8-7** — All transitions SHALL be logged; state is resumable from the last recorded transition.

---

# Example

```json
{
  "schema_version": "2.0.0",
  "build_id": "bld_9f2c7a10",
  "content_hash": "sha256:aa02...7d",
  "state": "Approved",
  "scene_states": [
    { "scene_id": "scn_0001", "state": "Locked" },
    { "scene_id": "scn_0002", "state": "Locked" },
    { "scene_id": "scn_0003", "state": "Validated" }
  ]
}
```

---

# Acceptance Criteria

- A transition from `Generated` directly to `Approved` is rejected.
- `Exported` is accepted only when preceded by `Approved`.
- Mutation of an `Approved` screenplay body is rejected.
- Scene states outside the four-value enumeration are rejected.

---
# 9.5 Shot Planner & Storyboard Layer Schemas

*Part 9 — JSON Schema / Appendix · Insynergy Cinematic Thought Leadership Platform · Master Specification v2.0*

*Formalization of the Part 4 artifact set: the render-ready visual plan produced by the Shot Planner & Storyboard Engine.*

---

# Purpose

This chapter formalizes the visual-planning artifact set of **Part 4 — Shot Planner & Storyboard Engine**. These schemas specify the render-ready plan that the Shot Planner emits and that the Rendering Platform (Part 5) consumes. Several of these artifacts reappear as Rendering ingest inputs in section 5.1.4; where the ingest form differs from the authoring form, both are documented and cross-referenced.

The layer converts the screenplay (Part 3) into an ordered set of atomic, independently-renderable shots, each carrying its camera, blocking, emotion, continuity, and render-strategy decisions. Every artifact in this chapter is a gate input: nothing proceeds to rendering until the shot- and storyboard-level gates pass.

# Design Philosophy

The **shot is the atomic, independently-renderable unit** of the platform. A shot is planned once, verified once, and rendered once; it carries no dependency on rendering internals and no leakage of technology into creative description. These schemas exist to make every planning artifact **verifiable before rendering** — each field is a decision that a gate can check, each invariant is a property that must hold before a frame is produced. The separation between the enumerated *unit-of-work list* (9.5.1) and the full *atomic planning record* (9.5.2) is deliberate: one drives scheduling, the other drives production.

The eleven schemas of this chapter:

- **9.5.1 shot-list.json** — enumerated unit-of-work list of shots.
- **9.5.2 shot** — canonical atomic planning record (the Shot object).
- **9.5.3 camera-plan.json** — per-shot lens, angle, movement, speed.
- **9.5.4 blocking.json** — observable movement, emotion arc, gaze, breathing.
- **9.5.5 storyboard.json** — technology-free visual frame plan.
- **9.5.6 continuity-report.json** — countdown temporal continuity.
- **9.5.7 render-strategy.json** — one render strategy per shot.
- **9.5.8 shot-metrics** — plan-level ratios and counts (embedded).
- **9.5.9 shot-gate-report** — per-shot readiness gate.
- **9.5.10 storyboard-gate-report** — storyboard-level gate.
- **9.5.11 shot-cache-key** — deterministic re-plan cache key (embedded).

---

# 9.5.1 Shot List (`shot-list.json`)

*The enumerated unit-of-work list emitted by decomposition and consumed by the Shot Planner and Rendering scheduler.*

---

# Purpose

The shot list is the **enumerated unit-of-work list** for a build. It names every shot to be planned and rendered, fixes its scene/shot ordinal position, and declares its coarse render dependencies. It is the authoritative index against which the richer Shot object (9.5.2) and the storyboard (9.5.5) must achieve bijective coverage. Owner: **4.1.2**; Rendering ingest form: **5.1.4**.

---

# Canonical Schema

```json
{
  "$schema": "https://json-schema.org/draft/2020-12/schema",
  "$id": "https://schemas.insynergy.co/cttp/v2.0/shot/shot-list.schema.json",
  "title": "Shot List",
  "description": "Enumerated unit-of-work list of shots for a build (Owner 4.1.2; ingest 5.1.4).",
  "allOf": [
    { "$ref": "https://schemas.insynergy.co/cttp/v2.0/common/defs.schema.json#/$defs/ArtifactEnvelope" },
    {
      "type": "object",
      "properties": {
        "storyboard_id": { "$ref": "https://schemas.insynergy.co/cttp/v2.0/common/defs.schema.json#/$defs/StoryboardId" },
        "shots": {
          "type": "array",
          "minItems": 1,
          "items": { "$ref": "#/$defs/ShotListEntry" }
        }
      },
      "required": ["storyboard_id", "shots"],
      "additionalProperties": false
    }
  ],
  "unevaluatedProperties": false,
  "$defs": {
    "ShotListEntry": {
      "type": "object",
      "description": "One unit of work (5.1.4).",
      "properties": {
        "shot_id": { "$ref": "https://schemas.insynergy.co/cttp/v2.0/common/defs.schema.json#/$defs/ShotId" },
        "scene_index": { "type": "integer", "minimum": 0 },
        "shot_index": { "type": "integer", "minimum": 0 },
        "duration_seconds": { "$ref": "https://schemas.insynergy.co/cttp/v2.0/common/defs.schema.json#/$defs/DurationSeconds" },
        "shot_type": { "$ref": "https://schemas.insynergy.co/cttp/v2.0/common/defs.schema.json#/$defs/ShotType" },
        "character_refs": {
          "type": "array",
          "items": { "$ref": "https://schemas.insynergy.co/cttp/v2.0/common/defs.schema.json#/$defs/RefId" }
        },
        "location_ref": { "$ref": "https://schemas.insynergy.co/cttp/v2.0/common/defs.schema.json#/$defs/RefId" },
        "dependencies": {
          "type": "array",
          "items": { "$ref": "https://schemas.insynergy.co/cttp/v2.0/common/defs.schema.json#/$defs/ShotId" }
        }
      },
      "required": ["shot_id", "scene_index", "shot_index", "duration_seconds", "shot_type", "location_ref"],
      "additionalProperties": false
    }
  }
}
```

---

# Field Reference

| Field | Type | Required | Owner | Description |
|---|---|---|---|---|
| `storyboard_id` | StoryboardId | yes | 4.1.2 | Storyboard this unit-of-work list belongs to. |
| `shots` | array[ShotListEntry] | yes | 4.1.2 | Non-empty enumerated list of units of work. |
| `shots[].shot_id` | ShotId | yes | 5.1.4 | Unique shot identifier within the build. |
| `shots[].scene_index` | integer ≥0 | yes | 5.1.4 | Scene ordinal for total ordering. |
| `shots[].shot_index` | integer ≥0 | yes | 5.1.4 | Shot ordinal within the scene. |
| `shots[].duration_seconds` | DurationSeconds | yes | 5.1.4 | Planned shot duration. |
| `shots[].shot_type` | ShotType | yes | 5.1.4 | Coarse shot classification. |
| `shots[].character_refs` | array[RefId] | no | 5.1.4 | Character Bible references present in the shot. |
| `shots[].location_ref` | RefId | yes | 5.1.4 | Location Bible reference for the shot. |
| `shots[].dependencies` | array[ShotId] | no | 5.1.4 | Shots that must be planned/rendered first. |

---

# Constraints & Invariants

- **INV-9.5.1-1** (P-401): `shots` is non-empty.
- **INV-9.5.1-2** (P-402): every `shot_id` is unique within the build.
- **INV-9.5.1-3** (P-403): the pairs `(scene_index, shot_index)` form a total order with no duplicates.
- **INV-9.5.1-4** (P-404): `dependencies` are acyclic and reference only `shot_id`s present in this same list.
- **INV-9.5.1-5** (P-405): every `location_ref` (and each `character_refs` entry, when present) resolves against the corresponding Bible.
- **INV-9.5.1-6** (P-406): the set of `shot_id`s is the reference set for bijective coverage by 9.5.2 and 9.5.5.

---

# Example

```json
{
  "schema_version": "2.0.0",
  "build_id": "bld_2026_07_20_a1",
  "artifact_type": "shot-list",
  "content_hash": "sha256:7c1e…",
  "created_at": "2026-07-20T09:12:00Z",
  "storyboard_id": "sbd-000-001",
  "shots": [
    {
      "shot_id": "scene-001-shot-01",
      "scene_index": 1,
      "shot_index": 1,
      "duration_seconds": 6,
      "shot_type": "wide",
      "character_refs": ["char-analyst"],
      "location_ref": "loc-trading-floor",
      "dependencies": []
    },
    {
      "shot_id": "scene-001-shot-02",
      "scene_index": 1,
      "shot_index": 2,
      "duration_seconds": 4,
      "shot_type": "medium",
      "location_ref": "loc-trading-floor",
      "dependencies": ["scene-001-shot-01"]
    }
  ]
}
```

---

# Acceptance Criteria

- Validates against the schema and the ArtifactEnvelope.
- `shots` non-empty; all `shot_id`s unique; `(scene_index, shot_index)` a strict total order.
- Dependency graph is a DAG and closed over the list.
- Every `shot_id` in 9.5.2 and 9.5.5 appears exactly once here (bijection).

---

# 9.5.2 Shot (`shot.schema.json`)

*The canonical Shot Schema — the atomic planning record for one independently-renderable shot.*

---

# Purpose

The Shot object is the **full atomic planning record**: the complete, self-contained specification of a single renderable shot. Where the shot list (9.5.1) enumerates work, the Shot object holds every creative decision — camera, blocking, emotion, continuity, and the single render strategy — required to render the shot without further planning. Owner: **4.1.2**. All top-level fields are mandatory; the nested creative objects may be empty at decomposition time but are never absent.

---

# Canonical Schema

```json
{
  "$schema": "https://json-schema.org/draft/2020-12/schema",
  "$id": "https://schemas.insynergy.co/cttp/v2.0/shot/shot.schema.json",
  "title": "Shot",
  "description": "Canonical atomic planning record for one shot (Owner 4.1.2).",
  "type": "object",
  "properties": {
    "shot_id": { "$ref": "https://schemas.insynergy.co/cttp/v2.0/common/defs.schema.json#/$defs/ShotId" },
    "scene_id": { "$ref": "https://schemas.insynergy.co/cttp/v2.0/common/defs.schema.json#/$defs/SceneId" },
    "act": { "$ref": "https://schemas.insynergy.co/cttp/v2.0/common/defs.schema.json#/$defs/Act" },
    "duration_seconds": { "type": "integer", "exclusiveMinimum": 0 },
    "shot_type": { "$ref": "https://schemas.insynergy.co/cttp/v2.0/common/defs.schema.json#/$defs/ShotType" },
    "purpose": { "type": "string", "minLength": 1 },
    "subject": { "$ref": "https://schemas.insynergy.co/cttp/v2.0/common/defs.schema.json#/$defs/RefId" },
    "location": { "$ref": "https://schemas.insynergy.co/cttp/v2.0/common/defs.schema.json#/$defs/RefId" },
    "camera": { "type": "object" },
    "blocking": { "type": "object" },
    "emotion": { "type": "object" },
    "continuity": { "type": "object" },
    "render_strategy": { "$ref": "https://schemas.insynergy.co/cttp/v2.0/common/defs.schema.json#/$defs/RenderStrategy" }
  },
  "required": [
    "shot_id", "scene_id", "act", "duration_seconds", "shot_type",
    "purpose", "subject", "location", "camera", "blocking",
    "emotion", "continuity", "render_strategy"
  ],
  "additionalProperties": false
}
```

---

# Field Reference

| Field | Type | Required | Owner | Description |
|---|---|---|---|---|
| `shot_id` | ShotId | yes | 4.1.2 | Identifier matching `scene-NNN-shot-NN`, prefixed by `scene_id`. |
| `scene_id` | SceneId | yes | 4.1.2 | Owning scene; must prefix `shot_id`. |
| `act` | Act | yes | 4.1.2 | Narrative act the shot belongs to. |
| `duration_seconds` | integer >0 | yes | 4.1.2 | Planned duration; strictly positive integer. |
| `shot_type` | ShotType | yes | 4.1.2 | Shot classification. |
| `purpose` | string (non-empty) | yes | 4.1.2 | Single stated narrative purpose of the shot. |
| `subject` | RefId | yes | 4.1.2 | Character Bible id of the primary subject. |
| `location` | RefId | yes | 4.1.2 | Location Bible id. |
| `camera` | object | yes | 4.1.4 | Camera decisions; may be `{}` at decomposition, never absent. |
| `blocking` | object | yes | 4.1.5 | Blocking decisions; may be `{}` at decomposition, never absent. |
| `emotion` | object | yes | 4.1.5 | Emotional arc; may be `{}` at decomposition, never absent. |
| `continuity` | object | yes | 4.1.8 | Continuity data; may be `{}` at decomposition, never absent. |
| `render_strategy` | RenderStrategy | yes | 4.1.9 | Exactly one render strategy. |

---

# Constraints & Invariants

- **INV-9.5.2-1** (P-421): all thirteen top-level fields are present; none may be omitted.
- **INV-9.5.2-2** (P-422): `camera`, `blocking`, `emotion`, `continuity` are always present as objects, possibly empty `{}`, but never absent.
- **INV-9.5.2-3** (P-423): `shot_id` matches the pattern `scene-NNN-shot-NN`.
- **INV-9.5.2-4** (P-424): `shot_id` is prefixed by `scene_id` (the scene component agrees).
- **INV-9.5.2-5** (P-425): `duration_seconds` is a positive integer (>0).
- **INV-9.5.2-6** (P-426): `purpose` is non-empty and expresses exactly one primary action.
- **INV-9.5.2-7** (P-427): exactly one `render_strategy` is assigned.
- **INV-9.5.2-8** (P-428): `subject` resolves in the Character Bible; `location` resolves in the Location Bible.
- **INV-9.5.2-9** (P-429): the `shot_id` corresponds to exactly one entry in the shot list (9.5.1).

---

# Example

```json
{
  "shot_id": "scene-001-shot-01",
  "scene_id": "scene-001",
  "act": "act_1",
  "duration_seconds": 6,
  "shot_type": "wide",
  "purpose": "Establish the analyst alone on the empty trading floor before dawn.",
  "subject": "char-analyst",
  "location": "loc-trading-floor",
  "camera": { "lens": "35mm", "angle": "eye", "movement": "slow_push", "speed": "slow" },
  "blocking": { "ANALYST": { "start": "at desk", "action": "stands", "end": "faces window" } },
  "emotion": { "before": "resignation", "after": "resolve" },
  "continuity": { "countdown": 5 },
  "render_strategy": "runway_video"
}
```

---

# Acceptance Criteria

- Validates against the schema; all mandatory fields present.
- `shot_id` well-formed and scene-prefixed; `duration_seconds` a positive integer.
- Exactly one `render_strategy`; `purpose` states one action.
- Nested creative objects present (empty allowed only pre-planning).

---

# 9.5.3 Camera Plan (`camera-plan.json`)

*Per-shot camera language: lens, angle, movement, and speed, with hard complexity caps.*

---

# Purpose

The camera plan assigns the controlled camera vocabulary to each shot and enforces the platform's **complexity ceilings**: a shot may carry at most two primary subjects, one camera movement, one primary action, and one emotional transition. These caps keep every shot within the render envelope of a single generated clip. Owner: **4.1.4**; Rendering ingest: **5.1.4**.

---

# Canonical Schema

```json
{
  "$schema": "https://json-schema.org/draft/2020-12/schema",
  "$id": "https://schemas.insynergy.co/cttp/v2.0/shot/camera-plan.schema.json",
  "title": "Camera Plan",
  "description": "Per-shot camera language with complexity caps (Owner 4.1.4; ingest 5.1.4).",
  "allOf": [
    { "$ref": "https://schemas.insynergy.co/cttp/v2.0/common/defs.schema.json#/$defs/ArtifactEnvelope" },
    {
      "type": "object",
      "properties": {
        "shots": {
          "type": "array",
          "minItems": 1,
          "items": {
            "type": "object",
            "properties": {
              "shot_id": { "$ref": "https://schemas.insynergy.co/cttp/v2.0/common/defs.schema.json#/$defs/ShotId" },
              "lens": { "type": "string", "enum": ["24mm", "35mm", "50mm", "85mm"] },
              "angle": { "type": "string", "enum": ["eye", "low", "high"] },
              "movement": { "type": "string", "enum": ["static", "slow_push", "slow_pull", "dolly", "pan", "tilt"] },
              "speed": { "type": "string", "enum": ["slow"] },
              "framing": { "type": "string" },
              "movement_speed": { "type": "string" },
              "focus": { "type": "string" },
              "constraints": {
                "type": "object",
                "properties": {
                  "primary_subjects": { "type": "integer", "minimum": 0, "maximum": 2 },
                  "camera_movements": { "type": "integer", "minimum": 0, "maximum": 1 },
                  "primary_actions": { "type": "integer", "minimum": 0, "maximum": 1 },
                  "emotional_transitions": { "type": "integer", "minimum": 0, "maximum": 1 }
                },
                "required": ["primary_subjects", "camera_movements", "primary_actions", "emotional_transitions"],
                "additionalProperties": false
              }
            },
            "required": ["shot_id", "lens", "angle", "movement", "speed"],
            "additionalProperties": false
          }
        }
      },
      "required": ["shots"],
      "additionalProperties": false
    }
  ],
  "unevaluatedProperties": false
}
```

---

# Field Reference

| Field | Type | Required | Owner | Description |
|---|---|---|---|---|
| `shots[].shot_id` | ShotId | yes | 4.1.4 | Shot this camera entry describes. |
| `shots[].lens` | enum | yes | 4.1.4 | One of `24mm`, `35mm`, `50mm`, `85mm`. |
| `shots[].angle` | enum | yes | 4.1.4 | One of `eye`, `low`, `high`. |
| `shots[].movement` | enum | yes | 4.1.4 | One of `static`, `slow_push`, `slow_pull`, `dolly`, `pan`, `tilt`. |
| `shots[].speed` | enum | yes | 4.1.4 | Fixed value `slow`. |
| `shots[].framing` | string | no | 4.1.4 | Optional framing note. |
| `shots[].movement_speed` | string | no | 4.1.4 | Optional movement-speed qualifier. |
