| `shots[].focus` | string | no | 4.1.4 | Optional focus note. |
| `shots[].constraints` | object | no | 4.1.4 | Modeled complexity caps (see invariants). |

---

# Constraints & Invariants

- **INV-9.5.3-1** (P-461): `primary_subjects` ≤ 2.
- **INV-9.5.3-2** (P-462): `camera_movements` ≤ 1 (a single `movement` value per shot).
- **INV-9.5.3-3** (P-463): `primary_actions` ≤ 1.
- **INV-9.5.3-4** (P-464): `emotional_transitions` ≤ 1.
- **INV-9.5.3-5** (P-465): `lens`, `angle`, `movement`, `speed` use only the enumerated vocabulary.
- **INV-9.5.3-6** (P-466): every `shot_id` resolves to a shot in the shot list (9.5.1).
- **INV-9.5.3-7** (P-467): `speed` is `slow` for every shot.
- **INV-9.5.3-8** (P-468): when `constraints` is present, all four caps are reported and satisfied.

---

# Example

```json
{
  "schema_version": "2.0.0",
  "build_id": "bld_2026_07_20_a1",
  "artifact_type": "camera-plan",
  "content_hash": "sha256:aa02…",
  "created_at": "2026-07-20T09:20:00Z",
  "shots": [
    {
      "shot_id": "scene-001-shot-01",
      "lens": "35mm",
      "angle": "eye",
      "movement": "slow_push",
      "speed": "slow",
      "framing": "single, centered",
      "focus": "subject",
      "constraints": {
        "primary_subjects": 1,
        "camera_movements": 1,
        "primary_actions": 1,
        "emotional_transitions": 1
      }
    }
  ]
}
```

---

# Acceptance Criteria

- Validates against schema and envelope.
- All four enumerated camera fields present and in-vocabulary; `speed` = `slow`.
- Complexity caps respected (≤2 subjects, ≤1 movement/action/transition).
- Every `shot_id` covered by the shot list.

---

# 9.5.4 Blocking (`blocking.json`)

*Observable physical movement, emotional arc, gaze, and breathing — performance separated from dialogue.*

---

# Purpose

The blocking artifact records **only observable movement**: what each character physically does, where they start and end, where they look, and how they breathe. It captures the emotional arc as a before/after pair and keeps performance direction strictly separate from dialogue. Owner: **4.1.5**. At most one action per character is permitted so that each shot maps to a single renderable performance beat.

---

# Canonical Schema

```json
{
  "$schema": "https://json-schema.org/draft/2020-12/schema",
  "$id": "https://schemas.insynergy.co/cttp/v2.0/shot/blocking.schema.json",
  "title": "Blocking",
  "description": "Observable movement, emotion arc, gaze and breathing per shot (Owner 4.1.5).",
  "type": "object",
  "properties": {
    "shots": {
      "type": "array",
      "minItems": 1,
      "items": {
        "type": "object",
        "properties": {
          "shot_id": { "$ref": "https://schemas.insynergy.co/cttp/v2.0/common/defs.schema.json#/$defs/ShotId" },
          "blocking": {
            "type": "object",
            "description": "Map of CHARACTER token to a single movement beat.",
            "additionalProperties": {
              "type": "object",
              "properties": {
                "start": { "type": "string" },
                "action": { "type": "string" },
                "end": { "type": "string" }
              },
              "required": ["start", "action", "end"],
              "additionalProperties": false
            }
          },
          "emotion": {
            "type": "object",
            "properties": {
              "before": { "type": "string", "minLength": 1 },
              "after": { "type": "string", "minLength": 1 }
            },
            "required": ["before", "after"],
            "additionalProperties": false
          },
          "eyes": {
            "type": "object",
            "properties": { "focus": { "type": "string" } },
            "required": ["focus"],
            "additionalProperties": false
          },
          "breathing": { "type": "string" }
        },
        "required": ["shot_id", "blocking", "emotion", "eyes", "breathing"],
        "additionalProperties": false
      }
    }
  },
  "required": ["shots"],
  "additionalProperties": false
}
```

---

# Field Reference

| Field | Type | Required | Owner | Description |
|---|---|---|---|---|
| `shots[].shot_id` | ShotId | yes | 4.1.5 | Shot this blocking entry describes. |
| `shots[].blocking` | object | yes | 4.1.5 | Map of `<CHARACTER>` → `{start, action, end}`. |
| `shots[].blocking.<CHAR>.start` | string | yes | 4.1.5 | Observable starting position. |
| `shots[].blocking.<CHAR>.action` | string | yes | 4.1.5 | Single observable action. |
| `shots[].blocking.<CHAR>.end` | string | yes | 4.1.5 | Observable ending position. |
| `shots[].emotion.before` | string | yes | 4.1.5 | Emotional state entering the shot. |
| `shots[].emotion.after` | string | yes | 4.1.5 | Emotional state leaving the shot. |
| `shots[].eyes.focus` | string | yes | 4.1.5 | Gaze target. |
| `shots[].breathing` | string | yes | 4.1.5 | Breathing description. |

---

# Constraints & Invariants

- **INV-9.5.4-1** (P-481): blocking describes observable movement only — no interior narration.
- **INV-9.5.4-2** (P-482): at most one `action` per character (one beat per character per shot).
- **INV-9.5.4-3** (P-483): `emotion` carries both `before` and `after`.
- **INV-9.5.4-4** (P-484): performance direction is separated from dialogue (no dialogue in this artifact).
- **INV-9.5.4-5** (P-485): each character key resolves against the Character Bible.
- **INV-9.5.4-6** (P-486): every `shot_id` resolves to a shot in the shot list (9.5.1).
- **INV-9.5.4-7** (P-487): `eyes.focus` and `breathing` are present for every shot.

---

# Example

```json
{
  "shots": [
    {
      "shot_id": "scene-001-shot-01",
      "blocking": {
        "ANALYST": { "start": "seated at desk", "action": "rises slowly", "end": "standing at window" }
      },
      "emotion": { "before": "resignation", "after": "resolve" },
      "eyes": { "focus": "the skyline outside" },
      "breathing": "slow, deliberate exhale"
    }
  ]
}
```

---

# Acceptance Criteria

- Validates against schema.
- Exactly one action per character per shot.
- `emotion.before` and `emotion.after` both present and non-empty.
- No dialogue present; `eyes.focus` and `breathing` populated.

---

# 9.5.5 Storyboard (`storyboard.json`)

*The technology-free visual frame plan — controlled composition, lighting, palette, and depth vocabulary.*

---

# Purpose

The storyboard is the **purely creative visual plan**. Each shot receives a controlled `frame` (composition, lighting, palette, depth) plus focal subject, camera, blocking, emotion, and purpose. The storyboard **never contains technology** — no provider, model, resolution, codec, lens, aperture, or prompt appears here. It maintains **bijective coverage** with the shot list. Owner: **4.1.6**; Rendering ingest: **5.1.4**.

---

# Canonical Schema

```json
{
  "$schema": "https://json-schema.org/draft/2020-12/schema",
  "$id": "https://schemas.insynergy.co/cttp/v2.0/shot/storyboard.schema.json",
  "title": "Storyboard",
  "description": "Technology-free visual frame plan (Owner 4.1.6; ingest 5.1.4).",
  "allOf": [
    { "$ref": "https://schemas.insynergy.co/cttp/v2.0/common/defs.schema.json#/$defs/ArtifactEnvelope" },
    {
      "type": "object",
      "properties": {
        "storyboard_id": { "$ref": "https://schemas.insynergy.co/cttp/v2.0/common/defs.schema.json#/$defs/StoryboardId" },
        "shots": {
          "type": "array",
          "minItems": 1,
          "items": {
            "type": "object",
            "properties": {
              "shot_id": { "$ref": "https://schemas.insynergy.co/cttp/v2.0/common/defs.schema.json#/$defs/ShotId" },
              "frame": {
                "type": "object",
                "properties": {
                  "composition": { "type": "string", "enum": ["rule_of_thirds", "centered", "leading_lines", "symmetry", "negative_space"] },
                  "lighting": { "type": "string", "enum": ["low_key", "high_key", "natural", "silhouette", "rim"] },
                  "palette": { "type": "string", "enum": ["graphite", "amber", "steel", "monochrome", "warm", "cool"] },
                  "depth": { "type": "string", "enum": ["deep_focus", "shallow_focus", "flat"] }
                },
                "required": ["composition", "lighting", "palette", "depth"],
                "additionalProperties": false
              },
              "focal_subject": { "$ref": "https://schemas.insynergy.co/cttp/v2.0/common/defs.schema.json#/$defs/RefId" },
              "camera": { "type": "object" },
              "blocking": { "type": "object" },
              "emotion": { "type": "object" },
              "shot_purpose": { "type": "string", "minLength": 1 },
              "visual_notes": { "type": "string" },
              "continuity_group": { "type": "string" }
            },
            "required": ["shot_id", "frame", "focal_subject", "camera", "blocking", "emotion", "shot_purpose"],
            "additionalProperties": false
          }
        }
      },
      "required": ["storyboard_id", "shots"],
      "additionalProperties": false
    }
  ],
  "unevaluatedProperties": false
}
```

---

# Field Reference

| Field | Type | Required | Owner | Description |
|---|---|---|---|---|
| `storyboard_id` | StoryboardId | yes | 4.1.6 | Storyboard identifier. |
| `shots[].shot_id` | ShotId | yes | 4.1.6 | Shot this frame describes. |
| `shots[].frame.composition` | enum | yes | 4.1.6 | Controlled composition term, e.g. `rule_of_thirds`. |
| `shots[].frame.lighting` | enum | yes | 4.1.6 | Controlled lighting term, e.g. `low_key`. |
| `shots[].frame.palette` | enum | yes | 4.1.6 | Controlled palette term, e.g. `graphite`. |
| `shots[].frame.depth` | enum | yes | 4.1.6 | Controlled depth term, e.g. `deep_focus`. |
| `shots[].focal_subject` | RefId | yes | 4.1.6 | Focal subject reference. |
| `shots[].camera` | object | yes | 4.1.6 | Creative camera summary (no technology). |
| `shots[].blocking` | object | yes | 4.1.6 | Creative blocking summary. |
| `shots[].emotion` | object | yes | 4.1.6 | Emotional summary. |
| `shots[].shot_purpose` | string | yes | 4.1.6 | Purpose of the shot. |
| `shots[].visual_notes` | string | no | 4.1.6 | Optional visual notes. |
| `shots[].continuity_group` | string | no | 4.1.6 | Optional continuity grouping key. |

---

# Constraints & Invariants

- **INV-9.5.5-1** (P-501): `frame` uses only controlled vocabulary for composition, lighting, palette, depth.
- **INV-9.5.5-2** (P-502): the storyboard contains **no technology** fields (provider, model, resolution, codec, lens, aperture, prompt) at any depth.
- **INV-9.5.5-3** (P-503): the set of `shot_id`s is in **bijection** with the shot-list `shot_id`s (9.5.1).
- **INV-9.5.5-4** (P-504): `focal_subject` resolves against the Character or Location Bible.
- **INV-9.5.5-5** (P-505): `shot_purpose` is non-empty.
- **INV-9.5.5-6** (P-506): `frame`, `focal_subject`, `camera`, `blocking`, `emotion`, `shot_purpose` are present for every shot.
- **INV-9.5.5-7** (P-507): `storyboard_id` equals the shot-list `storyboard_id` for the build.
- **INV-9.5.5-8** (P-508): `continuity_group`, where present, is shared only by shots that are continuity-linked.
- **INV-9.5.5-9** (P-509): each `shot_id` appears exactly once.
- **INV-9.5.5-10** (P-510): no numeric technical specification (aspect other than `Ratio`, fps, bitrate) appears.

---

# Example

```json
{
  "schema_version": "2.0.0",
  "build_id": "bld_2026_07_20_a1",
  "artifact_type": "storyboard",
  "content_hash": "sha256:bb14…",
  "created_at": "2026-07-20T09:35:00Z",
  "storyboard_id": "sbd-000-001",
  "shots": [
    {
      "shot_id": "scene-001-shot-01",
      "frame": { "composition": "rule_of_thirds", "lighting": "low_key", "palette": "graphite", "depth": "deep_focus" },
      "focal_subject": "char-analyst",
      "camera": { "language": "slow push, eye level" },
      "blocking": { "summary": "analyst rises, turns to window" },
      "emotion": { "arc": "resignation to resolve" },
      "shot_purpose": "Establish isolation before the turn.",
      "visual_notes": "Empty desks recede into shadow.",
      "continuity_group": "cg-open"
    }
  ]
}
```

---

# Acceptance Criteria

- Validates against schema and envelope.
- `frame` fully specified from controlled vocabulary.
- No technology fields anywhere in the artifact.
- `shot_id` set is a bijection with the shot list.

---

# 9.5.6 Continuity Report (`continuity-report.json`)

*Countdown temporal continuity: monotonic non-increasing markers, terminal STOP, forward-only.*

---

# Purpose

The continuity report models temporal continuity as a **countdown**: each shot carries a marker that is monotonically non-increasing across the scene, ending at the terminal floor `STOP`. Time moves forward only; flashbacks are tracked as bounded, returning excursions. The report also lists any continuity violations. Owner: **4.1.8**.

---

# Canonical Schema

```json
{
  "$schema": "https://json-schema.org/draft/2020-12/schema",
  "$id": "https://schemas.insynergy.co/cttp/v2.0/shot/continuity-report.schema.json",
  "title": "Continuity Report",
  "description": "Countdown temporal continuity for a scene (Owner 4.1.8).",
  "type": "object",
  "properties": {
    "scene_id": { "$ref": "https://schemas.insynergy.co/cttp/v2.0/common/defs.schema.json#/$defs/SceneId" },
    "temporal_representation": { "type": "string", "const": "countdown" },
    "markers": {
      "type": "array",
      "items": {
        "type": "object",
        "properties": {
          "shot": { "type": "integer", "minimum": 0 },
          "value": {
            "oneOf": [
              { "type": "integer", "minimum": 0 },
              { "type": "string", "const": "STOP" }
            ]
          }
        },
        "required": ["shot", "value"],
        "additionalProperties": false
      }
    },
    "monotonic": { "type": "boolean" },
    "direction": { "type": "string", "const": "forward_only" },
    "terminal_marker": { "type": "string", "const": "STOP" },
    "flashback_tracks": {
      "type": "array",
      "items": {
        "type": "object",
        "properties": {
          "track_id": { "type": "string" },
          "enclosing_shot": { "type": "integer", "minimum": 0 },
          "return_marker": {
            "oneOf": [
              { "type": "integer", "minimum": 0 },
              { "type": "string", "const": "STOP" }
            ]
          }
        },
        "required": ["track_id", "enclosing_shot", "return_marker"],
        "additionalProperties": false
      }
    },
    "violations": {
      "type": "array",
      "items": {
        "type": "object",
        "properties": {
          "previous": { "type": "integer", "minimum": 0 },
          "current": { "type": "integer", "minimum": 0 }
        },
        "required": ["previous", "current"],
        "additionalProperties": false
      }
    }
  },
  "required": ["scene_id", "temporal_representation", "markers", "monotonic", "direction", "terminal_marker"],
  "additionalProperties": false
}
```

---

# Field Reference

| Field | Type | Required | Owner | Description |
|---|---|---|---|---|
| `scene_id` | SceneId | yes | 4.1.8 | Scene the report covers. |
| `temporal_representation` | const `countdown` | yes | 4.1.8 | Fixed representation. |
| `markers` | array | yes | 4.1.8 | Per-shot countdown markers. |
| `markers[].shot` | integer | yes | 4.1.8 | Shot ordinal. |
| `markers[].value` | integer or `STOP` | yes | 4.1.8 | Countdown value or terminal `STOP`. |
| `monotonic` | boolean | yes | 4.1.8 | Whether markers are non-increasing. |
| `direction` | const `forward_only` | yes | 4.1.8 | Time direction. |
| `terminal_marker` | const `STOP` | yes | 4.1.8 | Terminal floor marker. |
| `flashback_tracks` | array | no | 4.1.8 | Bounded, returning flashback excursions. |
| `violations` | array | no | 4.1.8 | Detected `{previous, current}` continuity breaks. |

---

# Constraints & Invariants

- **INV-9.5.6-1** (P-541): `markers` values are monotonically non-increasing by `shot`.
- **INV-9.5.6-2** (P-542): `STOP` is the terminal floor; no marker follows a `STOP`.
- **INV-9.5.6-3** (P-543): `direction` is `forward_only`.
- **INV-9.5.6-4** (P-544): `monotonic` is `true` iff `violations` is empty.
- **INV-9.5.6-5** (P-545): each `flashback_track` returns via `return_marker` to the enclosing timeline.
- **INV-9.5.6-6** (P-546): `enclosing_shot` references a shot present in `markers`.
- **INV-9.5.6-7** (P-547): `temporal_representation` is `countdown`; `terminal_marker` is `STOP`.
- **INV-9.5.6-8** (P-548): every `violations` entry has `current > previous` (an increase, i.e. the countdown ran backward).

---

# Example

```json
{
  "scene_id": "scene-001",
  "temporal_representation": "countdown",
  "markers": [
    { "shot": 1, "value": 5 },
    { "shot": 2, "value": 3 },
    { "shot": 3, "value": 0 },
    { "shot": 4, "value": "STOP" }
  ],
  "monotonic": true,
  "direction": "forward_only",
  "terminal_marker": "STOP",
  "flashback_tracks": [],
  "violations": []
}
```

---

# Acceptance Criteria

- Validates against schema.
- Markers non-increasing; `STOP` terminal; no marker after `STOP`.
- `monotonic` consistent with `violations` emptiness.
- Flashback tracks bounded and returning.

---

# 9.5.7 Render Strategy (`render-strategy.json`)

*Exactly one render strategy per shot, bounded by the hybrid ratio cap.*

---

# Purpose

The render-strategy artifact assigns **exactly one** render strategy to each shot. No shot mixes strategies. `runway_video` is selected only where natural motion genuinely matters, and the overall use of it is bounded by the hybrid ratio governed by 4.1.10 (and verified in 9.5.8). Owner: **4.1.9**; Rendering ingest: **5.1.4**.

---

# Canonical Schema

```json
{
  "$schema": "https://json-schema.org/draft/2020-12/schema",
  "$id": "https://schemas.insynergy.co/cttp/v2.0/shot/render-strategy.schema.json",
  "title": "Render Strategy",
  "description": "One render strategy per shot (Owner 4.1.9; ingest 5.1.4).",
  "allOf": [
    { "$ref": "https://schemas.insynergy.co/cttp/v2.0/common/defs.schema.json#/$defs/ArtifactEnvelope" },
    {
      "type": "object",
      "properties": {
        "shots": {
          "type": "array",
          "minItems": 1,
          "items": {
            "type": "object",
            "properties": {
              "shot_id": { "$ref": "https://schemas.insynergy.co/cttp/v2.0/common/defs.schema.json#/$defs/ShotId" },
              "render_strategy": { "$ref": "https://schemas.insynergy.co/cttp/v2.0/common/defs.schema.json#/$defs/RenderStrategy" },
              "render_profile": { "type": "string" }
            },
            "required": ["shot_id", "render_strategy"],
            "additionalProperties": false
          }
        }
      },
      "required": ["shots"],
      "additionalProperties": false
    }
  ],
  "unevaluatedProperties": false
}
```

---

# Field Reference

| Field | Type | Required | Owner | Description |
|---|---|---|---|---|
| `shots[].shot_id` | ShotId | yes | 4.1.9 | Shot receiving a strategy. |
| `shots[].render_strategy` | RenderStrategy | yes | 4.1.9 | Exactly one strategy for the shot. |
| `shots[].render_profile` | string | no | 4.1.9 | Optional strategy profile qualifier. |

---

# Constraints & Invariants

- **INV-9.5.7-1** (P-561): exactly one `render_strategy` per shot.
- **INV-9.5.7-2** (P-562): no shot mixes strategies (single-valued, not an array).
- **INV-9.5.7-3** (P-563): `runway_video` is used only where natural motion matters.
- **INV-9.5.7-4** (P-564): aggregate `runway_video` use is bounded by the hybrid ratio cap (4.1.10; measured in 9.5.8).
- **INV-9.5.7-5** (P-565): every `shot_id` resolves to a shot in the shot list (9.5.1).
- **INV-9.5.7-6** (P-566): each shot's `render_strategy` agrees with the value on its Shot object (9.5.2).
- **INV-9.5.7-7** (P-567): `render_profile`, when present, is valid for the chosen strategy.

---

# Example

```json
{
  "schema_version": "2.0.0",
  "build_id": "bld_2026_07_20_a1",
  "artifact_type": "render-strategy",
  "content_hash": "sha256:cc27…",
  "created_at": "2026-07-20T09:40:00Z",
  "shots": [
    { "shot_id": "scene-001-shot-01", "render_strategy": "runway_video", "render_profile": "motion_preview" },
    { "shot_id": "scene-001-shot-02", "render_strategy": "animated" }
  ]
}
```

---

# Acceptance Criteria

- Validates against schema and envelope.
- Exactly one strategy per shot; no arrays.
- Aggregate `runway_video` ratio within the hybrid cap (9.5.8).
- Strategies agree with the corresponding Shot objects.

---

# 9.5.8 Shot Metrics (`shot-metrics`)

*Embedded plan-level counts and ratios; the three strategy ratios partition the plan.*

---

# Purpose

Shot metrics is an **embedded** summary of the completed plan: total shot count, average duration, and the three render-strategy ratios. The ratios **partition** the plan and sum to `1.0`; the `runway_ratio` must remain below the hybrid cap (0.40 preview, 0.50 final). Owner: **4.1.13**. As an embedded object it does not carry the full ArtifactEnvelope.

---

# Canonical Schema

```json
{
  "$schema": "https://json-schema.org/draft/2020-12/schema",
  "$id": "https://schemas.insynergy.co/cttp/v2.0/shot/shot-metrics.schema.json",
  "title": "Shot Metrics",
  "description": "Embedded plan-level counts and strategy ratios (Owner 4.1.13).",
  "type": "object",
  "properties": {
    "shots": { "type": "integer", "minimum": 0 },
    "average_duration": { "type": "number", "minimum": 0 },
    "runway_ratio": { "$ref": "https://schemas.insynergy.co/cttp/v2.0/common/defs.schema.json#/$defs/Ratio" },
    "animated_ratio": { "$ref": "https://schemas.insynergy.co/cttp/v2.0/common/defs.schema.json#/$defs/Ratio" },
    "graphics_ratio": { "$ref": "https://schemas.insynergy.co/cttp/v2.0/common/defs.schema.json#/$defs/Ratio" }
  },
  "required": ["shots", "average_duration", "runway_ratio", "animated_ratio", "graphics_ratio"],
  "additionalProperties": false
}
```

---

# Field Reference

| Field | Type | Required | Owner | Description |
|---|---|---|---|---|
| `shots` | integer ≥0 | yes | 4.1.13 | Total number of shots in the plan. |
| `average_duration` | number ≥0 | yes | 4.1.13 | Mean `duration_seconds` across shots. |
| `runway_ratio` | Ratio | yes | 4.1.13 | Fraction of shots using `runway_video`. |
| `animated_ratio` | Ratio | yes | 4.1.13 | Fraction of shots using `animated`. |
| `graphics_ratio` | Ratio | yes | 4.1.13 | Fraction of shots using graphics. |

---

# Constraints & Invariants

- **INV-9.5.8-1** (P-641): `runway_ratio + animated_ratio + graphics_ratio = 1.0` (the ratios partition the plan).
- **INV-9.5.8-2** (P-642): `runway_ratio` < 0.40 for preview builds.
- **INV-9.5.8-3** (P-643): `runway_ratio` < 0.50 for final builds.
- **INV-9.5.8-4** (P-644): `shots` equals the length of the shot list (9.5.1).
- **INV-9.5.8-5** (P-645): `average_duration` is the mean of the Shot objects' `duration_seconds`.

---

# Example

```json
{
  "shots": 24,
  "average_duration": 5.25,
  "runway_ratio": 0.33,
  "animated_ratio": 0.42,
  "graphics_ratio": 0.25
}
```

---

# Acceptance Criteria

- Validates against schema.
- Three ratios sum to `1.0`.
- `runway_ratio` under the applicable hybrid cap.
- `shots` and `average_duration` consistent with the plan.

---

# 9.5.9 Shot Gate Report (`shot-gate-report`)

*Per-shot readiness gate: eight boolean checks combined by logical AND.*

---

# Purpose

The shot gate report is the **per-shot readiness verdict**. Eight boolean checks confirm that purpose, camera, blocking, emotion, continuity, and render strategy are defined, and that the shot carries a single action and a single camera move. All eight must be `true` (logical AND) for `PASS`; any `false` blocks rendering for that shot. Owner: **4.1.12**.

---

# Canonical Schema

```json
{
  "$schema": "https://json-schema.org/draft/2020-12/schema",
  "$id": "https://schemas.insynergy.co/cttp/v2.0/shot/shot-gate-report.schema.json",
  "title": "Shot Gate Report",
  "description": "Per-shot readiness gate (Owner 4.1.12).",
  "type": "object",
  "properties": {
    "shot_id": { "$ref": "https://schemas.insynergy.co/cttp/v2.0/common/defs.schema.json#/$defs/ShotId" },
    "result": { "type": "string", "enum": ["PASS", "FAIL"] },
    "checks": {
      "type": "object",
      "properties": {
        "purpose_exists": { "type": "boolean" },
        "camera_defined": { "type": "boolean" },
        "blocking_defined": { "type": "boolean" },
        "emotion_defined": { "type": "boolean" },
        "continuity_valid": { "type": "boolean" },
        "render_strategy_defined": { "type": "boolean" },
        "single_action": { "type": "boolean" },
        "single_camera_move": { "type": "boolean" }
      },
      "required": [
        "purpose_exists", "camera_defined", "blocking_defined", "emotion_defined",
        "continuity_valid", "render_strategy_defined", "single_action", "single_camera_move"
      ],
      "additionalProperties": false
    },
    "failed_checks": { "type": "array", "items": { "type": "string" } },
    "owning_sections": { "type": "object", "additionalProperties": { "type": "string" } },
    "rendering_blocked": { "type": "boolean" }
  },
  "required": ["shot_id", "result", "checks", "failed_checks", "owning_sections", "rendering_blocked"],
  "additionalProperties": false
}
```

---

# Field Reference

| Field | Type | Required | Owner | Description |
|---|---|---|---|---|
| `shot_id` | ShotId | yes | 4.1.12 | Shot being gated. |
| `result` | enum PASS/FAIL | yes | 4.1.12 | Overall verdict. |
| `checks.purpose_exists` | boolean | yes | 4.1.12 | Purpose is present. |
| `checks.camera_defined` | boolean | yes | 4.1.12 | Camera decisions defined. |
| `checks.blocking_defined` | boolean | yes | 4.1.12 | Blocking defined. |
| `checks.emotion_defined` | boolean | yes | 4.1.12 | Emotion arc defined. |
| `checks.continuity_valid` | boolean | yes | 4.1.12 | Continuity valid. |
| `checks.render_strategy_defined` | boolean | yes | 4.1.12 | Render strategy assigned. |
| `checks.single_action` | boolean | yes | 4.1.12 | Exactly one action. |
| `checks.single_camera_move` | boolean | yes | 4.1.12 | Exactly one camera move. |
| `failed_checks` | array[string] | yes | 4.1.12 | Names of failed checks. |
| `owning_sections` | object | yes | 4.1.12 | Map of check → owning spec section. |
| `rendering_blocked` | boolean | yes | 4.1.12 | Whether rendering is blocked. |

---

# Constraints & Invariants

- **INV-9.5.9-1** (P-621): `result` is `PASS` iff all eight `checks` are `true` (logical AND).
- **INV-9.5.9-2** (P-622): `failed_checks` lists exactly the check keys whose value is `false`.
- **INV-9.5.9-3** (P-625): `rendering_blocked` is `true` iff `result` is `FAIL`.
- **INV-9.5.9-4** (P-626): `single_action` reflects the one-action rule from blocking (9.5.4).
- **INV-9.5.9-5** (P-627): `single_camera_move` reflects the `camera_movements ≤ 1` cap (9.5.3).
- **INV-9.5.9-6** (P-628): `owning_sections` provides a section citation for every failed check.

---

# Example

```json
{
  "shot_id": "scene-001-shot-01",
  "result": "PASS",
  "checks": {
    "purpose_exists": true,
    "camera_defined": true,
    "blocking_defined": true,
    "emotion_defined": true,
    "continuity_valid": true,
    "render_strategy_defined": true,
    "single_action": true,
    "single_camera_move": true
  },
  "failed_checks": [],
  "owning_sections": {},
  "rendering_blocked": false
}
```

---

# Acceptance Criteria

- Validates against schema.
- `result` = `PASS` only when all eight checks are `true`.
- `failed_checks` exactly matches the `false` checks.
- `rendering_blocked` consistent with `result`.

---

# 9.5.10 Storyboard Gate Report (`storyboard-gate-report`)

*Storyboard-level gate; runs only after every shot has passed.*

---

# Purpose

The storyboard gate report is the **storyboard-level verdict**, evaluated only after every shot has passed its own gate (9.5.9). It confirms composition, continuity, pacing, render balance, concept ratio, and emotional rhythm across the whole storyboard. Owner: **4.1.12**.

---

# Canonical Schema

```json
{
  "$schema": "https://json-schema.org/draft/2020-12/schema",
  "$id": "https://schemas.insynergy.co/cttp/v2.0/shot/storyboard-gate-report.schema.json",
  "title": "Storyboard Gate Report",
  "description": "Storyboard-level gate, post per-shot pass (Owner 4.1.12).",
  "type": "object",
  "properties": {
    "storyboard_id": { "$ref": "https://schemas.insynergy.co/cttp/v2.0/common/defs.schema.json#/$defs/StoryboardId" },
    "result": { "type": "string", "enum": ["PASS", "FAIL"] },
    "checks": {
      "type": "object",
      "properties": {
        "composition": { "type": "boolean" },
        "continuity": { "type": "boolean" },
        "pacing": { "type": "boolean" },
        "render_balance": { "type": "boolean" },
        "concept_ratio": { "type": "boolean" },
        "emotional_rhythm": { "type": "boolean" }
      },
      "required": ["composition", "continuity", "pacing", "render_balance", "concept_ratio", "emotional_rhythm"],
      "additionalProperties": false
    },
    "failed_checks": { "type": "array", "items": { "type": "string" } },
    "owning_sections": { "type": "object", "additionalProperties": { "type": "string" } },
    "rendering_blocked": { "type": "boolean" }
  },
  "required": ["storyboard_id", "result", "checks", "failed_checks", "owning_sections", "rendering_blocked"],
  "additionalProperties": false
}
```

---

# Field Reference

| Field | Type | Required | Owner | Description |
|---|---|---|---|---|
| `storyboard_id` | StoryboardId | yes | 4.1.12 | Storyboard being gated. |
| `result` | enum PASS/FAIL | yes | 4.1.12 | Overall verdict. |
| `checks.composition` | boolean | yes | 4.1.12 | Composition coherent across shots. |
| `checks.continuity` | boolean | yes | 4.1.12 | Continuity valid storyboard-wide. |
| `checks.pacing` | boolean | yes | 4.1.12 | Pacing acceptable. |
| `checks.render_balance` | boolean | yes | 4.1.12 | Render-strategy balance within caps. |
| `checks.concept_ratio` | boolean | yes | 4.1.12 | Concept ratio within bounds. |
| `checks.emotional_rhythm` | boolean | yes | 4.1.12 | Emotional rhythm sustained. |
| `failed_checks` | array[string] | yes | 4.1.12 | Names of failed checks. |
| `owning_sections` | object | yes | 4.1.12 | Map of check → owning section. |
| `rendering_blocked` | boolean | yes | 4.1.12 | Whether rendering is blocked. |

---

# Constraints & Invariants

- **INV-9.5.10-1** (P-623): this gate runs only after every shot gate (9.5.9) has `result = PASS`.
- **INV-9.5.10-2** (P-624): `result` is `PASS` iff all six `checks` are `true`; `failed_checks` lists the `false` ones and `rendering_blocked` is `true` iff `FAIL`.

---

# Example

```json
{
  "storyboard_id": "sbd-000-001",
  "result": "PASS",
  "checks": {
    "composition": true,
    "continuity": true,
    "pacing": true,
    "render_balance": true,
    "concept_ratio": true,
    "emotional_rhythm": true
  },
  "failed_checks": [],
  "owning_sections": {},
  "rendering_blocked": false
}
```

---

# Acceptance Criteria

- Validates against schema.
- Evaluated only after all per-shot gates pass.
- `result` = `PASS` only when all six checks are `true`.
- `rendering_blocked` consistent with `result`.

---

# 9.5.11 Shot Cache Key (`shot-cache-key`)

*Embedded deterministic re-plan key; any component change forces a full re-plan.*

---

# Purpose

The shot cache key is an **embedded deterministic key** derived from the inputs that fully determine a plan. It is `sha256` of the screenplay hash, shot-planner version, camera profile, character bible, and location bible. Any change to any component yields a new key, which forces a **full re-plan**. Owner: **4.1.13**. As an embedded value it does not carry the full ArtifactEnvelope.

---

# Canonical Schema

```json
{
  "$schema": "https://json-schema.org/draft/2020-12/schema",
  "$id": "https://schemas.insynergy.co/cttp/v2.0/shot/shot-cache-key.schema.json",
  "title": "Shot Cache Key",
  "description": "Embedded deterministic re-plan cache key (Owner 4.1.13).",
  "type": "object",
  "properties": {
    "cache_key": { "$ref": "https://schemas.insynergy.co/cttp/v2.0/common/defs.schema.json#/$defs/CacheKey" },
    "components": {
      "type": "object",
      "properties": {
        "screenplay_hash": { "$ref": "https://schemas.insynergy.co/cttp/v2.0/common/defs.schema.json#/$defs/ContentHash" },
        "shot_planner_version": { "type": "string" },
        "camera_profile": { "type": "string" },
        "character_bible": { "type": "string" },
        "location_bible": { "type": "string" }
      },
      "required": ["screenplay_hash", "shot_planner_version", "camera_profile", "character_bible", "location_bible"],
      "additionalProperties": false
    }
  },
  "required": ["cache_key", "components"],
  "additionalProperties": false
}
```

---

# Field Reference

| Field | Type | Required | Owner | Description |
|---|---|---|---|---|
| `cache_key` | CacheKey | yes | 4.1.13 | `sha256` over the ordered components. |
| `components.screenplay_hash` | ContentHash | yes | 4.1.13 | Hash of the source screenplay. |
| `components.shot_planner_version` | string | yes | 4.1.13 | Version of the Shot Planner. |
| `components.camera_profile` | string | yes | 4.1.13 | Camera profile identifier. |
| `components.character_bible` | string | yes | 4.1.13 | Character Bible identifier/hash. |
| `components.location_bible` | string | yes | 4.1.13 | Location Bible identifier/hash. |

---

# Constraints & Invariants

- **INV-9.5.11-1** (P-646): `cache_key = sha256(screenplay_hash + shot_planner_version + camera_profile + character_bible + location_bible)` over the components in this exact order.
- **INV-9.5.11-2** (P-647): any change to any component yields a different `cache_key`.
- **INV-9.5.11-3** (P-648): a changed `cache_key` forces a full re-plan (no partial reuse).
- **INV-9.5.11-4** (P-649): all five components are present and non-empty.

---

# Example

```json
{
  "cache_key": "sha256:9f3c0b7e2d1a4f68c5b9e0a7d2f4c1b8e6a3d0f9c2b5e8a1d4f7c0b3e6a9d2f5",
  "components": {
    "screenplay_hash": "sha256:41ab…",
    "shot_planner_version": "4.1.0",
    "camera_profile": "cttp-default-v2",
    "character_bible": "sha256:7d20…",
    "location_bible": "sha256:5c88…"
  }
}
```

---

# Acceptance Criteria

- Validates against schema.
- `cache_key` reproducible from the five components in the specified order.
- Any component change produces a new key and triggers a full re-plan.
- All components present and non-empty.

---
# 9.6 Rendering Platform Layer Schemas

### Part 9 — JSON Schema / Appendix · Insynergy Cinematic Thought Leadership Platform · Master Specification v2.0 · Part 5

---

# Purpose

This chapter formalizes, as JSON Schema (draft 2020-12), the **output and runtime artifacts** of the Rendering Platform (Part 5). Rendering is a closed-input, closed-output execution layer (RIO-301, RIO-302): it admits exactly six approved inputs — `shot-list`, `storyboard`, `camera-plan`, `render-strategy`, `character-bible`, and `location-bible` — and emits exactly the render manifest, queue snapshot, results roll-up, and build metadata, backed by three content-addressed asset directories.

Five of the six inputs are **governed by their producing layers' schemas** (9.3 Story/Screenplay, 9.5 Shot Planner / Storyboard) and are consumed here read-only under input immutability (RIO-305); they are not re-specified in 9.6. Only `location-bible` is treated as **render-owned** for the purpose of this appendix and is specified in 9.6.9. The four Rendering output documents, the runtime render-task record and state machine, the provider-independence boundary descriptor, and the deterministic prompt-assembly record are all specified here.

Where the Part 5 canonical block enumerates a field set explicitly, these schemas reproduce it faithfully (RIO-303). Where an output artifact is described by role rather than a fully enumerated field list, the schema is constructed conservatively from the annotated fields present and traced to its owning section (5.1.4 / 5.4.x).

# Design Philosophy

- **Planning before rendering (Principle 1).** Every render task exists in the manifest before it is enqueued; nothing is rendered from a partial or unapproved plan (RIO-307).
- **Rendering is provider-independent (5.3.1).** No provider-specific token appears above the interface; Runway is one provider among many, and the capability descriptor is the sole channel by which the core learns what a backend can do.
- **These schemas govern the render manifest, queue, results, and runtime state** — the execution ledger — never the approved creative plan, which they only reference by content hash.

The nine schemas:

- **9.6.1** `render-manifest.json` — authoritative runtime manifest: build header + per-task runtime state (5.1.4, 5.4.4).
- **9.6.2** `render-queue.json` — point-in-time snapshot of queued render tasks (5.1.4, 5.4.1).
- **9.6.3** `render-results.json` — final per-shot render outcomes (5.1.4).
- **9.6.4** `metadata.json` — build/render provenance and lineage index (5.1.4).
- **9.6.5** `render-task` — render task record and its state machine (5.4.3).
- **9.6.6** `provider-capability.yaml` — provider capability descriptor / independence boundary (5.3.2, 5.3.4).
- **9.6.7** `retry-policy` — retry, backoff, and failure-classification config (5.4.5).
- **9.6.8** `prompt-assembly` — deterministic prompt-assembly record (5.5.1).
- **9.6.9** `location-bible.yaml` — immutable location reference bible (5.1.4, 4.1.7).

Common definitions are referenced from `https://schemas.insynergy.co/cttp/v2.0/common/defs.schema.json` via `$ref` to its `$defs` (`SchemaVersion`, `BuildId`, `SceneId`, `ShotId`, `StoryboardId`, `RefId`, `ApprovalRef`, `ContentHash`, `CacheKey`, `Iso8601`, `DurationSeconds`, `Ratio`, `Score`, `RenderStrategy`, `BuildType`, `ArtifactEnvelope`). Sealed document artifacts compose `ArtifactEnvelope` via `allOf` and seal their surface with `unevaluatedProperties: false`.

---

# 9.6.1 render-manifest (`render-manifest.json`)

### The authoritative runtime ledger of the render run and its per-task runtime state. Owner: 5.1.4, 5.4.4.

---

# Purpose

`render-manifest.json` is the single authoritative source of render truth for a build (5.4.4). It records the build-level rollup, the strategy summary, and one per-task entry per shot carrying identity, current render state (5.4.3), attempt and transition history, produced asset references, validation outcome, cache key, and provenance. The on-disk sealed projection is owned by 5.1.4 (canonical block `rio-render-manifest`); the full runtime shape — build header plus `render_task_entry` — is owned by 5.4.4 (`rmf-build`, `rmf-task`). This schema is the union of both: the runtime manifest as written incrementally and sealed on build completion. Every field traces to 5.4.4 field-mutability classification; the manifest stores references and digests only — never prompt text, descriptions, secrets, or binary bytes.

---

# Canonical Schema

```json
{
  "$schema": "https://json-schema.org/draft/2020-12/schema",
  "$id": "https://schemas.insynergy.co/cttp/v2.0/render/render-manifest.schema.json",
  "title": "RenderManifest",
  "description": "Authoritative runtime render manifest for a single build. Owner: 5.1.4, 5.4.4.",
  "type": "object",
  "allOf": [
    { "$ref": "https://schemas.insynergy.co/cttp/v2.0/common/defs.schema.json#/$defs/ArtifactEnvelope" }
  ],
  "properties": {
    "schema_version": { "$ref": "https://schemas.insynergy.co/cttp/v2.0/common/defs.schema.json#/$defs/SchemaVersion" },
    "build_id": { "$ref": "https://schemas.insynergy.co/cttp/v2.0/common/defs.schema.json#/$defs/BuildId" },
    "input_admission_ref": { "type": "string", "minLength": 1, "description": "Reference to the passed precondition-gate admission record (RIO-307)." },
    "generated_at": { "$ref": "https://schemas.insynergy.co/cttp/v2.0/common/defs.schema.json#/$defs/Iso8601" },
    "sealed": { "type": "boolean", "description": "true once the build is complete; bytes immutable thereafter (RIO-306)." },
    "content_hash": { "$ref": "https://schemas.insynergy.co/cttp/v2.0/common/defs.schema.json#/$defs/ContentHash" },
    "manifest_meta": {
      "type": "object",
      "additionalProperties": false,
      "required": ["manifest_id", "build_id", "schema_version", "storyboard_ref", "render_strategy_ref", "created_at", "updated_at", "manifest_digest", "revision"],
      "properties": {
        "manifest_id": { "$ref": "https://schemas.insynergy.co/cttp/v2.0/common/defs.schema.json#/$defs/ContentHash", "description": "Deterministic: sha256(build_id + 'render_manifest'); immutable." },
        "build_id": { "$ref": "https://schemas.insynergy.co/cttp/v2.0/common/defs.schema.json#/$defs/BuildId" },
        "schema_version": { "$ref": "https://schemas.insynergy.co/cttp/v2.0/common/defs.schema.json#/$defs/SchemaVersion" },
        "storyboard_ref": { "$ref": "https://schemas.insynergy.co/cttp/v2.0/common/defs.schema.json#/$defs/ContentHash", "description": "Content hash of approved Storyboard; immutable." },
        "render_strategy_ref": { "$ref": "https://schemas.insynergy.co/cttp/v2.0/common/defs.schema.json#/$defs/ContentHash", "description": "Content hash of assigned Render Strategy; immutable." },
        "created_at": { "$ref": "https://schemas.insynergy.co/cttp/v2.0/common/defs.schema.json#/$defs/Iso8601" },
        "updated_at": { "$ref": "https://schemas.insynergy.co/cttp/v2.0/common/defs.schema.json#/$defs/Iso8601", "description": "Advances on every write." },
        "manifest_digest": { "$ref": "https://schemas.insynergy.co/cttp/v2.0/common/defs.schema.json#/$defs/ContentHash", "description": "Rolling content digest of the tasks map (tamper detection)." },
        "revision": { "type": "integer", "minimum": 0, "description": "Monotonic manifest revision counter." }
      }
    },
    "build": {
      "type": "object",
      "additionalProperties": false,
      "required": ["build_profile", "render_state", "total_tasks", "counts", "budget", "fail_closed"],
      "properties": {
        "build_profile": { "$ref": "https://schemas.insynergy.co/cttp/v2.0/common/defs.schema.json#/$defs/BuildType", "description": "preview | final; immutable per build." },
        "render_state": {
          "type": "string",
          "enum": ["PLANNING", "RENDERING", "VALIDATING", "READY", "BLOCKED", "COMPOSED"],
          "description": "Build-level rollup of task states (5.4.4)."
        },
        "total_tasks": { "type": "integer", "minimum": 0, "description": "Immutable once planning closes." },
        "counts": {
          "type": "object",
          "additionalProperties": false,
          "description": "Derived aggregate; must equal the sum of per-task states (RMF-401).",
          "required": ["new", "submitted", "running", "downloading", "validating", "ready", "composed", "failed", "retrying", "manual_review", "dead_letter", "cached"],
          "properties": {
            "new": { "type": "integer", "minimum": 0 },
            "submitted": { "type": "integer", "minimum": 0 },
            "running": { "type": "integer", "minimum": 0 },
            "downloading": { "type": "integer", "minimum": 0 },
            "validating": { "type": "integer", "minimum": 0 },
            "ready": { "type": "integer", "minimum": 0 },
            "composed": { "type": "integer", "minimum": 0 },
            "failed": { "type": "integer", "minimum": 0 },
            "retrying": { "type": "integer", "minimum": 0 },
            "manual_review": { "type": "integer", "minimum": 0 },
            "dead_letter": { "type": "integer", "minimum": 0 },
            "cached": { "type": "integer", "minimum": 0 }
          }
        },
        "budget": {
          "type": "object",
          "additionalProperties": false,
          "required": ["reserved", "consumed", "currency"],
          "properties": {
            "reserved": { "type": "number", "minimum": 0, "description": "Immutable reservation for the build." },
            "consumed": { "type": "number", "minimum": 0, "description": "Mutable; monotonically increasing." },
            "currency": { "type": "string", "const": "usd" }
          }
        },
        "fail_closed": { "type": "boolean", "const": true, "description": "Invariant flag; a partial trailer is never publishable (RMF-402)." },
        "blocked_reason": { "type": ["string", "null"], "description": "null unless render_state == BLOCKED." }
      }
    },
    "strategy_summary": {
      "type": "object",
      "additionalProperties": false,
      "description": "Per-strategy planned/completed/cached/cost rollup.",
      "properties": {
        "runway_video": { "$ref": "#/$defs/StrategyRollup" },
        "animated_still": { "$ref": "#/$defs/StrategyRollup" },
        "motion_graphics": { "$ref": "#/$defs/StrategyRollup" },
        "typography": { "$ref": "#/$defs/StrategyRollup" },
        "svg": { "$ref": "#/$defs/StrategyRollup" },
        "cached_asset": { "$ref": "#/$defs/StrategyRollup" }
      }
    },
    "tasks": {
      "type": "array",
      "description": "One render_task_entry per shot; authoritative render truth.",
      "minItems": 1,
      "items": { "$ref": "#/$defs/RenderTaskEntry" }
    }
  },
  "required": ["schema_version", "build_id", "input_admission_ref", "generated_at", "sealed", "content_hash", "manifest_meta", "build", "tasks"],
  "unevaluatedProperties": false,
  "$defs": {
    "StrategyRollup": {
      "type": "object",
      "additionalProperties": false,
      "properties": {
        "planned": { "type": "integer", "minimum": 0 },
        "completed": { "type": "integer", "minimum": 0 },
        "cached": { "type": "integer", "minimum": 0 },
        "cost": { "type": "number", "minimum": 0 }
      }
    },
    "RenderTaskEntry": {
      "type": "object",
      "additionalProperties": false,
      "required": ["render_task_id", "shot_id", "build_id", "strategy", "render_profile", "provider", "cache_key", "state", "attempt", "updated_at", "entry_revision"],
      "properties": {
        "render_task_id": { "$ref": "https://schemas.insynergy.co/cttp/v2.0/common/defs.schema.json#/$defs/ContentHash", "description": "Deterministic: sha256(build_id + shot_id); immutable." },
        "shot_id": { "$ref": "https://schemas.insynergy.co/cttp/v2.0/common/defs.schema.json#/$defs/ShotId" },
        "build_id": { "$ref": "https://schemas.insynergy.co/cttp/v2.0/common/defs.schema.json#/$defs/BuildId" },
        "scene_index": { "$ref": "https://schemas.insynergy.co/cttp/v2.0/common/defs.schema.json#/$defs/SceneId", "description": "Narrative position; immutable." },
        "shot_index": { "type": "integer", "minimum": 0, "description": "Immutable." },
        "strategy": { "$ref": "https://schemas.insynergy.co/cttp/v2.0/common/defs.schema.json#/$defs/RenderStrategy", "description": "Immutable; one of the fixed strategy set." },
        "render_profile": { "type": "string", "minLength": 1, "description": "e.g. runway_preview | runway_final; immutable." },
        "provider": { "type": "string", "enum": ["runway", "motion", "svg", "typography", "cache"], "description": "Immutable." },
        "cache_key": { "$ref": "https://schemas.insynergy.co/cttp/v2.0/common/defs.schema.json#/$defs/CacheKey", "description": "sha256 render cache key (5.6.3); immutable." },
        "state": {
          "type": "string",
          "enum": ["NEW", "SUBMITTED", "RUNNING", "DOWNLOADING", "VALIDATING", "READY", "COMPOSED", "FAILED", "RETRY", "MANUAL_REVIEW", "CANCELLED", "CACHED", "DEAD_LETTER"],
          "description": "Canonical per-shot render state (5.4.3); mutable, advances via legal transitions."
        },
        "attempt": { "type": "integer", "minimum": 1, "maximum": 4, "description": "Current attempt (1..max_retry+1)." },
        "provider_task_id": { "type": ["string", "null"], "description": "Provider-assigned job id for the current attempt; opaque; nullable." },
        "next_retry_at": { "oneOf": [{ "$ref": "https://schemas.insynergy.co/cttp/v2.0/common/defs.schema.json#/$defs/Iso8601" }, { "type": "null" }], "description": "Delayed re-admission timestamp; null unless RETRY." },
        "lease_ref": { "type": ["string", "null"], "description": "Current queue lease id (advisory mirror of 5.4.1); nullable." },
        "updated_at": { "$ref": "https://schemas.insynergy.co/cttp/v2.0/common/defs.schema.json#/$defs/Iso8601" },
        "entry_revision": { "type": "integer", "minimum": 0, "description": "Optimistic-concurrency version (RMF-408)." },
        "asset": {
          "type": "object",
          "additionalProperties": false,
          "description": "Append-on-success; written when a valid asset is produced.",
          "properties": {
            "asset_uri": { "type": ["string", "null"], "description": "Canonical location in Asset Repository; null until READY." },
            "asset_digest": { "oneOf": [{ "$ref": "https://schemas.insynergy.co/cttp/v2.0/common/defs.schema.json#/$defs/ContentHash" }, { "type": "null" }], "description": "sha256 of asset bytes; integrity anchor." },
            "content_type": { "type": "string", "description": "e.g. video/mp4 | image/png | image/svg+xml." },
            "duration_ms": { "type": "integer", "minimum": 0 },
            "resolution": { "type": "string", "pattern": "^[0-9]+x[0-9]+$" },
            "frame_rate": { "type": "number", "exclusiveMinimum": 0 },
            "codec": { "type": "string" },
            "produced_by_attempt": { "type": "integer", "minimum": 1 },
            "produced_at": { "$ref": "https://schemas.insynergy.co/cttp/v2.0/common/defs.schema.json#/$defs/Iso8601" }
          }
        },
        "validation": {
          "type": "object",
          "additionalProperties": false,
          "description": "Recorded by 5.6.",
          "properties": {
            "technical": { "type": "string", "enum": ["passed", "failed", "pending"], "description": "5.6.1." },
            "visual_quality_score": { "oneOf": [{ "$ref": "https://schemas.insynergy.co/cttp/v2.0/common/defs.schema.json#/$defs/Score" }, { "type": "null" }], "description": "0.00-1.00; null until validated (5.6.2)." },
            "visual_quality_passed": { "type": "boolean", "description": "score >= 0.90." },
            "checks": { "type": "object", "additionalProperties": true, "description": "resolution/duration/codec/frame_rate/decode/integrity." },
            "validated_at": { "$ref": "https://schemas.insynergy.co/cttp/v2.0/common/defs.schema.json#/$defs/Iso8601" },
            "validated_by_attempt": { "type": "integer", "minimum": 1 }
          }
        },
        "history": {
          "type": "array",
          "description": "Append-only attempt/transition history (RMF-305).",
          "items": {
            "type": "object",
            "additionalProperties": false,
            "required": ["attempt", "from_state", "to_state", "transition", "at"],
            "properties": {
              "attempt": { "type": "integer", "minimum": 1 },
              "from_state": { "type": "string" },
              "to_state": { "type": "string" },
              "transition": { "type": "string", "description": "e.g. submit | poll | download | validate | fail | retry." },
              "failure_class": { "type": ["string", "null"], "enum": ["transient", "permanent", "quality", "budget", null], "description": "5.4.5." },
              "provider_task_id": { "type": ["string", "null"] },
              "reason": { "type": ["string", "null"] },
              "at": { "$ref": "https://schemas.insynergy.co/cttp/v2.0/common/defs.schema.json#/$defs/Iso8601" }
            }
          }
        },
        "provenance": {
          "type": "object",
          "additionalProperties": false,
          "description": "Immutable once written.",
          "properties": {
            "storyboard_shot_ref": { "$ref": "https://schemas.insynergy.co/cttp/v2.0/common/defs.schema.json#/$defs/ContentHash", "description": "Content hash of the source Storyboard shot." },
            "render_strategy_ref": { "$ref": "https://schemas.insynergy.co/cttp/v2.0/common/defs.schema.json#/$defs/ContentHash" },
            "prompt_digest": { "$ref": "https://schemas.insynergy.co/cttp/v2.0/common/defs.schema.json#/$defs/ContentHash", "description": "Digest of the assembled prompt (5.5); NOT prompt text." },
            "provider_version": { "type": "string", "description": "Provider/model version used (feeds cache_key, 5.6.3)." },
            "upstream_cache_hit": { "type": "boolean" },
            "source_asset_task_id": { "type": ["string", "null"] }
          }
        }
      }
    }
  }
}
```

---

# Field Reference

| Field | Type | Req | Notes |
| --- | --- | --- | --- |
| `schema_version` | SchemaVersion | yes | Manifest schema version (envelope). |
| `build_id` | BuildId | yes | Build scope; consistent across inputs (RIO-308). |
| `input_admission_ref` | string | yes | Ref to passed precondition-gate record. |
| `generated_at` | Iso8601 | yes | Manifest emission time. |
| `sealed` | boolean | yes | true once build complete; bytes immutable (RIO-306). |
| `content_hash` | ContentHash | yes | Fixity over the sealed body. |
| `manifest_meta` | object | yes | Deterministic ids, refs, revision counter, rolling digest. |
| `build` | object | yes | Build-level rollup: profile, render_state, counts, budget, fail_closed. |
| `strategy_summary` | object | no | Per-strategy planned/completed/cached/cost. |
| `tasks[]` | RenderTaskEntry | yes | One entry per shot; authoritative per-task state. |
| `tasks[].render_task_id` | ContentHash | yes | sha256(build_id + shot_id); immutable. |
| `tasks[].state` | enum | yes | 5.4.3 canonical state (+ DEAD_LETTER disposition). |
| `tasks[].attempt` | integer 1..4 | yes | Bounded by max_retry+1. |
| `tasks[].asset` | object | no | Append-on-success; URI + digest + technical metadata. |
| `tasks[].validation` | object | no | technical + visual_quality_score (5.6). |
| `tasks[].history[]` | array | no | Append-only transition/attempt log. |
| `tasks[].provenance` | object | no | Immutable lineage: storyboard/strategy refs, prompt_digest. |

---

# Constraints & Invariants

- **INV-9.6.1-1 (RIO-306 / RMF-406).** When `sealed = true`, the manifest bytes are immutable; a re-render produces a new `build_id`-scoped manifest, never an in-place edit of a sealed one.
- **INV-9.6.1-2 (RMF-401).** `build.counts.*` is a derived projection and must equal the sum of per-task `state` values; on disagreement the tasks map wins.
- **INV-9.6.1-3 (RMF-402 / Fail Closed).** `build.render_state` never advances to `READY` or `COMPOSED` while any task is in `FAILED`, `MANUAL_REVIEW`, or `DEAD_LETTER`; `build.fail_closed` is `true`.
- **INV-9.6.1-4 (RTS-305 / RTB-402).** `tasks[].attempt` never exceeds 4 (`max_retry + 1`).
- **INV-9.6.1-5 (RMF-405).** Immutable fields (`render_task_id`, `shot_id`, `strategy`, `render_profile`, `provider`, `cache_key`, `provenance.*`) are set once; `history[]` is append-only; `state` moves only via legal transitions (5.4.3).
- **INV-9.6.1-6 (RIO-309/310).** No prompt text, descriptions, secrets, or binary bytes are stored; only references and digests.

---

# Example

```json
{
  "schema_version": "2.0.0",
  "build_id": "bld_2026_07_20_a1",
  "input_admission_ref": "adm_bld_2026_07_20_a1",
  "generated_at": "2026-07-20T09:14:02Z",
  "sealed": true,
  "content_hash": "sha256:5c1e...manifest",
  "manifest_meta": {
    "manifest_id": "sha256:9ab0...mid",
    "build_id": "bld_2026_07_20_a1",
    "schema_version": "2.0.0",
    "storyboard_ref": "sha256:11aa...sb",
    "render_strategy_ref": "sha256:22bb...rs",
    "created_at": "2026-07-20T09:00:00Z",
    "updated_at": "2026-07-20T09:14:02Z",
    "manifest_digest": "sha256:33cc...dig",
    "revision": 47
  },
  "build": {
    "build_profile": "final",
    "render_state": "COMPOSED",
    "total_tasks": 2,
    "counts": { "new": 0, "submitted": 0, "running": 0, "downloading": 0, "validating": 0, "ready": 0, "composed": 2, "failed": 0, "retrying": 0, "manual_review": 0, "dead_letter": 0, "cached": 0 },
    "budget": { "reserved": 12.0, "consumed": 7.4, "currency": "usd" },
    "fail_closed": true,
    "blocked_reason": null
  },
  "strategy_summary": {
    "runway_video": { "planned": 1, "completed": 1, "cached": 0, "cost": 6.2 },
    "typography": { "planned": 1, "completed": 1, "cached": 0, "cost": 1.2 }
  },
  "tasks": [
    {
      "render_task_id": "sha256:aa01...t1",
      "shot_id": "sh_0007",
      "build_id": "bld_2026_07_20_a1",
      "scene_index": "sc_002",
      "shot_index": 7,
      "strategy": "runway_video",
      "render_profile": "runway_final",
      "provider": "runway",
      "cache_key": "sha256:ck07...",
      "state": "COMPOSED",
      "attempt": 1,
      "provider_task_id": "rw_job_88af",
      "next_retry_at": null,
      "lease_ref": null,
      "updated_at": "2026-07-20T09:12:40Z",
      "entry_revision": 9,
      "asset": {
        "asset_uri": "video_assets/sh_0007.sha256-abc.mp4",
        "asset_digest": "sha256:abc...bytes",
        "content_type": "video/mp4",
        "duration_ms": 4000,
        "resolution": "1920x1080",
        "frame_rate": 24,
        "codec": "h264",
        "produced_by_attempt": 1,
        "produced_at": "2026-07-20T09:11:10Z"
      },
      "validation": {
        "technical": "passed",
        "visual_quality_score": 0.94,
        "visual_quality_passed": true,
        "checks": { "resolution": "pass", "codec": "pass", "integrity": "pass" },
        "validated_at": "2026-07-20T09:11:30Z",
        "validated_by_attempt": 1
      },
      "history": [
        { "attempt": 1, "from_state": "NEW", "to_state": "SUBMITTED", "transition": "submit", "failure_class": null, "provider_task_id": "rw_job_88af", "reason": null, "at": "2026-07-20T09:02:00Z" },
        { "attempt": 1, "from_state": "VALIDATING", "to_state": "READY", "transition": "validate", "failure_class": null, "provider_task_id": "rw_job_88af", "reason": null, "at": "2026-07-20T09:11:30Z" }
      ],
      "provenance": {
        "storyboard_shot_ref": "sha256:sbshot07",
        "render_strategy_ref": "sha256:22bb...rs",
        "prompt_digest": "sha256:pmt07...",
        "provider_version": "runway-gen3:2026.05",
        "upstream_cache_hit": false,
        "source_asset_task_id": null
      }
    }
  ]
}
```

---

# Acceptance Criteria

- Validates against draft 2020-12; composes `ArtifactEnvelope`; `unevaluatedProperties: false` on the root.
- `tasks[].state` is drawn only from the closed state set; `attempt` is 1..4.
- `build.counts` present with all twelve state counters; `build.fail_closed` is `true`.
- A sealed manifest that mutates an immutable field or edits `history[]` is rejected (INV-9.6.1-5).
- Every `tasks[]` entry carries a `cache_key` and `render_task_id` derivable from `build_id`/`shot_id`.

---

# 9.6.2 render-queue (`render-queue.json`)

### A point-in-time observability snapshot of the queued render tasks. Owner: 5.1.4, 5.4.1.

---

# Purpose

`render-queue.json` is a point-in-time snapshot of queue state for observability and crash recovery (5.1.4, canonical block `rio-render-queue`). It is **not** the authoritative source of render truth — the manifest is (5.4.1) — and queue state must be reconstructable from the manifest, retry schedule, leases, and provider records even if a snapshot is lost. It records queue depth per class and, optionally, item references only: never prompts, secrets, or binary payloads (RIO-309, RIO-310). Queue classes are the closed set defined in 5.4.1.

---

# Canonical Schema

```json
{
  "$schema": "https://json-schema.org/draft/2020-12/schema",
  "$id": "https://schemas.insynergy.co/cttp/v2.0/render/render-queue.schema.json",
  "title": "RenderQueue",
  "description": "Point-in-time snapshot of render queue state. Owner: 5.1.4, 5.4.1.",
  "type": "object",
  "allOf": [
    { "$ref": "https://schemas.insynergy.co/cttp/v2.0/common/defs.schema.json#/$defs/ArtifactEnvelope" }
  ],
  "properties": {
    "schema_version": { "$ref": "https://schemas.insynergy.co/cttp/v2.0/common/defs.schema.json#/$defs/SchemaVersion" },
    "build_id": { "$ref": "https://schemas.insynergy.co/cttp/v2.0/common/defs.schema.json#/$defs/BuildId" },
    "snapshot_at": { "$ref": "https://schemas.insynergy.co/cttp/v2.0/common/defs.schema.json#/$defs/Iso8601", "description": "Time of snapshot." },
    "content_hash": { "$ref": "https://schemas.insynergy.co/cttp/v2.0/common/defs.schema.json#/$defs/ContentHash" },
    "queues": {
      "type": "array",
      "description": "Depth per queue class.",
      "minItems": 1,
      "items": {
        "type": "object",
        "additionalProperties": false,
        "required": ["queue_class", "depth"],
        "properties": {
          "queue_class": {
            "type": "string",
            "enum": ["READY", "SUBMISSION", "PROVIDER_MONITOR", "DOWNLOAD", "VALIDATION", "RETRY", "CONTROL", "MANUAL_REVIEW", "DEAD_LETTER"],
            "description": "One of the fixed queue classes (5.4.1)."
          },
          "depth": { "type": "integer", "minimum": 0 },
          "items": {
            "type": "array",
            "description": "References only, never payloads (RIO-309, RIO-310).",
            "items": {
              "type": "object",
              "additionalProperties": false,
              "required": ["render_task_id", "shot_id", "attempt"],
              "properties": {
                "render_task_id": { "$ref": "https://schemas.insynergy.co/cttp/v2.0/common/defs.schema.json#/$defs/ContentHash" },
                "shot_id": { "$ref": "https://schemas.insynergy.co/cttp/v2.0/common/defs.schema.json#/$defs/ShotId" },
                "attempt": { "type": "integer", "minimum": 1, "maximum": 4 },
                "visible_at": { "$ref": "https://schemas.insynergy.co/cttp/v2.0/common/defs.schema.json#/$defs/Iso8601", "description": "Delayed-visibility target (retry backoff)." }
              }
            }
          }
        }
      }
    }
  },
  "required": ["schema_version", "build_id", "snapshot_at", "content_hash", "queues"],
  "unevaluatedProperties": false
}
```

---

# Field Reference

| Field | Type | Req | Notes |
| --- | --- | --- | --- |
| `schema_version` | SchemaVersion | yes | Envelope. |
| `build_id` | BuildId | yes | Build scope. |
| `snapshot_at` | Iso8601 | yes | Time of snapshot. |
| `content_hash` | ContentHash | yes | Fixity over the snapshot. |
| `queues[]` | array | yes | One entry per queue class present. |
| `queues[].queue_class` | enum | yes | READY..DEAD_LETTER (closed set). |
| `queues[].depth` | integer | yes | Queue depth. |
| `queues[].items[]` | array | no | Reference-only item projection. |
| `queues[].items[].render_task_id` | ContentHash | yes | Task reference. |
| `queues[].items[].shot_id` | ShotId | yes | Shot reference. |
| `queues[].items[].attempt` | integer 1..4 | yes | Attempt number. |
| `queues[].items[].visible_at` | Iso8601 | no | Delayed-visibility time. |

---

# Constraints & Invariants

- **INV-9.6.2-1 (5.4.1 governing principle).** The snapshot is not authoritative; the manifest is. Nothing here may contradict the manifest, and queue state must be reconstructable without it.
- **INV-9.6.2-2 (RIO-309, RIO-310).** `items[]` carry references only; a payload, prompt, or secret in a queue item is a violation.
- **INV-9.6.2-3 (RIO-306).** A snapshot is immutable once written; a later snapshot is a new file/version.
- **INV-9.6.2-4 (5.4.1).** Every item belongs to exactly one `queue_class` drawn from the closed set.

---

# Example

```json
{
  "schema_version": "2.0.0",
  "build_id": "bld_2026_07_20_a1",
  "snapshot_at": "2026-07-20T09:05:12Z",
  "content_hash": "sha256:queue...snap",
  "queues": [
    { "queue_class": "READY", "depth": 0, "items": [] },
    {
      "queue_class": "PROVIDER_MONITOR",
      "depth": 1,
      "items": [
        { "render_task_id": "sha256:aa01...t1", "shot_id": "sh_0007", "attempt": 1, "visible_at": "2026-07-20T09:05:32Z" }
      ]
    },
    { "queue_class": "DEAD_LETTER", "depth": 0 }
  ]
}
```

---

# Acceptance Criteria

- Validates against draft 2020-12; composes `ArtifactEnvelope`; `unevaluatedProperties: false`.
- `queue_class` restricted to the nine closed classes.
- `items[]` reject any property beyond the four reference fields.
- Snapshot re-emission produces a new document, never an in-place edit.

---

# 9.6.3 render-results (`render-results.json`)

### The final per-shot render outcome roll-up consumed by Composition. Owner: 5.1.4.

---

# Purpose

`render-results.json` is the settled conclusion of a render run (5.1.4, canonical block `rio-render-results`): for each shot, what was ultimately produced and whether it passed. Where the manifest is the process record, this is the outcome roll-up consumed by Composition. `quality_score` reflects the visual quality validation of 5.6.2 (`minimum_score: 0.90`). It is sealed on build completion and immutable thereafter (RIO-306). A shot that could not meet the quality threshold after `max_retry` (3) attempts is recorded as `manual_review` or `failed`, honouring Fail Closed.

---

# Canonical Schema

```json
{
  "$schema": "https://json-schema.org/draft/2020-12/schema",
  "$id": "https://schemas.insynergy.co/cttp/v2.0/render/render-results.schema.json",
  "title": "RenderResults",
  "description": "Final per-shot render outcome roll-up. Owner: 5.1.4.",
  "type": "object",
  "allOf": [
    { "$ref": "https://schemas.insynergy.co/cttp/v2.0/common/defs.schema.json#/$defs/ArtifactEnvelope" }
  ],
  "properties": {
    "schema_version": { "$ref": "https://schemas.insynergy.co/cttp/v2.0/common/defs.schema.json#/$defs/SchemaVersion" },
    "build_id": { "$ref": "https://schemas.insynergy.co/cttp/v2.0/common/defs.schema.json#/$defs/BuildId" },
    "input_admission_ref": { "type": "string", "minLength": 1, "description": "The inputs this result derives from (RIO-304)." },
    "generated_at": { "$ref": "https://schemas.insynergy.co/cttp/v2.0/common/defs.schema.json#/$defs/Iso8601" },
    "sealed": { "type": "boolean" },
    "content_hash": { "$ref": "https://schemas.insynergy.co/cttp/v2.0/common/defs.schema.json#/$defs/ContentHash" },
    "overall_status": {
      "type": "string",
      "enum": ["complete", "partial_blocked", "failed"],
      "description": "Build-level outcome."
    },
    "shots": {
      "type": "array",
      "description": "One final outcome per shot.",
      "minItems": 1,
      "items": {
        "type": "object",
        "additionalProperties": false,
        "required": ["shot_id", "outcome", "strategy", "attempts_used"],
        "properties": {
          "shot_id": { "$ref": "https://schemas.insynergy.co/cttp/v2.0/common/defs.schema.json#/$defs/ShotId" },
          "outcome": {
            "type": "string",
            "enum": ["rendered", "cache_hit", "manual_review", "failed"],
            "description": "Final disposition for the shot."
          },
          "strategy": { "$ref": "https://schemas.insynergy.co/cttp/v2.0/common/defs.schema.json#/$defs/RenderStrategy", "description": "The strategy actually used." },
          "chosen_asset_uri": { "type": "string", "description": "Final asset in video_assets/; absent if none passed." },
          "preview_asset_uri": { "type": "string", "description": "Asset in preview_assets/." },
          "thumbnail_uri": { "type": "string", "description": "Asset in thumbnail_assets/." },
          "quality_score": { "$ref": "https://schemas.insynergy.co/cttp/v2.0/common/defs.schema.json#/$defs/Score", "description": "Visual quality score (5.6.2); optional." },
          "attempts_used": { "type": "integer", "minimum": 0, "maximum": 4 }
        }
      }
    }
  },
  "required": ["schema_version", "build_id", "input_admission_ref", "generated_at", "sealed", "content_hash", "overall_status", "shots"],
  "unevaluatedProperties": false
}
```

---

# Field Reference

| Field | Type | Req | Notes |
| --- | --- | --- | --- |
| `schema_version` | SchemaVersion | yes | Envelope. |
| `build_id` | BuildId | yes | Build scope. |
| `input_admission_ref` | string | yes | Inputs this result derives from (RIO-304). |
| `generated_at` | Iso8601 | yes | Emission time. |
| `sealed` | boolean | yes | Sealed on build completion. |
| `content_hash` | ContentHash | yes | Fixity. |
| `overall_status` | enum | yes | complete \| partial_blocked \| failed. |
| `shots[]` | array | yes | One final outcome per shot. |
| `shots[].shot_id` | ShotId | yes | Shot reference. |
| `shots[].outcome` | enum | yes | rendered \| cache_hit \| manual_review \| failed. |
| `shots[].strategy` | RenderStrategy | yes | Strategy actually used. |
| `shots[].chosen_asset_uri` | string | no | Final asset; absent if none passed. |
| `shots[].preview_asset_uri` | string | no | Preview asset. |
| `shots[].thumbnail_uri` | string | no | Thumbnail/poster frame. |
| `shots[].quality_score` | Score | no | ≥ 0.90 for a passing shot (5.6.2). |
| `shots[].attempts_used` | integer 0..4 | yes | Attempts consumed. |

---

# Constraints & Invariants

- **INV-9.6.3-1 (RIO-306).** Sealed on build completion; immutable thereafter.
- **INV-9.6.3-2 (Fail Closed / RTB-407).** A shot below the 0.90 threshold after `max_retry` (3) attempts records `outcome: manual_review` or `failed`; a substandard shot is never presented as `rendered`.
- **INV-9.6.3-3 (RIO-302 / 5.1.4).** The `shots` set is bijective with the shot-list shot set; every shot has exactly one outcome.
- **INV-9.6.3-4.** `attempts_used` never exceeds 4 (`max_retry + 1`).
- **INV-9.6.3-5 (RIO-310).** Asset URIs reference content-addressed files; no bytes are embedded.

---

# Example

```json
{
  "schema_version": "2.0.0",
  "build_id": "bld_2026_07_20_a1",
  "input_admission_ref": "adm_bld_2026_07_20_a1",
  "generated_at": "2026-07-20T09:14:05Z",
  "sealed": true,
  "content_hash": "sha256:results...",
  "overall_status": "complete",
  "shots": [
    {
      "shot_id": "sh_0007",
      "outcome": "rendered",
      "strategy": "runway_video",
      "chosen_asset_uri": "video_assets/sh_0007.sha256-abc.mp4",
      "preview_asset_uri": "preview_assets/sh_0007.sha256-def.mp4",
      "thumbnail_uri": "thumbnail_assets/sh_0007.sha256-ghi.png",
      "quality_score": 0.94,
      "attempts_used": 1
    },
    {
      "shot_id": "sh_0008",
      "outcome": "cache_hit",
      "strategy": "typography",
      "chosen_asset_uri": "video_assets/sh_0008.sha256-jkl.mp4",
      "attempts_used": 0
    }
  ]
}
```

---

# Acceptance Criteria

- Validates against draft 2020-12; composes `ArtifactEnvelope`; `unevaluatedProperties: false`.
- `outcome` and `overall_status` restricted to their closed enums.
- Asset URIs and `quality_score` optional; every other shot field required.
- A `rendered` outcome without a `chosen_asset_uri` is rejected by profile validation (semantic check downstream of schema).

---

# 9.6.4 metadata (`metadata.json`)

### The build/render provenance and lineage index binding outputs to inputs. Owner: 5.1.4.

---

# Purpose

`metadata.json` is the lineage document that binds every output to the exact input set (by verified `content_hash`) and to the provider versions used (5.1.4, canonical block `rio-metadata`). It answers "what produced this trailer, from which approved plan, with which provider versions." It is sealed on build completion and immutable thereafter (RIO-306). Its `input_lineage[].content_hash` values are copied from the precondition gate's admission record, making the input→output binding non-repudiable (RIO-304, RIO-308).

---

# Canonical Schema

```json
{
  "$schema": "https://json-schema.org/draft/2020-12/schema",
  "$id": "https://schemas.insynergy.co/cttp/v2.0/render/metadata.schema.json",
  "title": "RenderMetadata",
  "description": "Build/render provenance and lineage index. Owner: 5.1.4.",
  "type": "object",
  "allOf": [
    { "$ref": "https://schemas.insynergy.co/cttp/v2.0/common/defs.schema.json#/$defs/ArtifactEnvelope" }
  ],
  "properties": {
    "schema_version": { "$ref": "https://schemas.insynergy.co/cttp/v2.0/common/defs.schema.json#/$defs/SchemaVersion" },
    "build_id": { "$ref": "https://schemas.insynergy.co/cttp/v2.0/common/defs.schema.json#/$defs/BuildId" },
    "generated_at": { "$ref": "https://schemas.insynergy.co/cttp/v2.0/common/defs.schema.json#/$defs/Iso8601" },
    "sealed": { "type": "boolean" },
    "content_hash": { "$ref": "https://schemas.insynergy.co/cttp/v2.0/common/defs.schema.json#/$defs/ContentHash" },
    "producer": {
      "type": "object",
      "additionalProperties": false,
      "required": ["component", "version"],
      "properties": {
        "component": { "type": "string", "const": "RenderingPlatform" },
        "version": { "type": "string", "minLength": 1, "description": "Rendering platform version." }
      }
    },
    "input_lineage": {
      "type": "array",
      "description": "Exact inputs consumed, by verified content hash (RIO-304, RIO-308).",
      "minItems": 1,
      "items": {
        "type": "object",
        "additionalProperties": false,
        "required": ["artifact", "content_hash", "producer", "approval_ref"],
        "properties": {
          "artifact": { "type": "string", "minLength": 1, "description": "e.g. shot-list.json." },
          "content_hash": { "$ref": "https://schemas.insynergy.co/cttp/v2.0/common/defs.schema.json#/$defs/ContentHash", "description": "Verified at the precondition gate." },
          "producer": { "type": "string", "minLength": 1, "description": "Upstream engine." },
          "approval_ref": { "$ref": "https://schemas.insynergy.co/cttp/v2.0/common/defs.schema.json#/$defs/ApprovalRef" }
        }
      }
    },
    "provider_versions": {
      "type": "array",
      "description": "Provider + model versions used.",
      "items": {
        "type": "object",
        "additionalProperties": false,
        "required": ["provider", "provider_version"],
        "properties": {
          "provider": { "type": "string", "minLength": 1 },
          "provider_version": { "type": "string", "minLength": 1 }
        }
      }
    },
    "output_index": {
      "type": "object",
      "additionalProperties": false,
      "description": "The sealed output set.",
      "required": ["render_manifest", "render_results", "render_queue", "asset_directories"],
      "properties": {
        "render_manifest": { "$ref": "https://schemas.insynergy.co/cttp/v2.0/common/defs.schema.json#/$defs/ContentHash" },
        "render_results": { "$ref": "https://schemas.insynergy.co/cttp/v2.0/common/defs.schema.json#/$defs/ContentHash" },
        "render_queue": { "$ref": "https://schemas.insynergy.co/cttp/v2.0/common/defs.schema.json#/$defs/ContentHash" },
        "asset_directories": { "type": "array", "items": { "type": "string" }, "description": "video_assets/ preview_assets/ thumbnail_assets/." }
      }
    }
  },
  "required": ["schema_version", "build_id", "generated_at", "sealed", "content_hash", "producer", "input_lineage", "provider_versions", "output_index"],
  "unevaluatedProperties": false
}
```

---

# Field Reference

| Field | Type | Req | Notes |
| --- | --- | --- | --- |
| `schema_version` | SchemaVersion | yes | Envelope. |
| `build_id` | BuildId | yes | Build scope. |
| `generated_at` | Iso8601 | yes | Emission time. |
| `sealed` | boolean | yes | Sealed on completion. |
| `content_hash` | ContentHash | yes | Fixity. |
| `producer` | object | yes | `component = RenderingPlatform` + version. |
| `input_lineage[]` | array | yes | Exact inputs with verified hashes and approvals. |
| `provider_versions[]` | array | yes | Provider + model versions used. |
| `output_index` | object | yes | Sealed output-set hashes + asset directories. |

---

# Constraints & Invariants

- **INV-9.6.4-1 (RIO-304, RIO-308).** `input_lineage[].content_hash` values are copied verbatim from the precondition-gate admission record; they must verify against the referenced input artifacts.
- **INV-9.6.4-2 (RIO-306).** Sealed on build completion; immutable thereafter.
- **INV-9.6.4-3 (5.1.4).** `producer.component` is exactly `RenderingPlatform`.
- **INV-9.6.4-4 (RIO-301).** `input_lineage` enumerates only the six admitted inputs; no other artifact appears.

---

# Example

```json
{
  "schema_version": "2.0.0",
  "build_id": "bld_2026_07_20_a1",
  "generated_at": "2026-07-20T09:14:06Z",
  "sealed": true,
  "content_hash": "sha256:meta...",
  "producer": { "component": "RenderingPlatform", "version": "5.0.3" },
  "input_lineage": [
    { "artifact": "shot-list.json", "content_hash": "sha256:sl...", "producer": "ShotPlanner", "approval_ref": "qg_shotlist_a1" },
    { "artifact": "storyboard.json", "content_hash": "sha256:sb...", "producer": "StoryboardEngine", "approval_ref": "qg_storyboard_a1" },
    { "artifact": "location-bible.yaml", "content_hash": "sha256:lb...", "producer": "LocationEngine", "approval_ref": "qg_locbible_a1" }
  ],
  "provider_versions": [
    { "provider": "runway", "provider_version": "gen3:2026.05" }
  ],
  "output_index": {
    "render_manifest": "sha256:5c1e...manifest",
    "render_results": "sha256:results...",
    "render_queue": "sha256:queue...snap",
    "asset_directories": ["video_assets/", "preview_assets/", "thumbnail_assets/"]
  }
}
```

---

# Acceptance Criteria

- Validates against draft 2020-12; composes `ArtifactEnvelope`; `unevaluatedProperties: false`.
- `producer.component` fixed to `RenderingPlatform`.
- Every `input_lineage[]` entry carries `content_hash` and `approval_ref`.
- `output_index` enumerates all three document hashes plus the three asset directories.

---

# 9.6.5 render-task (`render-task.schema.json`)

### The render task record and its state machine. Owner: 5.4.3.

---

# Purpose

The render task is the unit of rendering work: exactly one render task exists per shot per render profile (5.4.3). This schema fixes the task **record** — its immutable identity, its current state drawn from the closed render-task state enum, its attempt counter (separated from state per RTS-305), and its transition history — as the state-machine projection of the manifest per-task entry (5.4.4). The state and its legal transitions are owned by 5.4.3; the manifest is the authoritative store. The record deliberately holds references and digests, never prompts, descriptions, secrets, or bytes.

---

# Canonical Schema

```json
{
  "$schema": "https://json-schema.org/draft/2020-12/schema",
  "$id": "https://schemas.insynergy.co/cttp/v2.0/render/render-task.schema.json",
  "title": "RenderTask",
  "description": "Render task record and state-machine projection. Owner: 5.4.3.",
  "type": "object",
  "additionalProperties": false,
  "required": ["task_id", "shot_id", "build_id", "strategy", "render_profile", "provider", "cache_key", "state", "attempt", "max_attempts"],
  "properties": {
    "task_id": { "$ref": "https://schemas.insynergy.co/cttp/v2.0/common/defs.schema.json#/$defs/ContentHash", "description": "Deterministic: sha256(build_id + shot_id); immutable." },
    "shot_id": { "$ref": "https://schemas.insynergy.co/cttp/v2.0/common/defs.schema.json#/$defs/ShotId", "description": "References the approved Storyboard shot; immutable." },
    "build_id": { "$ref": "https://schemas.insynergy.co/cttp/v2.0/common/defs.schema.json#/$defs/BuildId" },
    "strategy": { "$ref": "https://schemas.insynergy.co/cttp/v2.0/common/defs.schema.json#/$defs/RenderStrategy", "description": "Assigned strategy; immutable; one per shot (no mixed strategies)." },
    "render_profile": { "type": "string", "minLength": 1, "description": "e.g. runway_preview | runway_final; immutable." },
```
