```json
    "provider": { "type": "string", "enum": ["runway", "motion", "svg", "typography", "cache"], "description": "Immutable." },
    "cache_key": { "$ref": "https://schemas.insynergy.co/cttp/v2.0/common/defs.schema.json#/$defs/CacheKey", "description": "Render cache key (5.6.3) and idempotency anchor; immutable." },
    "state": {
      "type": "string",
      "enum": ["NEW", "SUBMITTED", "RUNNING", "DOWNLOADING", "VALIDATING", "READY", "COMPOSED", "FAILED", "RETRY", "MANUAL_REVIEW", "CANCELLED", "CACHED"],
      "description": "Closed render-task state enum (5.4.3). Exactly one at all times."
    },
    "attempt": { "type": "integer", "minimum": 1, "maximum": 4, "description": "Current render attempt (1 = original). Separated from state (RTS-305)." },
    "max_attempts": { "type": "integer", "const": 4, "description": "max_retry + 1." },
    "attempts_remaining": { "type": "integer", "minimum": 0, "maximum": 3, "description": "max_attempts - attempt." },
    "delivery_count": { "type": "integer", "minimum": 0, "description": "Transport deliveries (informational; never gates retry)." },
    "provider_task_id": { "type": ["string", "null"], "description": "Provider job id for the current attempt; opaque; null pre-submit." },
    "next_retry_at": { "oneOf": [{ "$ref": "https://schemas.insynergy.co/cttp/v2.0/common/defs.schema.json#/$defs/Iso8601" }, { "type": "null" }], "description": "Delayed re-admission time; null unless RETRY." },
    "last_failure_code": { "type": ["string", "null"], "description": "Most recent classified failure code (5.4.5)." },
    "terminal": { "type": "boolean", "description": "true when state is COMPOSED | CACHED | MANUAL_REVIEW | CANCELLED." },
    "created_at": { "$ref": "https://schemas.insynergy.co/cttp/v2.0/common/defs.schema.json#/$defs/Iso8601" },
    "updated_at": { "$ref": "https://schemas.insynergy.co/cttp/v2.0/common/defs.schema.json#/$defs/Iso8601" },
    "history": {
      "type": "array",
      "description": "Append-only transition log (RTS-304 idempotent transitions).",
      "items": {
        "type": "object",
        "additionalProperties": false,
        "required": ["attempt", "from_state", "to_state", "event", "at"],
        "properties": {
          "attempt": { "type": "integer", "minimum": 1 },
          "from_state": { "type": "string" },
          "to_state": { "type": "string" },
          "event": {
            "type": "string",
            "enum": ["CREATE", "CACHE_HIT", "SUBMIT_OK", "SUBMIT_FAIL", "PROVIDER_RUNNING", "PROVIDER_SUCCEEDED", "PROVIDER_FAILED", "DOWNLOAD_OK", "DOWNLOAD_FAIL", "VALIDATE_OK", "VALIDATE_FAIL", "COMPOSE_OK", "RETRY_AUTHORIZED", "RETRY_EXHAUSTED", "NON_RETRYABLE", "RE_SUBMIT", "TIMEOUT", "CANCEL"],
            "description": "Driving event (5.4.3)."
          },
          "at": { "$ref": "https://schemas.insynergy.co/cttp/v2.0/common/defs.schema.json#/$defs/Iso8601" }
        }
      }
    }
  }
}
```

---

# Field Reference

| Field | Type | Req | Notes |
| --- | --- | --- | --- |
| `task_id` | ContentHash | yes | sha256(build_id + shot_id); immutable. |
| `shot_id` | ShotId | yes | Storyboard shot; immutable. |
| `build_id` | BuildId | yes | Build scope. |
| `strategy` | RenderStrategy | yes | One per shot; immutable. |
| `render_profile` | string | yes | e.g. runway_final; immutable. |
| `provider` | enum | yes | runway \| motion \| svg \| typography \| cache. |
| `cache_key` | CacheKey | yes | Idempotency anchor (5.6.3). |
| `state` | enum | yes | Closed 5.4.3 state enum. |
| `attempt` | integer 1..4 | yes | Current attempt; separated from state. |
| `max_attempts` | const 4 | yes | max_retry + 1. |
| `attempts_remaining` | integer 0..3 | no | Derived. |
| `delivery_count` | integer | no | Transport deliveries; never gates retry. |
| `provider_task_id` | string/null | no | Opaque; null pre-submit. |
| `next_retry_at` | Iso8601/null | no | null unless RETRY. |
| `last_failure_code` | string/null | no | Last classified failure (5.4.5). |
| `terminal` | boolean | no | Terminal-state flag. |
| `history[]` | array | no | Append-only event/transition log. |

---

# Constraints & Invariants

- **INV-9.6.5-1 (RTS-301).** At every instant the task is in exactly one `state` from the closed enum.
- **INV-9.6.5-2 (RTS-305 / RTB-402).** `attempt` ≤ `max_attempts` (4); transport re-delivery, lease expiry, rate-limit deferral, and poll cycles never increment `attempt` (they increment `delivery_count` only) (RTB-406).
- **INV-9.6.5-3 (RTS-303 / RTS-402).** Every transition is guarded and legal per the 5.4.3 state table; any transition not in "allowed successors" is prohibited.
- **INV-9.6.5-4 (RTS-307 / Fail Closed).** `COMPOSED` is reachable only after submission, provider completion, download, technical validation, and visual validation (≥ 0.90) have all passed; exhausted retries resolve to `MANUAL_REVIEW`, never `COMPOSED`.
- **INV-9.6.5-5 (RTS-302).** State is what the manifest records; queue class, worker memory, and provider status are transition inputs, not state.
- **INV-9.6.5-6 (RTB-405).** Retries reuse `cache_key` as idempotency anchor; a retry never causes a second side-effecting provider render for a result already produced.

---

# Example

```json
{
  "task_id": "sha256:aa01...t1",
  "shot_id": "sh_0007",
  "build_id": "bld_2026_07_20_a1",
  "strategy": "runway_video",
  "render_profile": "runway_final",
  "provider": "runway",
  "cache_key": "sha256:ck07...",
  "state": "RETRY",
  "attempt": 2,
  "max_attempts": 4,
  "attempts_remaining": 2,
  "delivery_count": 3,
  "provider_task_id": null,
  "next_retry_at": "2026-07-20T09:07:20Z",
  "last_failure_code": "PROVIDER_TIMEOUT",
  "terminal": false,
  "created_at": "2026-07-20T09:02:00Z",
  "updated_at": "2026-07-20T09:06:20Z",
  "history": [
    { "attempt": 1, "from_state": "NEW", "to_state": "SUBMITTED", "event": "SUBMIT_OK", "at": "2026-07-20T09:02:00Z" },
    { "attempt": 1, "from_state": "RUNNING", "to_state": "FAILED", "event": "TIMEOUT", "at": "2026-07-20T09:06:10Z" },
    { "attempt": 1, "from_state": "FAILED", "to_state": "RETRY", "event": "RETRY_AUTHORIZED", "at": "2026-07-20T09:06:20Z" }
  ]
}
```

---

# Acceptance Criteria

- Validates against draft 2020-12; `additionalProperties: false`.
- `state` and `history[].event` restricted to the closed 5.4.3 vocabularies.
- `attempt` in 1..4; `max_attempts` fixed to 4.
- A record whose `history` last `to_state` disagrees with `state` fails semantic validation (downstream of schema).

---

# 9.6.6 provider-capability (`provider-capability.yaml`)

### The provider capability descriptor at the provider-independence boundary. Owner: 5.3.2, 5.3.4.

---

# Purpose

The capability descriptor is the neutral, machine-readable declaration through which the rendering core learns what a backend can do (5.3.2). It is the sole channel for capability negotiation (5.3.3) and strategy selection (5.2); the core reads only declared capability and never branches on provider identity (PIF-402). Runway is one provider among many (5.3.1); any future Veo, Luma, Pika, OpenAI Video, or Hunyuan adapter publishes the same descriptor. An adapter must declare exactly what it supports and must not declare a capability it cannot honour (PIF-308).

---

# Canonical Schema

```json
{
  "$schema": "https://json-schema.org/draft/2020-12/schema",
  "$id": "https://schemas.insynergy.co/cttp/v2.0/render/provider-capability.schema.json",
  "title": "ProviderCapabilities",
  "description": "Provider-neutral capability descriptor. Owner: 5.3.2, 5.3.4.",
  "type": "object",
  "additionalProperties": false,
  "required": ["provider", "contract_version", "profiles", "max_duration_seconds", "supported_resolutions", "supported_frame_rates", "supported_aspect_ratios", "supports_seed", "supports_reference_image", "supports_cancel", "supports_progress", "emits_cost_signal"],
  "properties": {
    "provider": { "type": "string", "minLength": 1, "pattern": "^[a-z0-9_]+$", "description": "Stable lowercase provider_id; data, never control (PIF-402)." },
    "contract_version": { "type": "string", "pattern": "^[0-9]+\\.[0-9]+\\.[0-9]+$", "description": "Implemented Provider Interface Contract version (semver)." },
    "profiles": {
      "type": "array",
      "minItems": 1,
      "uniqueItems": true,
      "items": { "type": "string", "enum": ["preview", "final"] },
      "description": "Provider-neutral profiles supported."
    },
    "max_duration_seconds": { "$ref": "https://schemas.insynergy.co/cttp/v2.0/common/defs.schema.json#/$defs/DurationSeconds", "description": "Maximum clip length supported." },
    "supported_resolutions": {
      "type": "array",
      "minItems": 1,
      "uniqueItems": true,
      "items": { "type": "string", "pattern": "^[0-9]+x[0-9]+$" },
      "description": "e.g. [\"1280x720\", \"1920x1080\"]."
    },
    "supported_frame_rates": {
      "type": "array",
      "minItems": 1,
      "uniqueItems": true,
      "items": { "type": "number", "exclusiveMinimum": 0 },
      "description": "e.g. [24, 30]."
    },
    "supported_aspect_ratios": {
      "type": "array",
      "minItems": 1,
      "uniqueItems": true,
      "items": { "$ref": "https://schemas.insynergy.co/cttp/v2.0/common/defs.schema.json#/$defs/Ratio" },
      "description": "e.g. [\"16:9\", \"9:16\"]."
    },
    "supports_seed": { "type": "boolean", "description": "Deterministic seed honoured?" },
    "supports_reference_image": { "type": "boolean" },
    "supports_cancel": { "type": "boolean", "description": "True cancel vs. best-effort ignore." },
    "supports_progress": { "type": "boolean", "description": "Emits a progress fraction?" },
    "emits_cost_signal": { "type": "boolean", "description": "Returns cost units?" },
    "cost_units_per_second": { "type": ["number", "null"], "minimum": 0, "description": "Cost signal; null if not emitted." }
  }
}
```

---

# Field Reference

| Field | Type | Req | Notes |
| --- | --- | --- | --- |
| `provider` | string | yes | Stable lowercase provider_id; data not control. |
| `contract_version` | semver | yes | PIF contract version implemented. |
| `profiles[]` | enum array | yes | preview \| final. |
| `max_duration_seconds` | DurationSeconds | yes | Max clip length. |
| `supported_resolutions[]` | string array | yes | WxH strings. |
| `supported_frame_rates[]` | number array | yes | e.g. 24, 30. |
| `supported_aspect_ratios[]` | Ratio array | yes | e.g. 16:9. |
| `supports_seed` | boolean | yes | Deterministic seed. |
| `supports_reference_image` | boolean | yes | Storyboard still support. |
| `supports_cancel` | boolean | yes | Real vs. best-effort cancel. |
| `supports_progress` | boolean | yes | Progress fraction. |
| `emits_cost_signal` | boolean | yes | Cost units returned. |
| `cost_units_per_second` | number/null | no | null unless cost emitted. |

---

# Constraints & Invariants

- **INV-9.6.6-1 (PIF-308 / Capability Honesty).** A capability the adapter cannot honour must not be declared; the descriptor is the sole negotiation channel.
- **INV-9.6.6-2 (PIF-306).** `profiles`, and the closed capability keys, are drawn from versioned vocabularies; adding a term is a versioned contract change, not an adapter liberty.
- **INV-9.6.6-3 (Versioning).** An adapter whose `contract_version` major differs from the core is rejected fail-closed and never dispatched (PIF-407).
- **INV-9.6.6-4 (Runtime stability).** `capabilities()` is stable for the adapter's process lifetime; a capability change requires a new adapter version and re-registration.
- **INV-9.6.6-5 (PIF-402).** `provider` may be logged and used as a registry key but never used above the interface to select behaviour.

---

# Example

```yaml
provider: runway
contract_version: "1.2.0"
profiles: ["preview", "final"]
max_duration_seconds: 10
supported_resolutions: ["1280x720", "1920x1080"]
supported_frame_rates: [24, 30]
supported_aspect_ratios: ["16:9", "9:16"]
supports_seed: true
supports_reference_image: true
supports_cancel: true
supports_progress: true
emits_cost_signal: true
cost_units_per_second: 0.05
```

---

# Acceptance Criteria

- Validates against draft 2020-12; `additionalProperties: false`.
- `contract_version` is valid semver; `provider` is lowercase snake.
- `profiles` limited to the closed `preview`/`final` set.
- `cost_units_per_second` present iff cost is emitted (semantic pairing with `emits_cost_signal`).

---

# 9.6.7 retry-policy (`retry-policy.schema.json`)

### The retry, backoff, and failure-classification configuration. Owner: 5.4.5.

---

# Purpose

`retry-policy` fixes the retry ceiling, exponential backoff, and closed failure-classification taxonomy of the Rendering Platform (5.4.5). Retry is permitted only for transient provider/network/transport faults and forbidden for quality, invalidity, and unsupported-input failures; an unmapped failure is non-retryable by default (RTB-301). The canonical config is `rtb-config`; the failure taxonomy is the closed `failure_code` set; the authorization and failure records anchor idempotent, manifest-first retry. Total attempts never exceed `max_retry + 1` (four).

---

# Canonical Schema

```json
{
  "$schema": "https://json-schema.org/draft/2020-12/schema",
  "$id": "https://schemas.insynergy.co/cttp/v2.0/render/retry-policy.schema.json",
  "title": "RetryPolicy",
  "description": "Retry, backoff, and failure-classification config. Owner: 5.4.5.",
  "type": "object",
  "additionalProperties": false,
  "required": ["max_retry", "backoff", "classification", "authorization", "routing", "deadline_guard"],
  "properties": {
    "max_retry": { "type": "integer", "minimum": 0, "default": 3, "description": "Canonical 3; total attempts = max_retry + 1." },
    "backoff": {
      "type": "object",
      "additionalProperties": false,
      "required": ["strategy", "base", "cap", "jitter_max"],
      "properties": {
        "strategy": { "type": "string", "const": "exponential" },
        "base": { "type": "string", "const": "10s", "description": "Initial backoff interval." },
        "cap": { "type": "string", "const": "120s", "description": "Maximum backoff before jitter." },
        "jitter_max": { "type": "string", "const": "5s", "description": "Deterministic jitter ceiling." }
      }
    },
    "classification": {
      "type": "object",
      "additionalProperties": false,
      "required": ["retryable_codes", "non_retryable_codes", "unknown_default"],
      "properties": {
        "retryable_codes": {
          "type": "array",
          "uniqueItems": true,
          "items": { "type": "string", "enum": ["PROVIDER_TIMEOUT", "TEMPORARY_API_FAILURE", "CORRUPTED_DOWNLOAD", "PROVIDER_RATE_LIMITED", "NETWORK_TRANSIENT"] }
        },
        "non_retryable_codes": {
          "type": "array",
          "uniqueItems": true,
          "items": { "type": "string", "enum": ["FAILED_QUALITY_VALIDATION", "INVALID_PROMPT", "UNSUPPORTED_INPUT", "ASSET_TECHNICAL_INVALID", "PROVIDER_PERMANENT_REJECTION", "BUDGET_EXHAUSTED", "UNKNOWN_FAILURE"] }
        },
        "unknown_default": { "type": "string", "const": "NON_RETRYABLE", "description": "Fail-safe (RTB-301)." }
      }
    },
    "authorization": {
      "type": "object",
      "additionalProperties": false,
      "required": ["require_manifest_record", "check_budget", "check_cancellation"],
      "properties": {
        "require_manifest_record": { "type": "boolean", "const": true, "description": "RTB-303." },
        "check_budget": { "type": "boolean" },
        "check_cancellation": { "type": "boolean" }
      }
    },
    "routing": {
      "type": "object",
      "additionalProperties": false,
      "required": ["exhausted", "non_retryable"],
      "properties": {
        "exhausted": { "type": "string", "const": "DEAD_LETTER" },
        "non_retryable": { "type": "string", "const": "MANUAL_REVIEW" }
      }
    },
    "deadline_guard": {
      "type": "object",
      "additionalProperties": false,
      "required": ["respect_overall_timeout"],
      "properties": {
        "respect_overall_timeout": { "type": "boolean", "const": true, "description": "No retry scheduled past 5.4.6 overall_timeout (RTB-411)." }
      }
    }
  }
}
```

---

# Field Reference

| Field | Type | Req | Notes |
| --- | --- | --- | --- |
| `max_retry` | integer | yes | Canonical 3; ceiling = max_retry + 1. |
| `backoff.strategy` | const exponential | yes | Exponential only. |
| `backoff.base` | const 10s | yes | Initial interval. |
| `backoff.cap` | const 120s | yes | Hard ceiling. |
| `backoff.jitter_max` | const 5s | yes | Deterministic jitter bound. |
| `classification.retryable_codes[]` | enum array | yes | Five transient codes. |
| `classification.non_retryable_codes[]` | enum array | yes | Seven deterministic/substantive codes. |
| `classification.unknown_default` | const NON_RETRYABLE | yes | Fail-safe. |
| `authorization.require_manifest_record` | const true | yes | Manifest-first (RTB-303). |
| `routing.exhausted` | const DEAD_LETTER | yes | Exhaustion route. |
| `routing.non_retryable` | const MANUAL_REVIEW | yes | Non-retryable route. |
| `deadline_guard.respect_overall_timeout` | const true | yes | RTB-411. |

---

# Constraints & Invariants

- **INV-9.6.7-1 (RTB-402).** Total attempts never exceed `max_retry + 1` (four); backoff schedule is 10s / 20s / 40s pre-jitter for retries 1–3.
- **INV-9.6.7-2 (RTB-301 / RTB-407).** Quality-validation, invalid-prompt, and unsupported-input failures are never retryable; an unmapped failure defaults to `NON_RETRYABLE` and escalates to Manual Review.
- **INV-9.6.7-3 (RTB-403).** A Retry Queue item exists only if a matching authorization was persisted to the manifest first.
- **INV-9.6.7-4 (RTB-404 / RTB-410).** Backoff is bounded, capped, and deterministically jittered from `(task_id, attempt)`; disposition and delay are deterministic functions of failure code, attempt, and config.
- **INV-9.6.7-5 (Startup validation).** A code appearing in both retryable and non-retryable lists, or `base > cap`, or `max_retry < 0`, fails closed and blocks admission.
- **INV-9.6.7-6 (RTB-409).** Every failure ends in exactly one durable destination: scheduled retry, Dead Letter, or Manual Review — never silent loss.

---

# Example

```json
{
  "max_retry": 3,
  "backoff": { "strategy": "exponential", "base": "10s", "cap": "120s", "jitter_max": "5s" },
  "classification": {
    "retryable_codes": ["PROVIDER_TIMEOUT", "TEMPORARY_API_FAILURE", "CORRUPTED_DOWNLOAD", "PROVIDER_RATE_LIMITED", "NETWORK_TRANSIENT"],
    "non_retryable_codes": ["FAILED_QUALITY_VALIDATION", "INVALID_PROMPT", "UNSUPPORTED_INPUT", "ASSET_TECHNICAL_INVALID", "PROVIDER_PERMANENT_REJECTION", "BUDGET_EXHAUSTED", "UNKNOWN_FAILURE"],
    "unknown_default": "NON_RETRYABLE"
  },
  "authorization": { "require_manifest_record": true, "check_budget": true, "check_cancellation": true },
  "routing": { "exhausted": "DEAD_LETTER", "non_retryable": "MANUAL_REVIEW" },
  "deadline_guard": { "respect_overall_timeout": true }
}
```

---

# Acceptance Criteria

- Validates against draft 2020-12; `additionalProperties: false`.
- `retryable_codes` and `non_retryable_codes` restricted to their closed enums and disjoint.
- Backoff constants fixed to 10s / 120s / 5s exponential.
- `unknown_default`, `routing`, and `deadline_guard` fixed to their fail-safe constants.

---

# 9.6.8 prompt-assembly (`prompt-assembly.schema.json`)

### The deterministic prompt-assembly record. Owner: 5.5.1.

---

# Purpose

`prompt-assembly` records the output of the Deterministic Prompt Assembler (5.5.1): the eight ordered prompt components, the canonical single-string rendering over which the prompt hash is computed, and the completeness and article-freedom verification flags. Assembly is a pure function — same inputs yield byte-identical output and an identical `prompt_hash`, which anchors the render cache key (5.6.3). CHARACTER and LOCATION are injected by reference (5.5.2, 5.5.3), CAMERA is copied verbatim from the authoritative camera plan (5.5.4), and VISUAL_STYLE is subject to enforcement (5.5.5). No article text ever reaches the record; `provenance` is retained for audit but is not serialized into the provider prompt.

---

# Canonical Schema

```json
{
  "$schema": "https://json-schema.org/draft/2020-12/schema",
  "$id": "https://schemas.insynergy.co/cttp/v2.0/render/prompt-assembly.schema.json",
  "title": "PromptAssembly",
  "description": "Deterministic prompt-assembly record. Owner: 5.5.1.",
  "type": "object",
  "additionalProperties": false,
  "required": ["prompt_schema_version", "shot_id", "build_id", "render_profile", "provider", "components", "canonical_text", "prompt_hash", "article_free_verified", "complete_verified"],
  "properties": {
    "prompt_schema_version": { "type": "string", "minLength": 1, "description": "Pins template + normalization rules, e.g. 'pma-1'." },
    "shot_id": { "$ref": "https://schemas.insynergy.co/cttp/v2.0/common/defs.schema.json#/$defs/ShotId" },
    "build_id": { "$ref": "https://schemas.insynergy.co/cttp/v2.0/common/defs.schema.json#/$defs/BuildId" },
    "render_profile": { "type": "string", "minLength": 1, "description": "From render-strategy.json, e.g. runway_final." },
    "provider": { "type": "string", "enum": ["runway", "motion", "svg", "typography", "cache"] },
    "components": {
      "type": "array",
      "description": "Ordered list of the eight prompt components (fixed order 1..8).",
      "minItems": 7,
      "maxItems": 8,
      "items": {
        "type": "object",
        "additionalProperties": false,
        "required": ["component_id", "order", "source_artifact", "present"],
        "properties": {
          "component_id": {
            "type": "string",
            "enum": ["CHARACTER", "LOCATION", "CAMERA", "LIGHTING", "BLOCKING", "EMOTION", "SHOT_PURPOSE", "VISUAL_STYLE"]
          },
          "order": { "type": "integer", "minimum": 1, "maximum": 8, "description": "Fixed integer 1..8; immutable." },
          "source_artifact": { "type": "string", "minLength": 1, "description": "e.g. character-bible.yaml." },
          "source_ref": { "oneOf": [{ "$ref": "https://schemas.insynergy.co/cttp/v2.0/common/defs.schema.json#/$defs/RefId" }, { "type": "null" }], "description": "e.g. maya_v1; null for inline components." },
          "resolved_text": { "type": "string", "description": "Canonical normalized descriptive text (the only content in the prompt)." },
          "provenance": {
            "type": "object",
            "additionalProperties": false,
            "description": "Audit only; NOT serialized into the provider prompt (PMA-308).",
            "properties": {
              "artifact": { "type": "string" },
              "ref": { "type": ["string", "null"] },
              "artifact_version": { "type": "string" }
            }
          },
          "present": { "type": "boolean", "description": "false only for the optional BLOCKING component (PMA-305)." }
        }
      }
    },
    "canonical_text": { "type": "string", "minLength": 1, "description": "Deterministic single-string rendering used for hashing + submission." },
    "prompt_hash": { "$ref": "https://schemas.insynergy.co/cttp/v2.0/common/defs.schema.json#/$defs/ContentHash", "description": "sha256 over canonical_text; anchors the render cache key (5.6.3)." },
    "article_free_verified": { "type": "boolean", "description": "Must be true before submission (content firewall)." },
    "complete_verified": { "type": "boolean", "description": "Must be true before submission (completeness gate)." }
  }
}
```

---

# Field Reference

| Field | Type | Req | Notes |
| --- | --- | --- | --- |
| `prompt_schema_version` | string | yes | Pins template + normalization (e.g. pma-1). |
| `shot_id` | ShotId | yes | Shot reference. |
| `build_id` | BuildId | yes | Build scope. |
| `render_profile` | string | yes | From render-strategy.json. |
| `provider` | enum | yes | runway \| motion \| svg \| typography \| cache. |
| `components[]` | array (7–8) | yes | Eight fixed components, BLOCKING optional. |
| `components[].component_id` | enum | yes | CHARACTER..VISUAL_STYLE. |
| `components[].order` | integer 1..8 | yes | Fixed order; immutable. |
| `components[].source_artifact` | string | yes | Owning artifact. |
| `components[].source_ref` | RefId/null | no | Injection ref; null inline. |
| `components[].resolved_text` | string | no | Canonical text; only content in the prompt. |
| `components[].provenance` | object | no | Audit only; not serialized. |
| `components[].present` | boolean | yes | false only for BLOCKING. |
| `canonical_text` | string | yes | Hashed + submitted text. |
| `prompt_hash` | ContentHash | yes | sha256(canonical_text). |
| `article_free_verified` | boolean | yes | Must be true before submission. |
| `complete_verified` | boolean | yes | Must be true before submission. |

---

# Constraints & Invariants

- **INV-9.6.8-1 (PMA-301 / R4A-404).** Assembly is a pure function; the same unchanged shot yields byte-identical `canonical_text`, a stable `prompt_hash`, and therefore a stable `cache_key`.
- **INV-9.6.8-2 (PMA-302).** Components appear in the fixed order 1..8; `BLOCKING` is the only optional component (`present` may be false); every other component is mandatory and present.
- **INV-9.6.8-3 (Content firewall / R4A-405).** No article text, story prose, dialogue-as-narrative, or editorial copy appears; CHARACTER/LOCATION are injected by reference and CAMERA is copied verbatim (never overridden).
- **INV-9.6.8-4 (Fail Closed).** A prompt is submitted only when both `article_free_verified` and `complete_verified` are true; otherwise the shot is halted and escalated, never sent best-effort.
- **INV-9.6.8-5 (PMA-308).** `provenance` is retained for audit but never serialized into the provider prompt.

---

# Example

```json
{
  "prompt_schema_version": "pma-1",
  "shot_id": "sh_0007",
  "build_id": "bld_2026_07_20_a1",
  "render_profile": "runway_final",
  "provider": "runway",
  "components": [
    { "component_id": "CHARACTER", "order": 1, "source_artifact": "character-bible.yaml", "source_ref": "maya_v1", "resolved_text": "Maya, mid-30s analyst, charcoal blazer, calm focus", "provenance": { "artifact": "character-bible.yaml", "ref": "maya_v1", "artifact_version": "3" }, "present": true },
    { "component_id": "LOCATION", "order": 2, "source_artifact": "location-bible.yaml", "source_ref": "operations_center_night", "resolved_text": "Operations center at night, cool blue monitors, low ambient", "provenance": { "artifact": "location-bible.yaml", "ref": "operations_center_night", "artifact_version": "2" }, "present": true },
    { "component_id": "CAMERA", "order": 3, "source_artifact": "camera-plan.json", "source_ref": null, "resolved_text": "35mm, slow push-in, eye-level", "present": true },
    { "component_id": "LIGHTING", "order": 4, "source_artifact": "storyboard.json", "source_ref": null, "resolved_text": "Low-key, cool key, soft fill", "present": true },
    { "component_id": "BLOCKING", "order": 5, "source_artifact": "shot-list.json", "source_ref": null, "resolved_text": "", "present": false },
    { "component_id": "EMOTION", "order": 6, "source_artifact": "shot-list.json", "source_ref": null, "resolved_text": "Resolve tempered by concern", "present": true },
    { "component_id": "SHOT_PURPOSE", "order": 7, "source_artifact": "shot-list.json", "source_ref": null, "resolved_text": "Establish the analyst's stakes", "present": true },
    { "component_id": "VISUAL_STYLE", "order": 8, "source_artifact": "style profile", "source_ref": null, "resolved_text": "Restrained enterprise-cinematic realism", "present": true }
  ],
  "canonical_text": "[CHARACTER] Maya, mid-30s analyst, charcoal blazer, calm focus\n[LOCATION] Operations center at night, cool blue monitors, low ambient\n[CAMERA] 35mm, slow push-in, eye-level\n[LIGHTING] Low-key, cool key, soft fill\n[EMOTION] Resolve tempered by concern\n[SHOT_PURPOSE] Establish the analyst's stakes\n[VISUAL_STYLE] Restrained enterprise-cinematic realism",
  "prompt_hash": "sha256:pmt07...",
  "article_free_verified": true,
  "complete_verified": true
}
```

---

# Acceptance Criteria

- Validates against draft 2020-12; `additionalProperties: false`.
- `component_id` and `order` restricted to the closed 1..8 set; BLOCKING is the only entry permitted `present: false`.
- `prompt_hash` is a sha256 over `canonical_text`.
- A record with either verification flag false is not submittable (semantic gate downstream of schema).

---

# 9.6.9 location-bible (`location-bible.yaml`)

### The immutable location reference bible, read-only to rendering. Owner: 5.1.4, 4.1.7.

---

# Purpose

`location-bible.yaml` is the immutable source of environment identity keyed by RefId (5.1.4 input contract `rio-location-bible`; produced by the Location Engine, 4.1.7). Location injection (5.5.3) resolves each `location_ref` from `shot-list.json` against this bible. It is read-only to rendering under input immutability (RIO-305) and environment-locked: descriptions are canonical and may never be altered by rendering or a provider, guaranteeing environment consistency across every shot that shares a location. Every entry is keyed by a unique `ref`; `environment_lock` must be `true`; only `time_of_day` is optional.

---

# Canonical Schema

```json
{
  "$schema": "https://json-schema.org/draft/2020-12/schema",
  "$id": "https://schemas.insynergy.co/cttp/v2.0/render/location-bible.schema.json",
  "title": "LocationBible",
  "description": "Immutable location reference bible keyed by RefId. Owner: 5.1.4, 4.1.7.",
  "type": "object",
  "allOf": [
    { "$ref": "https://schemas.insynergy.co/cttp/v2.0/common/defs.schema.json#/$defs/ArtifactEnvelope" }
  ],
  "properties": {
    "schema_version": { "$ref": "https://schemas.insynergy.co/cttp/v2.0/common/defs.schema.json#/$defs/SchemaVersion" },
    "build_id": { "$ref": "https://schemas.insynergy.co/cttp/v2.0/common/defs.schema.json#/$defs/BuildId" },
    "approved": { "type": "boolean", "const": true, "description": "Must be true (passed upstream Quality Gate)." },
    "approval_ref": { "$ref": "https://schemas.insynergy.co/cttp/v2.0/common/defs.schema.json#/$defs/ApprovalRef" },
    "generated_at": { "$ref": "https://schemas.insynergy.co/cttp/v2.0/common/defs.schema.json#/$defs/Iso8601" },
    "content_hash": { "$ref": "https://schemas.insynergy.co/cttp/v2.0/common/defs.schema.json#/$defs/ContentHash" },
    "locations": {
      "type": "array",
      "description": "Keyed by ref id; every ref unique.",
      "minItems": 1,
      "items": {
        "type": "object",
        "additionalProperties": false,
        "required": ["ref", "display_name", "description", "environment_lock"],
        "properties": {
          "ref": { "$ref": "https://schemas.insynergy.co/cttp/v2.0/common/defs.schema.json#/$defs/RefId", "description": "e.g. operations_center_night; stable, unique." },
          "display_name": { "type": "string", "minLength": 1 },
          "description": { "type": "string", "minLength": 1, "description": "Canonical environment description; immutable." },
          "time_of_day": { "type": "string", "description": "Optional; e.g. night | day." },
          "environment_lock": { "type": "boolean", "const": true, "description": "Must be true (immutable environment)." }
        }
      }
    }
  },
  "required": ["schema_version", "build_id", "approved", "approval_ref", "generated_at", "content_hash", "locations"],
  "unevaluatedProperties": false
}
```

---

# Field Reference

| Field | Type | Req | Notes |
| --- | --- | --- | --- |
| `schema_version` | SchemaVersion | yes | Envelope. |
| `build_id` | BuildId | yes | Build scope. |
| `approved` | const true | yes | Passed upstream Quality Gate. |
| `approval_ref` | ApprovalRef | yes | Approval reference. |
| `generated_at` | Iso8601 | yes | Emission time. |
| `content_hash` | ContentHash | yes | Fixity; must verify at gate. |
| `locations[]` | array | yes | Keyed by unique ref. |
| `locations[].ref` | RefId | yes | Stable, unique. |
| `locations[].display_name` | string | yes | Human-readable name. |
| `locations[].description` | string | yes | Canonical environment description; immutable. |
| `locations[].time_of_day` | string | no | Only optional field. |
| `locations[].environment_lock` | const true | yes | Immutable environment. |

---

# Constraints & Invariants

- **INV-9.6.9-1 (RIO-305 / environment-locked).** Read-only to rendering; descriptions are canonical and may never be altered by rendering or a provider.
- **INV-9.6.9-2 (5.5.3 referential integrity).** Every `location_ref` used in `shot-list.json` must resolve to a `ref` here; every `ref` is unique.
- **INV-9.6.9-3 (Input contract).** `approved` and every `environment_lock` must be `true`; `content_hash` must verify at the precondition gate (RIO-307).
- **INV-9.6.9-4 (Immutability).** Only `time_of_day` is optional; every other field is required and non-empty.
- **INV-9.6.9-5 (RIO-308).** The verified `content_hash` is copied into `metadata.json.input_lineage`, binding the trailer to this exact bible version.

---

# Example

```yaml
schema_version: "2.0.0"
build_id: "bld_2026_07_20_a1"
approved: true
approval_ref: "qg_locbible_a1"
generated_at: "2026-07-20T08:40:00Z"
content_hash: "sha256:lb..."
locations:
  - ref: "operations_center_night"
    display_name: "Operations Center (Night)"
    description: "A darkened operations center; banks of cool blue monitors, low ambient light, glass partitions"
    time_of_day: "night"
    environment_lock: true
  - ref: "rooftop_dawn"
    display_name: "Rooftop (Dawn)"
    description: "An open rooftop at first light; muted amber sky, wet concrete, distant skyline"
    time_of_day: "day"
    environment_lock: true
```

---

# Acceptance Criteria

- Validates against draft 2020-12; composes `ArtifactEnvelope`; `unevaluatedProperties: false`.
- `approved` and every `environment_lock` fixed to `true`.
- `locations[].ref` values unique across the bible.
- Only `time_of_day` optional; all other entry fields required.
- Read-only to rendering; any render-side mutation is a violation (INV-9.6.9-1).

---
# 9.7 Performance & Build Layer Schemas

### Insynergy Cinematic Thought Leadership Platform — Master Specification v2.0, Part 9 (JSON Schema / Appendix)

---

# Purpose

This chapter formalizes the build-orchestration, performance, configuration, and operational-state artifacts of **Part 6 — Performance & Build Architecture**. These are the artifacts that **plan, budget, execute, and track** a build: the per-stage time budget, the immutable execution plan, the dependency DAG, the build profile, the resolved performance configuration, the operational lifecycle record, and the consolidated Quality-Gate registry.

Each schema is a complete, valid **JSON Schema draft 2020-12** document. Schemas reuse the shared primitives defined in `https://schemas.insynergy.co/cttp/v2.0/common/defs.schema.json` (`SchemaVersion`, `BuildId`, `ShotId`, `ApprovalRef`, `ContentHash`, `CacheKey`, `Iso8601`, `DurationSeconds`, `Ratio`, `Score`, `BuildType`, `ArtifactEnvelope`) via `$ref`. Sealed artifacts compose `ArtifactEnvelope` through `allOf` with `"unevaluatedProperties": false`.

# Design Philosophy

Part 6 elevates performance to a **first-class architectural requirement** — equal to story, visual, and reliability requirements. The schemas below encode that stance structurally rather than by convention:

- **Determinism** — every operational entity exists in exactly one explicit state; transitions are recorded (Owner: 6.1.11).
- **Immutable planning** — the execution plan and dependency graph are immutable for the duration of a build (Principle 3, Owner: 6.1.3).
- **Incrementality** — profiles, cache usage, and dependency edges make reuse and fine-grained parallelism first-class (Principles 5–6).
- **Fail-fast** — budgets, gates, and validation are blocking and fail-closed (Principle 10; Owner: 6.1.6).

The seven schemas of this chapter:

- **9.7.1 performance-budget** — per-stage maximum-duration allocation (Owner: 6.1.1).
- **9.7.2 execution-plan** — the immutable build/pipeline plan (Owner: 6.1.3).
- **9.7.3 dependency-graph** — the acyclic stage/shot DAG (Owner: 6.1.3).
- **9.7.4 build-profile** — build profiles and execution modes (Owner: 6.1.7).
- **9.7.5 performance-config** — the layered, runtime-immutable performance configuration snapshot (Owner: 6.1.8).
- **9.7.6 operational-state** — the lifecycle-state record of a build artifact (Owner: 6.1.11).
- **9.7.7 quality-gate-registry** — the consolidated registry of platform Quality Gates (Owner: 6.1.6).

---

# 9.7.1 performance-budget (`performance-budget.schema.json`)

### Per-stage maximum execution budget for a build (Owner: 6.1.1)

---

# Purpose

Section 6.1.1 allocates each pipeline stage a **maximum execution budget**. A build is successful only when total duration remains within the configured Service Level Objective (SLO); meeting the time target alone does not constitute success. This schema captures the declarative budget so that any stage exceeding its allocation can deterministically emit a performance warning.

**SLO/KPI relation.** The per-stage `max_duration` values are the *budgets*; the section's Primary Performance Objectives (Preview ≤ 25 min, Final ≤ 35 min, Planning ≤ 3 min, etc.) are the *SLOs*. The sum of stage budgets must remain consistent with the build-level SLO, and the ratio of observed to budgeted duration is the KPI surfaced to the Optimization Metrics Engine. All durations are modelled in **seconds** via `DurationSeconds`.

---

# Canonical Schema

```json
{
  "$schema": "https://json-schema.org/draft/2020-12/schema",
  "$id": "https://schemas.insynergy.co/cttp/v2.0/build/performance-budget.schema.json",
  "title": "PerformanceBudget",
  "description": "Per-stage maximum execution budget. Owner: 6.1.1.",
  "type": "object",
  "additionalProperties": false,
  "required": ["schema_version", "stages"],
  "properties": {
    "schema_version": {
      "$ref": "https://schemas.insynergy.co/cttp/v2.0/common/defs.schema.json#/$defs/SchemaVersion"
    },
    "build_type": {
      "$ref": "https://schemas.insynergy.co/cttp/v2.0/common/defs.schema.json#/$defs/BuildType",
      "description": "Optional scope; budgets may differ between preview and final builds."
    },
    "stages": {
      "type": "object",
      "additionalProperties": false,
      "description": "Maximum duration per pipeline stage (seconds). Owner: 6.1.1.",
      "required": [
        "planning",
        "screenplay",
        "shot_planning",
        "storyboard",
        "render_submission",
        "download",
        "validation",
        "composition",
        "packaging"
      ],
      "properties": {
        "planning": { "$ref": "#/$defs/StageBudget" },
        "screenplay": { "$ref": "#/$defs/StageBudget" },
        "shot_planning": { "$ref": "#/$defs/StageBudget" },
        "storyboard": { "$ref": "#/$defs/StageBudget" },
        "render_submission": { "$ref": "#/$defs/StageBudget" },
        "provider_rendering": {
          "type": "object",
          "additionalProperties": false,
          "description": "Provider rendering is external and un-budgeted. Owner: 6.1.1.",
          "required": ["external"],
          "properties": { "external": { "const": true } }
        },
        "download": { "$ref": "#/$defs/StageBudget" },
        "validation": { "$ref": "#/$defs/StageBudget" },
        "composition": { "$ref": "#/$defs/StageBudget" },
        "packaging": { "$ref": "#/$defs/StageBudget" }
      }
    },
    "slo": {
      "type": "object",
      "additionalProperties": false,
      "description": "Build-level SLO the stage budgets must sum within.",
      "properties": {
        "total_max_duration": {
          "$ref": "https://schemas.insynergy.co/cttp/v2.0/common/defs.schema.json#/$defs/DurationSeconds"
        },
        "priority": {
          "type": "string",
          "enum": ["Critical", "High", "Medium", "Low"]
        }
      }
    },
    "on_exceed": {
      "type": "string",
      "description": "Action when a stage exceeds its allocation. Owner: 6.1.1.",
      "enum": ["warn", "fail"],
      "default": "warn"
    }
  },
  "$defs": {
    "StageBudget": {
      "type": "object",
      "additionalProperties": false,
      "required": ["max_duration"],
      "properties": {
        "max_duration": {
          "$ref": "https://schemas.insynergy.co/cttp/v2.0/common/defs.schema.json#/$defs/DurationSeconds",
          "description": "Maximum permitted stage duration in seconds."
        },
        "priority": {
          "type": "string",
          "enum": ["Critical", "High", "Medium", "Low"]
        }
      }
    }
  }
}
```

---

# Field Reference

| Field | Type | Required | Description |
| ----- | ---- | -------- | ----------- |
| `schema_version` | `SchemaVersion` | Yes | Schema version of this budget document. |
| `build_type` | `BuildType` | No | Scope of the budget (e.g. preview vs final). |
| `stages` | object | Yes | Container of per-stage budgets. |
| `stages.<stage>.max_duration` | `DurationSeconds` | Yes | Maximum stage duration, in seconds. |
| `stages.<stage>.priority` | enum | No | Criticality of the stage's SLO. |
| `stages.provider_rendering.external` | `true` | Yes | Marks provider rendering as external / un-budgeted. |
| `slo.total_max_duration` | `DurationSeconds` | No | Build-level SLO ceiling. |
| `on_exceed` | enum | No | `warn` (default) or `fail` on budget breach. |

---

# Constraints & Invariants

- **INV-9.7.1-1** — Every mandatory stage (`planning`, `screenplay`, `shot_planning`, `storyboard`, `render_submission`, `download`, `validation`, `composition`, `packaging`) must declare a `max_duration` (Owner: 6.1.1).
- **INV-9.7.1-2** — `provider_rendering` carries no `max_duration`; it is `external` because rendering is a stateless external execution layer (Principle 4, *Rendering Is Stateless*).
- **INV-9.7.1-3** — When `slo.total_max_duration` is present, the sum of stage `max_duration` values must not exceed it (*Performance by Design*, Principle 1). Structural where expressible; otherwise enforced by the budget validator.
- **INV-9.7.1-4** — Durations are non-negative integers in seconds, delegated to `DurationSeconds`.
- **INV-9.7.1-5** — A stage exceeding its allocation emits a performance warning; with `on_exceed: "fail"` the build fails fast (Principle 10, *Fail Fast*).

---

# Example

```json
{
  "schema_version": "2.0.0",
  "build_type": "final",
  "stages": {
    "planning": { "max_duration": 180, "priority": "Critical" },
    "screenplay": { "max_duration": 30, "priority": "High" },
    "shot_planning": { "max_duration": 60, "priority": "High" },
    "storyboard": { "max_duration": 90, "priority": "High" },
    "render_submission": { "max_duration": 120, "priority": "Critical" },
    "provider_rendering": { "external": true },
    "download": { "max_duration": 300 },
    "validation": { "max_duration": 120 },
    "composition": { "max_duration": 300, "priority": "Medium" },
    "packaging": { "max_duration": 30, "priority": "Low" }
  },
  "slo": { "total_max_duration": 2100, "priority": "Critical" },
  "on_exceed": "warn"
}
```

---

# Acceptance Criteria

- A conforming document declares all nine mandatory stage budgets in seconds.
- `provider_rendering` is expressed as external and un-budgeted.
- Budget totals are consistent with any declared build-level SLO.
- Documents that omit a mandatory stage, express a negative duration, or add unknown stage keys are rejected.

---

# 9.7.2 execution-plan (`execution-plan.schema.json`)

### The immutable build plan produced by the Build Planner (Owner: 6.1.3)

---

# Purpose

Section 6.1.3 defines the Build Planner, which analyzes the Storyboard and emits `execution-plan.json`. The plan reconciles the *Execution Plan Schema* and the pipeline-plan object into one artifact: `build_id`, `pipeline_version`, `shots`, `cached_assets`, `render_queue`, `validation_queue`, and `composition_plan`. It records render strategy, provider profiles, identified cache hits, and estimated cost. **This document is immutable for the duration of the build** — execution never modifies planning artifacts (Principle 3, *Immutable Planning*). It is a sealed artifact and composes `ArtifactEnvelope`.

---

# Canonical Schema

```json
{
  "$schema": "https://json-schema.org/draft/2020-12/schema",
  "$id": "https://schemas.insynergy.co/cttp/v2.0/build/execution-plan.schema.json",
  "title": "ExecutionPlan",
  "description": "Immutable build/pipeline plan. Owner: 6.1.3.",
  "allOf": [
    { "$ref": "https://schemas.insynergy.co/cttp/v2.0/common/defs.schema.json#/$defs/ArtifactEnvelope" },
    {
      "type": "object",
      "required": [
        "build_id",
        "pipeline_version",
        "shots",
        "cached_assets",
        "render_queue",
        "validation_queue",
        "composition_plan"
      ],
      "properties": {
        "build_id": {
          "$ref": "https://schemas.insynergy.co/cttp/v2.0/common/defs.schema.json#/$defs/BuildId"
        },
        "pipeline_version": {
          "$ref": "https://schemas.insynergy.co/cttp/v2.0/common/defs.schema.json#/$defs/SchemaVersion",
          "description": "Version of the pipeline that produced the plan."
        },
        "build_type": {
          "$ref": "https://schemas.insynergy.co/cttp/v2.0/common/defs.schema.json#/$defs/BuildType"
        },
        "shots": {
          "type": "array",
          "description": "Planned shots with resolved render strategy. Owner: 6.1.3.",
          "items": { "$ref": "#/$defs/PlannedShot" }
        },
        "cached_assets": {
          "type": "array",
          "description": "Assets satisfied from cache; no rendering required.",
          "items": { "$ref": "#/$defs/CachedAsset" }
        },
        "render_queue": {
          "type": "array",
          "description": "Shots requiring provider rendering.",
          "items": { "$ref": "#/$defs/RenderQueueEntry" }
        },
        "validation_queue": {
          "type": "array",
          "description": "Assets awaiting technical and editorial validation.",
          "items": {
            "$ref": "https://schemas.insynergy.co/cttp/v2.0/common/defs.schema.json#/$defs/ShotId"
          }
        },
        "composition_plan": {
          "type": "object",
          "additionalProperties": false,
          "description": "FFmpeg composition ordering. Owner: 6.1.3.",
          "properties": {
            "ordered_shots": {
              "type": "array",
              "items": {
                "$ref": "https://schemas.insynergy.co/cttp/v2.0/common/defs.schema.json#/$defs/ShotId"
              }
            },
            "target_duration": {
              "$ref": "https://schemas.insynergy.co/cttp/v2.0/common/defs.schema.json#/$defs/DurationSeconds"
            }
          }
        },
        "dependency_graph_ref": {
          "$ref": "https://schemas.insynergy.co/cttp/v2.0/common/defs.schema.json#/$defs/ContentHash",
          "description": "Content hash of the associated dependency-graph artifact (9.7.3)."
        },
        "estimated_cost_usd": {
          "type": "number",
          "minimum": 0,
          "description": "Estimated provider cost prior to submission. Owner: 6.1.3."
        }
      }
    }
  ],
  "unevaluatedProperties": false,
  "$defs": {
    "PlannedShot": {
      "type": "object",
      "additionalProperties": false,
      "required": ["shot_id", "render_strategy"],
      "properties": {
        "shot_id": {
          "$ref": "https://schemas.insynergy.co/cttp/v2.0/common/defs.schema.json#/$defs/ShotId"
        },
        "render_strategy": {
          "type": "string",
          "enum": ["render", "cache_hit", "placeholder"]
        },
        "provider_profile": { "type": "string" },
        "cache_key": {
          "$ref": "https://schemas.insynergy.co/cttp/v2.0/common/defs.schema.json#/$defs/CacheKey"
        }
      }
    },
    "CachedAsset": {
      "type": "object",
      "additionalProperties": false,
      "required": ["shot_id", "cache_key", "content_hash"],
      "properties": {
        "shot_id": {
          "$ref": "https://schemas.insynergy.co/cttp/v2.0/common/defs.schema.json#/$defs/ShotId"
        },
        "cache_key": {
          "$ref": "https://schemas.insynergy.co/cttp/v2.0/common/defs.schema.json#/$defs/CacheKey"
        },
        "content_hash": {
          "$ref": "https://schemas.insynergy.co/cttp/v2.0/common/defs.schema.json#/$defs/ContentHash"
        }
      }
    },
    "RenderQueueEntry": {
      "type": "object",
      "additionalProperties": false,
      "required": ["shot_id", "provider_profile"],
      "properties": {
        "shot_id": {
          "$ref": "https://schemas.insynergy.co/cttp/v2.0/common/defs.schema.json#/$defs/ShotId"
        },
        "provider_profile": { "type": "string" },
        "cache_key": {
          "$ref": "https://schemas.insynergy.co/cttp/v2.0/common/defs.schema.json#/$defs/CacheKey"
        }
      }
    }
  }
}
```

---

# Field Reference

| Field | Type | Required | Description |
| ----- | ---- | -------- | ----------- |
| `build_id` | `BuildId` | Yes | Identifier of the build this plan governs. |
| `pipeline_version` | `SchemaVersion` | Yes | Version of the producing pipeline. |
| `build_type` | `BuildType` | No | Preview / final scope. |
| `shots` | array of `PlannedShot` | Yes | Planned shots with resolved render strategy. |
| `cached_assets` | array of `CachedAsset` | Yes | Cache-satisfied assets; no rendering issued. |
| `render_queue` | array of `RenderQueueEntry` | Yes | Shots requiring provider rendering. |
| `validation_queue` | array of `ShotId` | Yes | Assets awaiting validation. |
| `composition_plan` | object | Yes | Ordered composition and target duration. |
| `dependency_graph_ref` | `ContentHash` | No | Hash link to the dependency graph (9.7.3). |
| `estimated_cost_usd` | number ≥ 0 | No | Pre-submission cost estimate. |

---

# Constraints & Invariants

- **INV-9.7.2-1** — The plan is immutable for the build's duration; execution never mutates it (Principle 3, *Immutable Planning*; Owner: 6.1.3).
- **INV-9.7.2-2** — A shot appears in exactly one of `cached_assets` or `render_queue`; a `render_strategy` of `cache_hit` implies membership in `cached_assets`, not `render_queue` (avoid unnecessary rendering — Principle 1).
- **INV-9.7.2-3** — Every `ShotId` in `validation_queue` and in `composition_plan.ordered_shots` must resolve to a member of `shots`.
- **INV-9.7.2-4** — `estimated_cost_usd` is computed before provider submission, enabling budget enforcement (Owner: 6.1.8 budget domain).
- **INV-9.7.2-5** — As a sealed artifact, no properties beyond the envelope and this body are permitted (`unevaluatedProperties: false`).

---

# Example

```json
{
  "artifact_id": "exec-plan-20260720-001",
  "artifact_type": "execution_plan",
  "schema_version": "2.0.0",
  "created_at": "2026-07-20T09:15:00Z",
  "content_hash": "sha256:6f1a...c92e",
  "build_id": "20260720-001",
  "pipeline_version": "2.0.0",
  "build_type": "final",
  "shots": [
    { "shot_id": "shot-001", "render_strategy": "cache_hit", "cache_key": "ck:9ab...1" },
    { "shot_id": "shot-002", "render_strategy": "render", "provider_profile": "gen4.5" }
  ],
  "cached_assets": [
    { "shot_id": "shot-001", "cache_key": "ck:9ab...1", "content_hash": "sha256:11a...ff" }
  ],
  "render_queue": [
    { "shot_id": "shot-002", "provider_profile": "gen4.5", "cache_key": "ck:7cd...2" }
  ],
  "validation_queue": ["shot-002"],
  "composition_plan": { "ordered_shots": ["shot-001", "shot-002"], "target_duration": 60 },
  "dependency_graph_ref": "sha256:a11...b22",
  "estimated_cost_usd": 18.5
}
```

---

# Acceptance Criteria

- A conforming plan declares all seven canonical members and composes `ArtifactEnvelope`.
- Cache hits and render-queue entries are mutually exclusive per shot.
- All queued and composed shot identifiers resolve to planned shots.
- Unknown top-level properties are rejected via `unevaluatedProperties: false`.

---

# 9.7.3 dependency-graph (`dependency-graph.schema.json`)

### The acyclic stage/shot dependency DAG (Owner: 6.1.3)

---

# Purpose

The Build Planner constructs a **Directed Acyclic Graph** over stages and shots (Story → Screenplay → Storyboard → Shots → Validation → Composition). Explicit dependencies enable fine-grained parallelism: independent nodes execute concurrently, and only invalidated nodes re-execute (Principles 5–6, *Fine-Grained Parallelism* and *Explicit Dependencies*). Circular dependencies are prohibited. This schema models the graph as typed `nodes` and directed `edges` with an asserted `acyclic` flag.

---

# Canonical Schema

```json
{
  "$schema": "https://json-schema.org/draft/2020-12/schema",
  "$id": "https://schemas.insynergy.co/cttp/v2.0/build/dependency-graph.schema.json",
  "title": "DependencyGraph",
  "description": "Acyclic stage/shot dependency graph. Owner: 6.1.3.",
  "type": "object",
  "additionalProperties": false,
  "required": ["schema_version", "build_id", "nodes", "edges", "acyclic"],
  "properties": {
    "schema_version": {
      "$ref": "https://schemas.insynergy.co/cttp/v2.0/common/defs.schema.json#/$defs/SchemaVersion"
    },
    "build_id": {
      "$ref": "https://schemas.insynergy.co/cttp/v2.0/common/defs.schema.json#/$defs/BuildId"
    },
    "nodes": {
      "type": "array",
      "minItems": 1,
      "items": { "$ref": "#/$defs/Node" }
    },
    "edges": {
      "type": "array",
      "description": "Directed dependency edges (from depends-on target).",
      "items": { "$ref": "#/$defs/Edge" }
    },
    "acyclic": {
      "const": true,
      "description": "Assertion that the graph contains no cycles. Circular dependencies are prohibited. Owner: 6.1.3."
    }
  },
  "$defs": {
    "Node": {
      "type": "object",
      "additionalProperties": false,
      "required": ["id", "kind"],
      "properties": {
        "id": {
          "type": "string",
          "description": "Unique node identifier within the graph."
        },
        "kind": {
          "type": "string",
          "description": "Stage or artifact class of the node.",
          "enum": [
            "story",
            "screenplay",
            "storyboard",
            "shot",
            "validation",
            "composition",
            "packaging"
          ]
        },
        "shot_id": {
          "$ref": "https://schemas.insynergy.co/cttp/v2.0/common/defs.schema.json#/$defs/ShotId",
          "description": "Present when kind = shot."
        }
      }
    },
    "Edge": {
      "type": "object",
      "additionalProperties": false,
      "required": ["from", "to"],
      "properties": {
        "from": {
          "type": "string",
          "description": "Dependent node id (executes after 'to')."
        },
        "to": {
          "type": "string",
          "description": "Dependency node id (must complete first)."
        }
      }
    }
  }
}
```

---

# Field Reference

| Field | Type | Required | Description |
| ----- | ---- | -------- | ----------- |
| `schema_version` | `SchemaVersion` | Yes | Schema version of the graph. |
| `build_id` | `BuildId` | Yes | Build the graph belongs to. |
| `nodes` | array of `Node` | Yes | Graph vertices (≥ 1). |
| `nodes[].id` | string | Yes | Unique vertex identifier. |
| `nodes[].kind` | enum | Yes | Stage/artifact class of the vertex. |
| `nodes[].shot_id` | `ShotId` | No | Shot reference when `kind = shot`. |
| `edges` | array of `Edge` | Yes | Directed dependency edges. |
| `edges[].from` / `.to` | string | Yes | Dependent and dependency node identifiers. |
| `acyclic` | `true` | Yes | Structural assertion of acyclicity. |

---

# Constraints & Invariants

- **INV-9.7.3-1** — `acyclic` is fixed `true`; a graph containing a cycle is invalid by contract (Owner: 6.1.3). The topological check is enforced by the planner; the flag records the guarantee.
- **INV-9.7.3-2** — Every `edges[].from` and `edges[].to` must reference a declared `nodes[].id`; dangling edges are prohibited (*Explicit Dependencies*, Principle 6).
- **INV-9.7.3-3** — `from` and `to` must differ; self-edges are prohibited.
- **INV-9.7.3-4** — Node identifiers are unique within the graph.
- **INV-9.7.3-5** — Independent (mutually unreachable) nodes may execute in parallel (*Fine-Grained Parallelism*, Principle 5).

---

# Example

```json
{
  "schema_version": "2.0.0",
  "build_id": "20260720-001",
  "nodes": [
    { "id": "n-story", "kind": "story" },
    { "id": "n-screenplay", "kind": "screenplay" },
    { "id": "n-storyboard", "kind": "storyboard" },
    { "id": "n-shot-a", "kind": "shot", "shot_id": "shot-001" },
    { "id": "n-shot-b", "kind": "shot", "shot_id": "shot-002" },
    { "id": "n-validation", "kind": "validation" },
    { "id": "n-composition", "kind": "composition" }
  ],
  "edges": [
    { "from": "n-screenplay", "to": "n-story" },
    { "from": "n-storyboard", "to": "n-screenplay" },
    { "from": "n-shot-a", "to": "n-storyboard" },
    { "from": "n-shot-b", "to": "n-storyboard" },
    { "from": "n-validation", "to": "n-shot-a" },
    { "from": "n-validation", "to": "n-shot-b" },
    { "from": "n-composition", "to": "n-validation" }
  ],
  "acyclic": true
}
```

---

# Acceptance Criteria

- A conforming graph declares at least one node and asserts `acyclic: true`.
- Every edge endpoint resolves to a declared node; no self-edges.
- Node kinds are drawn from the enumerated stage classes.
- Graphs containing cycles are rejected by the planner before the plan is sealed.

---

# 9.7.4 build-profile (`build-profile.schema.json`)

### Build profiles and execution modes (Owner: 6.1.7)

---

# Purpose

Section 6.1.7 defines standard **build profiles** (policy) and **execution modes** (intent), held orthogonal by ADR-622. A profile fixes rendering fidelity, validation strictness, cache usage, placeholders, retries, concurrency, and the target duration; a mode fixes what the run executes. This schema captures a named profile together with its resolved knobs and its selected execution mode.

---

# Canonical Schema

```json
{
  "$schema": "https://json-schema.org/draft/2020-12/schema",
  "$id": "https://schemas.insynergy.co/cttp/v2.0/build/build-profile.schema.json",
  "title": "BuildProfile",
  "description": "Build profile and execution mode. Owner: 6.1.7.",
  "type": "object",
  "additionalProperties": false,
  "required": ["schema_version", "profile", "build_type", "execution_mode", "settings"],
  "properties": {
    "schema_version": {
      "$ref": "https://schemas.insynergy.co/cttp/v2.0/common/defs.schema.json#/$defs/SchemaVersion"
    },
    "profile": {
      "type": "string",
      "description": "Standard build profile. Owner: 6.1.7.",
      "enum": [
        "development",
        "preview",
        "production",
        "benchmark",
        "recovery",
        "cost_optimized",
        "quality_max"
      ]
    },
    "build_type": {
      "$ref": "https://schemas.insynergy.co/cttp/v2.0/common/defs.schema.json#/$defs/BuildType"
    },
    "execution_mode": {
      "type": "string",
      "description": "Execution intent, orthogonal to profile (ADR-622). Owner: 6.1.7.",
      "enum": [
        "full",
        "incremental",
        "resume",
        "dry_run",
        "validate_only",
        "render_only",
        "compose_only"
      ]
    },
    "settings": {
      "type": "object",
      "additionalProperties": false,
      "required": ["rendering", "validation", "cache"],
      "properties": {
        "runway_profile": {
          "type": "string",
          "description": "Provider render profile (e.g. gen4.5, preview, draft)."
        },
        "rendering": {
          "type": "string",
          "enum": ["optional", "draft", "final", "premium", "missing_only"]
        },
        "render_ratio": {
          "$ref": "https://schemas.insynergy.co/cttp/v2.0/common/defs.schema.json#/$defs/Ratio",
          "description": "Fraction of shots rendered at fidelity vs placeholder."
        },
        "validation": {
          "type": "string",
          "enum": [
            "basic",
            "editorial",
            "strict",
            "strictest",
            "verify_existing"
          ]
        },
        "cache": {
          "type": "string",
          "enum": ["enabled", "aggressive", "maximum", "configurable"]
        },
        "placeholders": {
          "type": "string",
          "enum": ["enabled", "disabled", "preferred", "prohibited"]
        },
        "retries": {
          "type": "string",
          "enum": ["disabled", "enabled", "unlimited_until_budget"]
        },
        "concurrency": {
          "type": "string",
          "enum": ["low", "medium", "high"]
        },
        "target_duration": {
          "$ref": "https://schemas.insynergy.co/cttp/v2.0/common/defs.schema.json#/$defs/DurationSeconds",
          "description": "Target end-to-end build duration for the profile."
        }
      }
    }
  }
}
```

---

# Field Reference

| Field | Type | Required | Description |
| ----- | ---- | -------- | ----------- |
| `schema_version` | `SchemaVersion` | Yes | Schema version. |
| `profile` | enum | Yes | One of the seven standard profiles. |
| `build_type` | `BuildType` | Yes | Preview / final classification. |
| `execution_mode` | enum | Yes | Execution intent (orthogonal to profile). |
| `settings.runway_profile` | string | No | Provider render profile identifier. |
| `settings.rendering` | enum | Yes | Rendering fidelity policy. |
| `settings.render_ratio` | `Ratio` | No | Rendered-vs-placeholder fraction. |
| `settings.validation` | enum | Yes | Validation strictness. |
| `settings.cache` | enum | Yes | Cache-usage policy. |
| `settings.placeholders` | enum | No | Placeholder policy. |
| `settings.retries` | enum | No | Retry policy. |
| `settings.concurrency` | enum | No | Worker concurrency tier. |
| `settings.target_duration` | `DurationSeconds` | No | Target end-to-end duration. |

---

# Constraints & Invariants

- **INV-9.7.4-1** — `profile` and `execution_mode` are orthogonal; any valid profile may pair with any valid mode (ADR-622, Owner: 6.1.7).
- **INV-9.7.4-2** — The `production` and `quality_max` profiles set `placeholders` to `disabled`/`prohibited` and `validation` to `strict`/`strictest`; every Quality Gate is mandatory under these profiles (Owner: 6.1.7).
- **INV-9.7.4-3** — `recovery` implies `execution_mode = resume` and `rendering = missing_only`; no completed task is repeated (Principle 13, *Resume by Default*).
- **INV-9.7.4-4** — `render_ratio` is a ratio in [0,1] (delegated to `Ratio`); `cost_optimized` minimizes it, `quality_max` maximizes fidelity.
- **INV-9.7.4-5** — Enumerated values are drawn verbatim from the profile and execution-mode definitions of 6.1.7.

---

# Example

```json
{
  "schema_version": "2.0.0",
  "profile": "preview",
  "build_type": "preview",
  "execution_mode": "incremental",
  "settings": {
    "runway_profile": "preview",
    "rendering": "draft",
    "render_ratio": 0.4,
    "validation": "editorial",
    "cache": "aggressive",
    "placeholders": "enabled",
    "retries": "disabled",
    "concurrency": "medium",
    "target_duration": 1500
  }
}
```

---

# Acceptance Criteria

- A conforming profile names one of the seven standard profiles and one of the seven execution modes.
- Rendering, validation, and cache policies are always present.
- Production-class profiles disable placeholders and enforce strict validation.
- Unknown profiles, modes, or setting keys are rejected.

---

# 9.7.5 performance-config (`performance-config.schema.json`)

### The layered, runtime-immutable performance configuration snapshot (Owner: 6.1.8)

---

# Purpose

Section 6.1.8 externalizes all performance behavior into declarative configuration: "execution behavior belongs in configuration, not source code." Configuration is resolved through a fixed hierarchy (System Defaults → Environment Defaults → Build Profile → Execution Mode → Project Configuration → CLI Overrides → Environment Variables), validated before execution, and the **resolved** result is recorded per build for reproducibility (ADR-630). This schema is that resolved snapshot: the ten independent domains under a single `performance` root, versioned, and immutable at runtime. Unknown keys fail validation.

---

# Canonical Schema

```json
{
  "$schema": "https://json-schema.org/draft/2020-12/schema",
  "$id": "https://schemas.insynergy.co/cttp/v2.0/build/performance-config.schema.json",
  "title": "PerformanceConfig",
  "description": "Resolved, runtime-immutable performance configuration. Owner: 6.1.8.",
  "type": "object",
  "additionalProperties": false,
  "required": ["schema_version", "configuration", "performance"],
  "properties": {
    "schema_version": {
      "$ref": "https://schemas.insynergy.co/cttp/v2.0/common/defs.schema.json#/$defs/SchemaVersion"
    },
    "configuration": {
      "type": "object",
      "additionalProperties": false,
      "description": "Configuration versioning block. Owner: 6.1.8.",
      "required": ["profile_version", "updated_at"],
      "properties": {
        "profile_version": {
          "$ref": "https://schemas.insynergy.co/cttp/v2.0/common/defs.schema.json#/$defs/SchemaVersion"
        },
        "updated_at": {
          "$ref": "https://schemas.insynergy.co/cttp/v2.0/common/defs.schema.json#/$defs/Iso8601"
        },
        "environment": {
          "type": "string",
          "enum": ["local", "github_actions", "staging", "production"]
        }
      }
    },
    "performance": {
      "type": "object",
      "additionalProperties": false,
      "required": [
        "scheduler",
        "providers",
        "cache",
        "retry",
        "polling",
        "validation",
        "composition",
        "budget",
        "telemetry",
        "recovery"
      ],
      "properties": {
        "scheduler": {
          "type": "object",
          "additionalProperties": false,
          "properties": {
            "global_workers": { "type": "integer", "minimum": 1 },
            "planning_workers": { "type": "integer", "const": 1 },
            "render_workers": { "type": "integer", "minimum": 1 },
            "validation_workers": { "type": "integer", "minimum": 1 },
            "ffmpeg_workers": { "type": "integer", "minimum": 1 },
            "packaging_workers": { "type": "integer", "minimum": 1 }
          }
        },
        "providers": {
          "type": "object",
          "additionalProperties": {
            "type": "object",
            "additionalProperties": false,
            "required": ["enabled"],
            "properties": {
              "enabled": { "type": "boolean" },
              "profile": { "type": "string" },
              "max_parallel_jobs": { "type": "integer", "minimum": 1 },
              "polling_interval_seconds": {
                "$ref": "https://schemas.insynergy.co/cttp/v2.0/common/defs.schema.json#/$defs/DurationSeconds"
              },
              "timeout_minutes": { "type": "integer", "minimum": 1 },
              "retry_limit": { "type": "integer", "minimum": 0 }
            }
          }
        },
        "cache": {
          "type": "object",
          "additionalProperties": false,
          "properties": {
            "enabled": { "type": "boolean" },
            "local": { "$ref": "#/$defs/Toggle" },
            "shared": { "$ref": "#/$defs/Toggle" },
            "validation_cache": { "$ref": "#/$defs/Toggle" },
            "composition_cache": { "$ref": "#/$defs/Toggle" }
          }
        },
        "retry": {
          "type": "object",
          "additionalProperties": false,
          "properties": {
            "maximum_attempts": { "type": "integer", "minimum": 0 },
            "exponential_backoff": { "type": "boolean" },
            "multiplier": { "type": "number", "minimum": 1 },
            "maximum_delay_seconds": {
              "$ref": "https://schemas.insynergy.co/cttp/v2.0/common/defs.schema.json#/$defs/DurationSeconds"
            },
            "retryable_errors": {
              "type": "array",
              "items": {
                "type": "string",
                "enum": ["timeout", "rate_limit", "temporary_network"]
              }
            }
          }
        },
        "polling": {
          "type": "object",
          "additionalProperties": false,
          "properties": {
            "initial_seconds": { "type": "number", "minimum": 0 },
            "maximum_seconds": { "type": "number", "minimum": 0 },
            "multiplier": { "type": "number", "minimum": 1 },
            "jitter_ratio": {
              "$ref": "https://schemas.insynergy.co/cttp/v2.0/common/defs.schema.json#/$defs/Ratio"
            }
          }
        },
        "validation": {
          "type": "object",
          "additionalProperties": false,
          "properties": {
            "technical": { "$ref": "#/$defs/Toggle" },
            "cinematic": { "$ref": "#/$defs/Toggle" },
            "continuity": { "$ref": "#/$defs/Toggle" },
            "fail_fast": { "type": "boolean" }
          }
        },
        "composition": {
          "type": "object",
          "additionalProperties": false,
          "properties": {
            "ffmpeg": {
              "type": "object",
              "additionalProperties": false,
              "properties": {
                "hardware_acceleration": {
                  "type": "string",
                  "enum": ["auto", "enabled", "disabled"]
                },
                "parallel_jobs": { "type": "integer", "minimum": 1 },
                "temporary_directory": { "type": "string" },
                "preserve_intermediate_files": { "type": "boolean" }
              }
            }
          }
        },
        "budget": {
          "type": "object",
          "additionalProperties": false,
          "properties": {
            "preview": {
              "type": "object",
              "additionalProperties": false,
              "properties": { "maximum_usd": { "type": "number", "minimum": 0 } }
            },
            "production": {
              "type": "object",
              "additionalProperties": false,
              "properties": { "maximum_usd": { "type": "number", "minimum": 0 } }
            },
            "stop_on_budget_exceeded": { "type": "boolean" },
            "estimate_before_submission": { "type": "boolean" }
          }
        },
        "telemetry": {
          "type": "object",
          "additionalProperties": false,
          "properties": {
            "metrics": { "$ref": "#/$defs/Toggle" },
            "tracing": { "$ref": "#/$defs/Toggle" },
            "structured_logs": { "$ref": "#/$defs/Toggle" },
            "performance_reports": { "$ref": "#/$defs/Toggle" }
          }
        },
        "recovery": {
          "type": "object",
          "additionalProperties": false,
          "properties": {
            "checkpoint_interval": {
              "type": "string",
              "enum": ["every_stage", "every_task"]
            },
            "automatic_resume": { "type": "boolean" },
            "verify_assets_before_resume": { "type": "boolean" }
          }
        }
      }
    }
  },
  "$defs": {
    "Toggle": {
      "type": "object",
      "additionalProperties": false,
      "required": ["enabled"],
      "properties": { "enabled": { "type": "boolean" } }
    }
  }
}
```

---

# Field Reference

| Field | Type | Required | Description |
| ----- | ---- | -------- | ----------- |
| `schema_version` | `SchemaVersion` | Yes | Schema version of the snapshot. |
| `configuration.profile_version` | `SchemaVersion` | Yes | Version of the resolved profile. |
| `configuration.updated_at` | `Iso8601` | Yes | Resolution timestamp. |
| `configuration.environment` | enum | No | Target environment. |
| `performance.scheduler` | object | Yes | Worker allocation; planning stays sequential. |
| `performance.providers` | map | Yes | Per-provider concurrency and limits. |
| `performance.cache` | object | Yes | Independently toggled cache layers. |
| `performance.retry` | object | Yes | Retry policy; validation is never auto-retried. |
| `performance.polling` | object | Yes | Adaptive provider polling. |
| `performance.validation` | object | Yes | Validation domains and `fail_fast`. |
| `performance.composition` | object | Yes | FFmpeg execution parameters. |
| `performance.budget` | object | Yes | Cost ceilings and enforcement. |
| `performance.telemetry` | object | Yes | Telemetry toggles (mandatory in production). |
| `performance.recovery` | object | Yes | Checkpoint and resume behavior. |

---

# Constraints & Invariants

- **INV-9.7.5-1** — Unknown keys fail validation everywhere (`additionalProperties: false` on each domain); configuration is validated before execution (Owner: 6.1.8).
- **INV-9.7.5-2** — `scheduler.planning_workers` is fixed to `1`; planning remains sequential (Owner: 6.1.8).
- **INV-9.7.5-3** — The snapshot is the *resolved* configuration recorded per build and is immutable at runtime (ADR-630, *Performance Configuration is Declarative*).
- **INV-9.7.5-4** — `budget.estimate_before_submission` and `budget.stop_on_budget_exceeded` govern pre-submission enforcement; expensive work is deferred until approval (Principle 12, *Human Approval Before High-Cost Work*).
- **INV-9.7.5-5** — Telemetry domains may not be disabled in production; validated by the configuration validator against `configuration.environment`.

---

# Example

```json
{
  "schema_version": "2.0.0",
  "configuration": {
    "profile_version": "2.0.0",
    "updated_at": "2026-07-20T09:00:00Z",
    "environment": "github_actions"
  },
  "performance": {
    "scheduler": {
      "global_workers": 12,
      "planning_workers": 1,
      "render_workers": 4,
      "validation_workers": 4,
      "ffmpeg_workers": 2,
      "packaging_workers": 1
    },
    "providers": {
      "runway": {
        "enabled": true,
        "profile": "gen4.5",
        "max_parallel_jobs": 4,
        "polling_interval_seconds": 15,
        "timeout_minutes": 45,
        "retry_limit": 3
      },
      "veo": { "enabled": false }
    },
    "cache": {
      "enabled": true,
      "local": { "enabled": true },
      "shared": { "enabled": false },
      "validation_cache": { "enabled": true },
      "composition_cache": { "enabled": true }
    },
    "retry": {
      "maximum_attempts": 3,
      "exponential_backoff": true,
      "multiplier": 2,
      "maximum_delay_seconds": 300,
      "retryable_errors": ["timeout", "rate_limit", "temporary_network"]
    },
    "polling": { "initial_seconds": 10, "maximum_seconds": 60, "multiplier": 1.5, "jitter_ratio": 0.15 },
    "validation": {
      "technical": { "enabled": true },
      "cinematic": { "enabled": true },
      "continuity": { "enabled": true },
      "fail_fast": true
    },
    "composition": {
      "ffmpeg": {
        "hardware_acceleration": "auto",
        "parallel_jobs": 2,
        "temporary_directory": "temp/",
        "preserve_intermediate_files": false
      }
    },
    "budget": {
      "preview": { "maximum_usd": 20 },
      "production": { "maximum_usd": 60 },
      "stop_on_budget_exceeded": true,
      "estimate_before_submission": true
    },
    "telemetry": {
      "metrics": { "enabled": true },
      "tracing": { "enabled": true },
      "structured_logs": { "enabled": true },
      "performance_reports": { "enabled": true }
    },
    "recovery": {
      "checkpoint_interval": "every_stage",
      "automatic_resume": true,
      "verify_assets_before_resume": true
    }
  }
}
```

---

# Acceptance Criteria

- A conforming snapshot declares all ten performance domains plus the versioning block.
- `planning_workers` equals 1 and all worker counts are positive integers.
- Retryable errors are drawn from the enumerated set; validation is not among them.
- Any unknown key at any level is rejected.

---

# 9.7.6 operational-state (`operational-state.schema.json`)

### The lifecycle-state record of a build artifact (Owner: 6.1.11)

---

# Purpose

Section 6.1.11 mandates that every operational entity exist in exactly one explicit state at any moment, that transitions be monotonic (forward-only), and that every transition be recorded — implicit state is prohibited. This schema records the canonical lifecycle state of a build **artifact** together with its append-only transition log. The artifact lifecycle states are drawn verbatim from the canonical cache-object lifecycle: `CREATED → VALIDATED → APPROVED → REFERENCED → ARCHIVED → EXPIRED → DELETED`. Only forward transitions are allowed.

---

# Canonical Schema

```json
{
  "$schema": "https://json-schema.org/draft/2020-12/schema",
  "$id": "https://schemas.insynergy.co/cttp/v2.0/build/operational-state.schema.json",
  "title": "OperationalState",
  "description": "Lifecycle-state record of a build artifact. Owner: 6.1.11.",
  "type": "object",
  "additionalProperties": false,
  "required": ["schema_version", "artifact_ref", "state", "transitions_logged", "transitions"],
  "properties": {
    "schema_version": {
      "$ref": "https://schemas.insynergy.co/cttp/v2.0/common/defs.schema.json#/$defs/SchemaVersion"
    },
    "artifact_ref": {
      "$ref": "https://schemas.insynergy.co/cttp/v2.0/common/defs.schema.json#/$defs/ContentHash",
      "description": "Content-addressed reference to the governed artifact."
    },
    "build_id": {
      "$ref": "https://schemas.insynergy.co/cttp/v2.0/common/defs.schema.json#/$defs/BuildId"
    },
    "state": {
      "$ref": "#/$defs/LifecycleState",
      "description": "Current canonical lifecycle state. Owner: 6.1.11."
    },
    "owner": {
      "type": "string",
      "description": "Exclusive owner of transitions for this artifact class.",
      "enum": ["Build Orchestrator", "Retention Manager", "Cleanup Manager", "Asset Manager"]
    },
    "transitions_logged": {
      "const": true,
      "description": "Assertion that every transition is recorded. No transition exists only in memory. Owner: 6.1.11."
    },
    "transitions": {
      "type": "array",
      "description": "Append-only audit trail of state transitions.",
      "items": {
        "type": "object",
        "additionalProperties": false,
        "required": ["previous_state", "new_state", "timestamp"],
        "properties": {
          "previous_state": { "$ref": "#/$defs/LifecycleState" },
          "new_state": { "$ref": "#/$defs/LifecycleState" },
          "timestamp": {
            "$ref": "https://schemas.insynergy.co/cttp/v2.0/common/defs.schema.json#/$defs/Iso8601"
          },
          "approval_ref": {
            "$ref": "https://schemas.insynergy.co/cttp/v2.0/common/defs.schema.json#/$defs/ApprovalRef",
            "description": "Present when the transition required human approval."
          }
        }
      }
    }
  },
  "$defs": {
    "LifecycleState": {
      "type": "string",
      "description": "Canonical artifact lifecycle states, verbatim. Owner: 6.1.11.",
      "enum": [
        "CREATED",
        "VALIDATED",
        "APPROVED",
        "REFERENCED",
        "ARCHIVED",
        "EXPIRED",
        "DELETED"
      ]
    }
  }
}
```

---

# Field Reference

| Field | Type | Required | Description |
| ----- | ---- | -------- | ----------- |
| `schema_version` | `SchemaVersion` | Yes | Schema version. |
| `artifact_ref` | `ContentHash` | Yes | Content-addressed reference to the artifact. |
| `build_id` | `BuildId` | No | Owning build. |
| `state` | `LifecycleState` | Yes | Current canonical state. |
| `owner` | enum | No | Exclusive transition owner. |
| `transitions_logged` | `true` | Yes | Assertion that transitions are recorded. |
